# Integrations

<a id="bolt-execution-log"></a>
## Bolt Logs

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/bolt-execution-log_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to navigate to the Bolt Logs
- How to use the Bolt Logs

### Purpose

The Bolt Logs keeps a record of all Bolts executed within your tenancy. These are advanced integration and automation tools.

This page is primarily used by our integrations team for troubleshooting purposes.

If you wish to set up a Bolt, please get in contact with our integration team by contacting us through the [Support desk](https://support.cartoncloud.com/servicedesk/customer/portal/2).

### How to navigate to the Bolt Logs

- Select More > Bolt Logs.

### How to use the Bolt Logs

You can use the filters at the top of the page to find the bolt you are wishing to investigate. You can then click **view** against the relevant bolt and time stamp to see more information relating to the bolt execution.

![bolt-execution-log-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bolt-execution-log-0.png?width=670&height=303&name=bolt-execution-log-0.png)

![bolt-execution-log-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bolt-execution-log-1.png?width=670&height=236&name=bolt-execution-log-1.png)

<a id="cartoncloud-link"></a>
## CartonCloud Link

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/cartoncloud-link_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Example use cases
- The benefits of CartonCloud Link
- How to get CartonCloud link set up

### Purpose

CartonCloud Link provides the ability to send data from one CartonCloud account to another.

By creating a link between two separate CartonCloud accounts data can be passed in both directions as required, sending information such as consignments, PODs, orders, status updates and more.
 ![cartoncloud-link-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/cartoncloud-link-0.png?width=670&height=335&name=cartoncloud-link-0.png)

### Example Use Case

**Example Use Case #1**

*“Blue Warehouse” and “Green Transport” both use CartonCloud. Blue Warehouse also uses Green Transport for deliveries to some areas.*

*After setting up CartonCloud Link, Blue Warehouse can now automatically send consignments across to Green Transport’s CartonCloud account from their warehouse sales orders.*

*Once Green Transport delivers these consignments, the POD is automatically attached to Blue Warehouse’s consignment records. The delivery status is updated automatically and the consignment is now ready for invoicing.*

**Example Use Case #2**

*“Red Transport” and “Green Transport” both use CartonCloud. Red Transport also uses Green Transport as an onforwarder for deliveries to some areas.*

*After setting up CartonCloud Link, Red Transport can now automatically send consignments across to Green Transport’s CartonCloud account by allocating their own Consignments to a delivery run named “Green Transport”.*

*Once Green Transport delivers these consignments, the POD is automatically attached to Red Transport’s consignment records. The delivery status is updated automatically and the consignment is now ready for invoicing.*

CartonCloud Link is configurable based on your requirements. During the setup process, our support team will ask what CartonCloud client you would like to send data to or receive jobs from.

Whether you want to send a consignment or warehouse order, we've made it easy with this feature. Once linked all you have to do is select the receiver account in your workflow and CartonCloud will take care of the rest.

### The benefits of CartonCloud Link

- Reduce data entry to remove the opportunity for errors
- Reduce wasted staff hours manually entering work that once automated could be completed in seconds
- Simplify invoicing by always having a POD on hand
- Automated status updates in real-time ensuring nothing gets missed
- Better service and visibility for your customers!

Check out our [automation report](https://help.cartoncloud.com/kb2/web-app-page-specific-support/administrator-pages/reports/automation-report) to help you reduce manual data entry within CartonCloud.

**The network effect**

Having your wider network utilising CartonCloud with integrations between each other is a huge advantage for your operation. Gone are the days of picking up the phone to check on where deliveries are up to, waiting for paper proof of deliveries to be returned and manually processing them come invoicing time.

Make your life easier and streamline your workflow across your wider network through CartonCloud Link.

If you have companies in your network who are not using CartonCloud, let us know who they are and you can earn a finders fee! Submit their details [here.](https://www.cartoncloud.com/refer-earn)

### How to get a CartonCloud Link set up

If this is something that you think might benefit your operation please contact our

integrations team.

---

<a id="custom-buttons"></a>
## Custom Buttons

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/custom-buttons_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How it works
- Example 1 - refresh information in CartonCloud from an external system
- Example 2 - send a custom notification (via email or SMS)
- Example 3 - print a file within CartonCloud
- Example 4 - send data to a 3rd party API
- How to get a custom button

### Purpose

Custom Buttons allow you to trigger various custom actions and workflows with the click of a button.

### How it works

These buttons can be added to the screens on Sale Orders, Purchase Orders, Consignments or Run Sheets. The button colour, text and icon can all be customised. The buttons appear along the top button bar, for example, here’s a button to send an SMS from within the Sale Order page:

![custom-buttons-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-buttons-0.png?width=493&height=212&name=custom-buttons-0.png)

A few examples of how these may be used are outlined below:

### Example 1 - Refresh information in CartonCloud from an external system

Where an order has been imported via integration with another software application, such as Shopify, a Custom Button can be added to re-sync the order with the external system to allow for a quick and easy way to bring in refreshed data. This can be particularly useful if there are any cancellations or changes to the original order to avoid manual communications, data entry and any potential errors occurring.

![custom-buttons-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-buttons-1.png?width=300&height=66&name=custom-buttons-1.png)

### Example 2 - Send a custom notification (via email or SMS)

A Custom Button can be added to send a customised notification, via email or SMS, to allow you to provide better updates, visibility and service to your Customers.

![custom-buttons-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-buttons-2.png?width=300&height=57&name=custom-buttons-2.png)

### Example 3 - Print a file within CartonCloud

A Custom Button can be added that can print (via [CartonCloud Connect](https://help.cartoncloud.com/kb2/technical-information/printing-from-cartoncloud-printer-setup)) the associated Customer Invoice from a Sale Order or Consignment, removing the need to navigate to a separate place to complete this activity.

![custom-buttons-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-buttons-3.png?width=300&height=59&name=custom-buttons-3.png)

### Example 4 - Send data to a 3rd party API

If you have a workflow which requires information from CartonCloud to be sent to a third-party API, such as sending a booking to another carrier’s system for a particular order, this can also be triggered by a Custom Button to allow users control over when this action occurs whilst removing any data entry or errors.

![custom-buttons-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-buttons-4.png?width=300&height=60&name=custom-buttons-4.png)

### How to get a Custom Button

There are many other examples of how these Custom Buttons may be able to be integrated into your CartonCloud account. To discuss adding a Custom Button and applicable pricing, or other custom-workflow options, for your CartonCloud account, please get in touch with our integrations team via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport)

Please note that these Custom Buttons can also be added to most existing triggers in CartonCloud (Bolts), and all of the above functionality is also available based on pre-defined events within CartonCloud without the need for a Custom Button.

---

<a id="exporting-orders-from-xero"></a>
## Exporting Orders from Xero

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/exporting-orders-from-xero_

You can export orders from Xero which can be imported into CartonCloud as either Consignments or Sale Orders.

To do so, simply navigate to your orders, search for the orders you wish to export, click "search", then click Export.

The resulting CSV file can be imported into CartonCloud through a Parser. If you need a Parser setup for Xero, please contact us

![exporting-orders-from-xero-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-orders-from-xero-0.png?width=670&height=227&name=exporting-orders-from-xero-0.png)

<a id="how-to-print-shipping-labels-from-within-cartoncloud"></a>
## How to print shipping labels from within CartonCloud

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-print-shipping-labels-from-within-cartoncloud_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Solution 1 - custom button (printing from within CartonCloud)
- Solution 2 - print on status change (printing from within CartonCloud)
- Solution 3 - scan label barcode (printing from the shipping aggregator platform)

### Purpose

To print shipping aggregator labels (such as [Shippit](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Shippit+Integration) & [Starshipit](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Starshipit+Integration)) from within CartonCloud or the shipping aggregators platform.

**Process flow for printing shipping aggregator labels from within CartonCloud:**

![how-to-print-shipping-labels-from-within-cartoncloud-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-print-shipping-labels-from-within-cartoncloud-0.png?width=670&height=335&name=how-to-print-shipping-labels-from-within-cartoncloud-0.png)

Please note that for the below workflows to work an existing integration with a shipping aggregator platform such as [Shippit](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Shippit+Integration)or [Starshipit](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Starshipit+Integration) must exist. If you have an account with either of these platforms and are not yet integrated, please reach out to our integrations team via  [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport)

### Solution 1 - Custom Button (printing from within CartonCloud)

A [Custom Button](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/GwS-I) allows you to trigger various custom actions and workflows with the click of a button. In this case, the Custom Button would be configured to print the courier label when clicked in CartonCloud. This is useful if you do not want automatic printing, but do not wish to continually change between platforms.

**Requirement:**You will need to add a [Custom Button](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/custom-buttons) to your CartonCloud account. To do so, please reach out to our integrations team via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport)

### Solution 2 - Print on status change (printing from within CartonCloud)

By using an order status update as the trigger, such as when a Sale Order is marked as 'Packed' or 'Dispatched', the system will then automatically pull label data from the shipping aggregator and send it to your printer.

**Requirement:**You will need to add a printing integration to your CartonCloud account. To do so, please reach out to our integrations team via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) .

### Solution 3 - Scan Label Barcode (printing from the shipping aggregator platform)

From within the shipping aggregators platform, you can scan the CartonCloud label barcode and print the shipping label.

The Sale Order PDF template uses the Sale Order reference in the barcode. If you have adjusted this barcode please download and edit the Sale Order PDF template (see  [Document Templates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/document-templates) article) and update the barcode to the Sale Order reference.

To print by scanning the CartonCloud label barcode:

- Using the quick print function in Starshippit or the printmode search function in Shippit (depending on what shipping aggregator platform you are using) scan the CartonCloud label into the applicable feature to trigger the printing process.

**Requirement**: WMS only account, be using a barcode scanner and utilising the Sale Order PDF template (with the Sale Order reference in the barcode).

---

<a id="how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp"></a>
## How to Split Multi-Page PDF and Upload via FTP

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to steps

### Purpose

This guide is to be used if you've found that large, multi-page PDFs have been loaded into CartonCloud as Invoices / PODs. If this has happened, and you're unable to re-scan the pages, then you'll need to download, split, and then re-upload the individual pages into CartonCloud so they can be processed individually.

Normally you'll realise this issue has arisen because you'll have many Consignments which are missing Scanned Invoices, and one Consignment with a huge file attached to it.

### How to steps

Firstly, download the large PDF file from CartonCloud to your computer - you can do this by downloading the Consignment Customer Invoice from the Consignment that has the large file linked.

You'll need to first download and install two applications to do this, both are free, open-source applications:

1. PDFSAM Basic - for splitting the PDF into multiple files
2. FileZilla Client - for uploading to the CartonCloud FTP Server

**Step 1: Split the Multi-Page PDF into individual files:**

![how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-0.png?width=670&height=172&name=how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-0.png)

- Once you have finished downloading the file, "Delete" the file from the server because we no longer want this large file in the system.
- Next, use PDFSAM to split the PDF into multiple files. You can download PDFSAM from here: http://www.pdfsam.org/downloads/ - it's free.
- Select Split

![how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-1.png?width=670&height=172&name=how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-1.png)

- Select the large file you want to split, make sure it's splitting every page, choose an output location (make sure this folder is empty!!) and then click run.

![how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-2.png?width=670&height=243&name=how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-2.png)

- You can then click Open to take you to the directory where the files extracted:

![how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-3.png?width=670&height=160&name=how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-3.png)

- Here you'll have all the files individually split up:

![how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-4.png?width=427&height=457&name=how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-4.png)

**Step 2. Upload the files to the CartonCloud FTP Server**

- Open FileZilla and connect to the CartonCloud FTP Server. If you don't know your FTP login details, please contact us.
- On the left find the files you want to transfer to the server, highlight them all, and drag them into the correct folder within the server:

![how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-5.png?width=670&height=367&name=how-to-split-multi-page-pdf-and-upload-via-ftp-5.png)

- The files will then be picked up and processed within the next few minutes.

---

<a id="parsing-log"></a>
## Import Log

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/parsing-log_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Viewing the Import Log
- Understanding and interpreting the Import Log
  - Error code status mapping
- Filtering the Import Log
- Reprocess emails
- Downloading attachments

### Purpose

The Import Log provides a history of all orders coming into CartonCloud via a parser or the API. The Import Log can be utilised to diagnose issues with the import of the order or to verify what orders have been imported.

### Viewing the Import Log

- The Import Log can be accessed by selecting More in the main menu, then Import Log in the drop-down.
- From there, you can see all orders that have been received by parser or the API up to 30 days ago.

### Understanding and interpreting the Import Log

From the Import Log you can see if an order was successful, successful with warnings, successful with errors or failed. You are then provided detail relating to what the warnings, errors or failure were due to.

- Success (green tick): the order has been successfully processed with no issues
- Success with warnings (green tick with yellow warning symbol): the order has been successfully imported, however, with minor issues such as an incorrect product code or insufficient stock.
- Success with errors (green tick with red error symbol): the order has been successfully imported, however, with more serious issues, such as an invalid quantity or invalid warehouse location.
- Failure (red cross): the order has failed and not been imported. There are major issues preventing the order from being successfully imported.

![parsing-log-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/parsing-log-0.png?width=670&height=110&name=parsing-log-0.png)

The error code status mappings will help you understand what type of error will warrant a warning or error message upon import.

#### Error code status mapping

**Sale Order**

| **Error** | **Status (Success with warning or error)** |
| --- | --- |
| Remove lines with blank product codes | Warning |
| Remove lines with not enough stock | Warning |
| Remove lines with zero quantity | Warning |
| Remove lines with failed conversions | Warning |
| Remove lines with invalid conversions | Warning |
| Unit of measure adjusted to default UOM | Warning |
| Remove lines with invalid UOM | Warning |
| Line item has expired | Warning |
| Before expiry threshold | Warning |
| After expiry threshold | Warning |
| Not enough stock use available stock | Warning |
| MLOR per address expiry multiple address for address code found | Error |
| MLOR address not found | Error |
| MLOR expiry threshold | Error |
| Unable to parse | Error |
| Multiple products found for line item | Error |
| Missing product code reject | Error |
| Not enough stock reject | Error |
| Invalid quantity (non-positive number) | Error |
| UOM conversion failed reject | Error |
| UOM invalid reject | Error |

**Purchase Order**

| **Error** | **Status (Success with warning or error)** |
| --- | --- |
| Product code available (item removed) | Warning |
| Product code available (reject order) | Error |
| Product expiry invalid | Error |
| Product quantity invalid | Error |
| PUOM unit invalid (item removed) | Warning |
| PUOM unit invalid (reject order) | Error |
| PUOM unit invalid (substitute with default UOM) | Warning |
| Warehouse location invalid | Error |
| Warehouse location cannot handle product type | Error |
| Custom field invalid type | Error |
| Custom field non unique | Error |

### Filtering the Import Log

The Import Log can be filtered by Source, Recipient, Message, Status and the time it was logged at. These filter options make it easier to find the import you are looking for.

![parsing-log-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/parsing-log-1.png?width=670&height=114&name=parsing-log-1.png)

### Reprocess Emails

If you have a particular parser import which was unsuccessful for some reason (email address not setup, parser not configured etc), then you can reprocess an email directly from within the Email Parsing Log by simply clicking the "Reprocess" button:

![parsing-log-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/parsing-log-2.png?width=582&height=153&name=parsing-log-2.png)

This will re-process the job, and provide you with the result once completed.

### Downloading Attachments

You can download the attachments from the email by clicking the "Download Attachments" button.
This will download a zip file that contains all of the attachments that were within the original email.

---

<a id="pdf-to-purchase-order-integration"></a>
## PDF to Purchase Order Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/pdf-to-purchase-order-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How it works
- Benefits
- Requirements
- How to get set up
- Once you are set up
- Pricing

### Purpose

The PDF to Purchase Order integration is a PDF reader that generates a Purchase Order in CartonCloud via email or upload of a true PDF. The integration removes the requirement to send a CSV or text file via Parser or manually create an order in CartonCloud.

### How it works

- The customer emails the PDF to the designated email address.
- The Purchase Order is created in CartonCloud using the information on the PDF document.

### Benefits

- Increase data accuracy
- Reduce manual admin time
- Eliminates the need for csv or text files to use a Purchase Order parser.
- Can map Custom Fields at the order and product level

### Requirements

- The PDF must be a true PDF. A true PDF is created via a system rather than being scanned manually.
- Product Code, item quantity and any other relevant information (that will be used to create the order) need to be in their own column (or at least in a consistent format).

### How to get set up

- Create an API Client - (see instructions here on how to create an API Client). Ensure you associate the Customers that will be using the integration to the API Client you create.
- Use CartonCloud Help to lodge a case with the team and request a PDF to Purchase Order Parser to be created for the relevant Customers and an example of the PDF you would like to be sent in.

### Once you are set up with the integration

- The email from address will need to be approved. To be approved you will need to send an email with the PDF to the provided to address.
- Once the from address is approved, you will now be able to use that address (and any other email addresses that have been approved) to send the Purchase Order Order PDF from.

### Pricing

$5 ex GST per week, billed annually in advance + 30c per invoice parsed in (price is per invoice format, per customer)

---

<a id="pdf-to-sale-order-integration"></a>
## PDF to Sale Order Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/pdf-to-sale-order-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How it works
- Benefits
- Requirements
- How to get set up
- Once you are set up
- Pricing

### Purpose

The PDF to Sale Order integration is a PDF reader that generates a Sale Order in CartonCloud via email or upload of a true PDF. The integration removes the requirement to send a CSV or text file via Parser or manually create an order in CartonCloud. In addition, the PDF is automatically assigned to the Sale Order it has created.

### How it works

- The customer emails the PDF to the designated email address.
- The Sale Order is created in CartonCloud using the information on the PDF document.
- The PDF document is attached to the Sale Order in CartonCloud.

### Benefits

- Increase data accuracy
- Reduce manual admin time
- Eliminates the need for csv or text files to use a Sale Order parser.
- Removes the need to manually assign the Sale Order document to the Sale Order
- Completes two steps in one (creation and upload of Sale Order)

### Requirements

- The PDF must be a true PDF. A true PDF is created via a system rather than being scanned manually.
- Product Code, item quantity and any other relevant information (that will be used to create the order) need to be in their own column (or at least in a consistent format).

### How to get set up

- Create an API Client - (see instructions here on how to create an API Client). Ensure you associate the Customers that will be using the integration to the API Client you create.
- Lodge a case with our support team and request a PDF to Sale Order Parser to be created for the relevant Customers and an example of the PDF you would like to be sent in.

### Once you are set

- The email from address will need to be approved. To be approved you will need to send an email with the PDF to the provided to address.
- Once the from address is approved, you will now be able to use that address (and any other email addresses that have been approved) to send the Sale Order PDF from.

### Pricing

$5 ex GST per week, billed annually in advance + 30c per invoice parsed in (price is per invoice format, per customer)

---

<a id="scanning-to-cartoncloud-ftp-server"></a>
## Scanning to CartonCloud FTP Server

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/scanning-to-cartoncloud-ftp-server_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Creating a new FTP login
- Predefined subdirectories
- Configuring your printer

### Purpose

To scan into the CartonCloud FTP Server, the normal setup is to configure your Multi-Function printer to scan documents straight into CartonClouds FTP Server.

Note, if you would like to send the files to a Parser and have it process them please reach out to our Integrations team via

CartonCloud Help

### Creating a new FTP login

Firstly, head to the

FTP Users

page by typing "FTP Users" in the search for anything box.

Next, click

Add FTP User.

Create a Username, Password and select where you want to upload to within the Subdirectory. (you can leave this blank if you want to login to the directory root). See below for using predefined subdirectories.

![scanning-to-cartoncloud-ftp-server-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/scanning-to-cartoncloud-ftp-server-2.png?width=670&height=243&name=scanning-to-cartoncloud-ftp-server-2.png)

Select **Save** once completed.

### Predefined Subdirectories

There are predefined subdirectories within the FTP root directory which handle uploaded files in certain ways. Also, other folders can be configured for specific processing (ie: importing into [Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parsers)) by CartonCloud staff. For example, if you are scanning in POD's, then using the pods subdirectory ensures the files uploaded follow that behaviour and load into CartonCloud as POD files.

| **Subdirectory** | **Function** |
| --- | --- |
| invoices | Files uploaded will be processed as "Consignment Customer Invoices" with "invoice" type.   Invoices can be used for signature overlay when providing PODs back to your client. For more information on this, see: [Superimposed Proof Of Delivery](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Superimposed+Proof+Of+Delivery) |
| pods | Files uploaded will be processed as "Consignment Customer Invoices" with "proof of delivery" type.      Additional logic:   When a "proof of delivery" type Consignment Customer Invoice is attached to a Consignment, it will automatically mark the Consignment Delivered (if not already), and clear the "Awaiting Paper POD" status (if set).      For files received as POD's - they work off the QR code that can be enabled on the Consignment POD output. CartonCloud uses this to find the matching Consignment and then mark it as delivered automatically when attaching. The QR code is the consignment barcode i.e the one with the Customer Code prefix and then the Consignment ID. e.g. TEST000000000123445      Proof Of Delivery uploads will also be used as the first page(s) when the POD is downloaded from CartonCloud. |

### Configuring your Printer

This step varies depending on your printer, however, the normal process is to:

1. Login to your printer through its inbuilt web-server
2. Configure an FTP / Network folder to upload to
3. Load in the credentials you provided above. (Note that CartonCloud's FTP Server is ftp.cartoncloud.com)

This can be done through the Printer Settings, webserver or printer control panel. Generally if you Google Search "Configure scan to FTP *Insert name here*" and then include your printer or scanner name, this will provide instructions for configuring your scanner or printer. It's generally different for every device but follows a similar flow as described above.

**Common FTP Configuration will require:**

username: (this is the CartonCloud username created in the FTP Users page)

password: (created for the FTP user)

Port: 21

Directory: /  (it is not necessary to create a subdirectory)

After configuring, test the process by scanning a test file to the FTP server. It should show in CartonCloud under the [Consignment Customer Invoices / Scanned Proof Of Delivery](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/createpage.action?spaceKey=KB2&title=Consignment+Customer+Invoices+%2F+Scanned+Proof+Of+Delivery&linkCreation=true&fromPageId=532546057) - give it a few minutes as they can take a little while to appear sometimes. On that page, there is also the ability to add an invoice file manually too.

**Determining your printers IP address**

If you don't know the IP Address of your printer, an easy way to work this out is using the "Advanced IP Scanner" utility, run the program and if successful you will see your printers name and its IP address:

Windows: [ipscan25.exe](https://help.cartoncloud.com/download/attachments/532546057/ipscan25.exe?version=1&modificationDate=1578893034822&api=v2)

Or try options from here if that doesn't work: [https://www.google.co.nz/search?q=find+my+printer+ip+address&oq=find+my+printer+ip+addres&aqs=chrome.0.0j69i57j0l4.5326j0j7&sourceid=chrome&ie=UTF-8](https://www.google.co.nz/search?q=find+my+printer+ip+address&oq=find+my+printer+ip+addres&aqs=chrome.0.0j69i57j0l4.5326j0j7&sourceid=chrome&ie=UTF-8)

---

<a id="webhooks"></a>
## Webhooks

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/webhooks_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Standard Webhooks
  - Standard Webhook Payloads
  - Standard Authentication
  - Standard Webhook Triggers
  - Standard Webhook Requirements
  - How to get set up for standard webhooks
- Custom Webhooks

### Purpose

Webhooks are available for most entity changes, and can be configured based on conditions (ie: specific customer, specific status etc.). The standard payload, triggers and authentication are provided free of charge. However, if you require any customisation then this is at an additional cost and it the Integration team will be required to analyse the requirements and quote for the scope of work.

### Standard Webhooks

The standard payload, triggers and authentication are provided free of charge.

#### **Standard Webhook Payloads**

Below is detailed information regarding the standard webhook payloads for each entity, which are available at no extra cost. Additionally, we offer custom payloads, which are subject to additional charges see Custom Webhooks for more information.

- Sale Orders
- Purchase Orders
- Consignments

#### **Standard Authentication**

For standard authentication, an API-Key header parameter can be utilised. Should there be a need for an oAuth expiry bearer token, this option is available for a fee.

#### **Standard Webhook Triggers**

The standard webhooks triggers are listed below. These triggers are provided complimentary. Custom triggers or conditions, such as triggering only on certain statuses, will however incur charges see Custom Webhooks for more information.

- Order creation
- Order status change.

#### **Standard Webhook Requirements**

Requirements for the standard webhooks are as follows

- URL endpoints
- API-Key (if required)

#### **How to get set up for standard Webhooks**

Please reach out to the Integration team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport)with the standard webhooks you would like set up.

Our team is committed to setting up standard webhooks within 5 business days.

### Custom Webhooks

Custom Webhooks can be set up with custom payload and trigger conditions.

Please reach out to the Integration team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport)with your requirements.

For custom webhooks, the timeline extends to 15 days following the approval of the quote.

Custom payloads or triggers will necessitate a comprehensive analysis and scoping to fully understand your needs. This would include documentation of the proposed workflow and message structure.

---

# Integrations > Accounting Integrations

<a id="accounting-software-integrations-accounting-connectors"></a>
## Accounting Software Integrations (Accounting Connectors)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/accounting-software-integrations-accounting-connectors_

### Table of Contents

- What is an accounting connector
- How to set up an Accounting Connector
- How to configure the Accounting connector settings
- Multiple Accounting Connectors

### What is an accounting connector

CartonCloud can integrate with accounting software applications (in CartonCloud, called Accounting Connectors) to streamline your invoicing process. Once connected, you will be able to send invoices directly from CartonCloud to the accounting platform and have the payment status from the accounting platform automatically updated in CartonCloud.

### How to set up an Accounting Connector

CartonCloud integrates with the following accounting software applications:

| **Accounting Connector** | **How to set up the Accounting Connector** |
| --- | --- |
| Xero | I[ntegrate CartonCloud with Xero](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Integrate+CartonCloud+with+Xero) |
| MYOB Accounting Right Live | [Integrate CartonCloud with MYOB (Account Right Live)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Integrate-CartonCloud-with-MYOB-Account-Right-Live) |
| QuickBooks | [Integrate CartonCloud with QuickBooks](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Integrate-CartonCloud-with-QuickBooks) |
| Reckon | [Integrate CartonCloud with Reckon](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Integrate-CartonCloud-with-Reckon) |

### How to configure the Accounting Connector Settings

Each software application has its specific options, which can be configured in CartonCloud. You can either configure these at the [Organisation](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Organisation-Settings-Invoice) or [Customer Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Accounting-Software-Integrations-Accounting-Connectors) level.

### Multiple Accounting Connectors

CartonCloud supports multiple simultaneous Accounting Software Connections. This means you could have several MYOB connections, several Xero connections, or a combination of both within a single CartonCloud Account. You can then link some customers to one Accounting Connector and others to the other.

![accounting-software-integrations-accounting-connectors-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/accounting-software-integrations-accounting-connectors-0.png?width=404&height=215&name=accounting-software-integrations-accounting-connectors-0.png)

---

<a id="expired-token-for-accounting-connector"></a>
## Expired Token for Accounting Connector

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/expired-token-for-accounting-connector_

### Table of Contents

- Issue
- Why the issue has occurred
- How to resolve the issue
- If the issue persists after troubleshooting

### Issue

Your Accounting Connector (for example, XERO or MYOB) is no longer linked to CartonCloud due to the token expiring. This means you are no longer able to send invoices to your Accounting Connector.

### Why the issue has occurred

The Accounting Connector token will expire if:

- The admin's login credentials (for the Accounting Connector software) have changed or their profile is deleted.
- The 30-day two-factor authentication has expired on your trusted devices.

### How to resolve the issue

To resolve an expired token you will need to refresh the token.

Steps to refresh the token:

- Navigate to Organisation Settings by selecting, More>Organisation Settings.
- Select the Invoice tab.
- You will see your list of Accounting Connectors and under the Status column, the ones with expired tokens will read Token has Expired .
- To connect back to the Accounting Connector click Reconnect .
- You will then be prompted to log back into the accounting platform to refresh the token access. This will then reconnect the Accounting Connector and CartonCloud.

![expired-token-for-accounting-connector-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/expired-token-for-accounting-connector-0.png?width=670&height=238&name=expired-token-for-accounting-connector-0.png)

### If the issue persists after troubleshooting

If after selecting the reconnect button the token still does not refresh you can use the below steps to try and rectify the issue:

- If you don't receive a response from a token refresh you can retry using your existing refresh token for up to 30 minutes.
- If you can't refresh your access token in that time you'll need to send the user through the authorisation flow again to get a code that can be exchanged for new access and refresh token.

---

<a id="export-invoice-in-reckon-accounts-hosted-readable-format"></a>
## Export Invoice in Reckon Accounts Hosted readable format

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/export-invoice-in-reckon-accounts-hosted-readable-format_

In order to export invoices in Reckon readable format (IIF):

1) Connect to Reckon. Click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Integrate+CartonCloud+with+Reckon) on how to.

2) Go to Invoices/index page.

3) Select the Invoices that need to be exported and click "Export as" > "Reckon Importable format"

![export-invoice-in-reckon-accounts-hosted-readable-format-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/export-invoice-in-reckon-accounts-hosted-readable-format-0.png?width=670&height=370&name=export-invoice-in-reckon-accounts-hosted-readable-format-0.png)

4) A file with .iif format will be downloaded that can be imported to reckon directly.

<a id="import-cartoncloud-invoices-into-reckon-accounts-hosted"></a>
## Import CartonCloud Invoices into Reckon Accounts (Hosted)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/import-cartoncloud-invoices-into-reckon-accounts-hosted_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to steps

### Purpose

CartonCloud has functionality to allow you to export invoice files from the system and import directly into your Reckon Accounts (Hosted) application.

### How to steps

- Navigate to the Invoices page by selecting More > Invoices.
- Select the invoices you wish to export.
- Click Export as > Reckon Importable Format .
- The file will be created with the extension of .iif
- Navigate to Reckon .
- Select the toolbox icon on the right-hand side of the screen.
- Click Upload files and select the CartonCloud export file.
- This uploads the file into the hosted Reckon drive.
- Within Reckon go to the File Tab dropdown > Utilities > Import > IIF Files .
- Select the latest invoice and open.
- The file uploads, and invoices are created and an import confirmation pop-up is shown.

---

<a id="invoice-references-for-accounting-connector"></a>
## Invoice References for Accounting Connector

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/invoice-references-for-accounting-connector_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Adjusting the default invoice reference for the entire account
- Adjusting the invoice reference for a single customer
- Adjusting the invoice reference when pushing an invoice

### Purpose

When utilising CartonCloud's accounting integration for both Xero and MYOB you can select a reference to be applied to each invoice generated within the Accounting Software.

This reference is saved against the following fields in the Accounting Connectors:

1) In **Xero** as **Reference**

2) In **MYOB** as **JournalMemo**

This can be configured on a per-Customer basis, by editing the Customer settings, or it can be configured for all customers through the Organisation settings.

Please note that customer settings will override the organisation settings for a particular field if both settings are configured.

### Adjusting the default invoice reference for the entire account

- Navigate to the Organisation Settings, **More**>**Organisation Settings**.
- Select the Invoice tab.
- Scroll down to the Default Invoice Reference.
- Here you can customise the reference by either writing in the text that will appear on each invoice or using one of the Placeholders.

![invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-0.png?width=670&height=102&name=invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-0.png)

**The Placeholders include:**
![invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-1.png?width=205&height=264&name=invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-1.png)
If you select **Apply to all Customers** you will override every Customer's individual setting inside their Customer record. Only ever tick this if you want to update **ALL** Customers.

The placeholders will be replaced automatically with their value when the Invoice Reference is imported into your accounting software.

### Adjusting the invoice reference for a single Customer

- Navigate to the Customers page, Contacts > Customers .
- Select the relevant Customer and click Edit.
- Select the Invoice tab and then the Accounting Connector tab.

![invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-2.png?width=670&height=84&name=invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-2.png)

- Scroll down to the Default Invoice Reference.
- Here you can customise the reference by either writing in the text that will appear on each invoice or using one of the Placeholders.

![invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-3.png?width=670&height=102&name=invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-3.png)
**The Placeholders include:**
![invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-4.png?width=223&height=218&name=invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-4.png)

### Adjusting the invoice reference when pushing an Invoice

When pushing invoices to your Accounting Application manually, you're able to control the Reference which is sent, these changes will only affect the invoice you are pushing, and will not interfere with any Organisation or Customer settings.
![invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-5.png?width=266&height=293&name=invoice-references-for-accounting-connector-5.png)

---

<a id="integrate-cartoncloud-with-myob-account-right-live"></a>
## MYOB (Account Right Live) Accounting Connector (Invoicing)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/integrate-cartoncloud-with-myob-account-right-live_

### Table of Contents

- How it works
- How to set up the CartonCloud / MYOB integration

### How it works

Please note, we also can connect with MYOB Business

CartonCloud can be integrated with MYOB to allow automated invoicing.

The above steps can be automated entirely for every invoicing cycle. See step 4 for instructions on automating the process.

Note that **every time the Invoice is Uploaded to MYOB, a new Invoice is created** - you cannot alter an existing invoice by re-uploading it.

### How to set up the CartonCloud / MYOB integration

Connecting to MYOB can be broken into three main parts:

1. Connecting CartonCloud to your MYOB Organisation
2. Linking each customer in CartonCloud with the appropriate contact in MYOB
3. Pushing Invoices to MYOB
4. (optional) - Go Completely Automated

**1.****Connecting CartonCloud to your MYOB Organisation**

- Navigate to Organisation Settings, **More**>**Organisation Settings**.
- Select the **Invoice** tab and select **Connect to MYOB**.
- MYOB will now ask you to log in to your MYOB Organisation.
- Once you sign in, you'll be redirected back to CartonCloud, and you'll be able to see the MYOB connector is now active. The **Status** will read as **Need to connect to Company File**.
- Click on **Connect to Company File**to link your Organisation's company file to CartonCloud.

- This will open a box in the browser to link your desired MYOB Organisation Company File to CartonCloud. Leave the password BLANK as usually the company file has no password applied.

- Once you have selected and saved your Company File, MYOB connection to CartonCloud will be complete, and the status of MYOB will show 'Connected'.

- To configure which "Account" from your General Ledger to use for each payment type, click on **Modify Setting****s**.

**Fields that can be modified:**

| **Field** | **Description** | **Default** |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Name | The name of the Accounting Connection is shown in several places throughout the app. If you create multiple accounting connections (i.e., you push invoices for different clients into different MYOB accounts), it's important to name them differently. i.e., "Company A", "Company B." | MYOB Public App |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Default Tax Code | The default tax code to be applied to Line Items which pushed into MYOB The Tax Code can be overwritten for specific Customers / Suppliers within the Edit Customers / Edit Suppliers pages. | GST (if available) |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Start Date for Invoice/Bills | By default, if an invoice covers the week: "2016-11-21" to "2016-11-27", then the Invoice uploaded to MYOB will have an Invoice Date of "2016-11-28". This field sets the number of days which should be added to the Invoice Ending Date when uploaded to MYOB. For example, if you wanted the invoice to have the same date as the last day of the invoice, then you would enter the value 0, which would add 0 days to the End Date, making the Date "2016-11-27." Examples:     Start Date for Invoice/Bills   Date of Invoice in MYOB     2   2016-11-29     1   2016-11-28     0   2016-11-27     -1   2016-11-26     -7   2016-11-20 | Start Date for Invoice/Bills | Date of Invoice in MYOB | 2 | 2016-11-29 | 1 | 2016-11-28 | 0 | 2016-11-27 | -1 | 2016-11-26 | -7 | 2016-11-20 | 1 (the day after the Invoice is finished) |
| Start Date for Invoice/Bills | Date of Invoice in MYOB |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 2 | 2016-11-29 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 1 | 2016-11-28 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 0 | 2016-11-27 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| -1 | 2016-11-26 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| -7 | 2016-11-20 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Chart of Accounts | CartonCloud uses various types of Income and Expenses, which can be mapped to specific accounts within MYOB. Generally, you'll link these to your income accounts related to that particular type of charging. We suggest creating a unique account for each different revenue type as this allows you to report more accurately on where your revenue is coming from.   For example, in your MYOB chart of accounts, you should have an account for "Storage Income", which is used only for recording revenue from the Storage of items in your warehouse. However, all Expenses (coming from Bills) are always linked to a single Expense Account.    The Chart of Accounts can also be overwritten for specific Customers / Suppliers within the Edit Customers / Edit Suppliers pages. **For WMS Premium accounts the CartonCloud Account can be mapped to the Accounting Connectors General Ledger codes. See [Custom General Ledger Mapping](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Custom-General-Ledger-Mapping) for more information.** | N/A |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

- Once you have linked up each of your accounts, click **Save**.

The chart of accounts is reloaded from MYOB each time this page is reloaded, so if you make changes in your Chart of Accounts in MYOB and want to show that on CartonCloud, refresh the page.

**1.1 CartonCloud's Invoice number**

- CartonCloud provides the option to upload Invoices to MYOB with CartonCloud's Invoice number. To use this functionality, check the following checkbox (default state is unchecked):

For example, if the Invoice to be uploaded to MYOB has invoice number **1234**, its related MYOB Invoice will have Invoice number **'CC-1234'.**

**2. Linking each customer in CartonCloud with the appropriate contact in MYOB**

You now need to link each of your customers in CartonCloud with MYOB contacts. This needs to be performed so that CartonCloud knows which Contact in MYOB the invoice should be loaded against.

- Navigate to the Customers page, **Contacts**>**Customers**.
- Click the More Dropdown and select **Bulk Link Customers to {the name of your MYOB Connection}.**

Note: The following page may take a while to load as it first downloads a list of all your MYOB contacts and attempts to match as many as possible automatically.

- You can now see a list of all your CartonCloud customers and link them with the appropriate account in MYOB.
- Use the **MYOB Customer search box** to find each **MYOB Contact**. Select **Create New Contact in MYOB** if you can not find the contact.
- Once you have finished linking each of your **Customers in CartonCloud** to your **MYOB Contacts**, click **Save** at the bottom of the page.
- If you ever need to change an individual customer's link to **MYOB**, navigate the relevant Customer Settings and select **Invoice**>**Accounting Connector** tabs.

**3. Pushing Invoices to MYOB**

Suppose you have existing invoices in CartonCloud that you want to upload to **MYOB** (invoices created in CartonCloud before linking the customer to **MYOB**). In that case, you can do so by manually pushing them to MYOB from CartonCloud.

- Navigate to the Invoices page, **More**>**Invoices**.
- Select the Invoices you wish to upload to MYOB using the tick box.

- Scroll down and select **Link Accounting Connector**.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-myob-account-right-live-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-myob-account-right-live-0.png?width=670&height=308&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-myob-account-right-live-0.png)

- Once this is completed, the Invoice will appear with a faded MYOB logo. This means the Invoice is set up to be sent to MYOB but has not yet been sent.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-myob-account-right-live-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-myob-account-right-live-1.png?width=670&height=310&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-myob-account-right-live-1.png)

- Navigate to one of the individual Invoices you just selected to upload to MYOB and click **Upload to MYOB.**
- Uploading an invoice to MYOB will allow overwrite**the previous invoice; this** checkbox is ticked by default. Without this checked, it will create a new invoice in MYOB.

**3.1. Editing invoices outside of Cartoncloud**

Suppose you're editing an invoice created by Cartoncloud directly in MYOB itself. In that case, any changes made to the invoice will be retained and **NOT** overridden by any updates to the invoice from Cartoncloud unless you choose to overwrite the previous invoice when uploading.

**3.2. Emailing invoices to customers**

- You can email the Invoice to the customer by clicking **Email Invoice to Customer.**
- Suppose the customer's email address is not auto-populating in the email field. In that case, you can add this into the customer's email settings (See section  4.3 in 'Go Completely Automated' below for more information).

**4. Go Completely Automated**

With CartonCloud, you can automate your invoicing process so that everything (charges, invoice generation, sending invoices to MYOB and emailing of invoices) is seamless and done automatically for you. Provided the Invoice does not have any charge errors (requiring manual intervention), complete automation is possible and recommended.

**The below set-up is done within the Customer Settings.
You should only move to complete automation once you're happy that your rates are correct that you have everything connected correctly between CartonCloud and MYOB.**

**4.1. MYOB Invoice Status to Approved**

Complete automation requires **Approved**invoices to be sent to MYOB.

- Navigate to the relevant Customer Settings.
- Select the **Invoice** tab.
- Se the **Myob Invoice Status** to **Approved**.

**4.2. Turn on automatic Invoicing**

- Within the **Invoice**>**Details** tab, enable **Automatically Upload Invoices to MYOB** and **Automatically Email Invoice (with MYOB PDF attached), and Mark Invoice Approved**enabled.

**4.3. Ensure you have your customers email address set up to receive 'Invoice Notifications'**

For the email to be sent automatically, you need to have at least one email address set up to receive Invoice Notifications.

- Navigate to the **Email**>**Address** tab.
- Add a new email address to the **New email**field.
- Click **Add new email**.

- Enter the recipient's name and select the **Invoice Notification**.

---

<a id="error-orderconvertedtoinvoice-order"></a>
## MYOB - Error! OrderConvertedToInvoice:Order

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/error-orderconvertedtoinvoice-order_

### Table of Contents

- The error message
- Reasons for why the error has occurred
- How to resolve the error

### The error message

When uploading a CartonCloud invoice to MYOB you receive the following error message -

**Error! OrderConvertedToInvoice:Order should be in open status to convert to an invoice; Order.UID.**

### Reasons for why the error occurred

The error is usually seen when the MYOB order has already been updated to invoice status but the CartonCloud invoice still shows the MYOB order a 'Order'.

### How to resolve the error

You can either:

- Delete the MYOB invoice and re-create/re-upload it via CartonCloud.
- Delete both the MYOB and CartonCloud invoices and create entirely new invoices with the same charge entities associated with it.

---

<a id="myob-accountright-live-integration"></a>
## MYOB AccountRight Live Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/myob-accountright-live-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- What does the integration allow?
- Next steps to get connected

### Overview

MYOB (Account Right Live) is an accounting software and has the ability to integrate with CartonCloud.

Please note that we **do not** support MYOB Essentials

### What does the integration allow?

**Invoices from CartonCloud to be sent to MYOB**

![myob-accountright-live-integration-0-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/myob-accountright-live-integration-0-1.png?width=670&height=168&name=myob-accountright-live-integration-0-1.png)

- Allows you to link your CartonCloud account to your MYOB account
- Upload invoices from CartonCloud to MYOB
- Link customers in CartonCloud to your customers in MYOB
- This connection can be set up yourself. Please see MYOB (Account Right Live) Accounting Connector (Invoicing) for more information.

**Pulling orders from MYOB into CartonCloud as either Sales Orders or Consignments.**

![myob-accountright-live-integration-1-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/myob-accountright-live-integration-1-1.png?width=670&height=168&name=myob-accountright-live-integration-1-1.png)

- Invoices in MYOB can create orders in CartonCloud
- Rules can be defined to determine what invoices in MYOB are sent through to CartonCloud

Note: This integration is one-way and does not support updating the status of the order within MYOB, or providing any information back to MYOB upon pack completion/delivery.

### Next steps to get connected

- If you would like to set up the invoice integration from CartonCloud to MYOB, you can set this up yourself. Please see MYOB (Account Right Live) Accounting Connector (Invoicing) for more information.
- If you would like to set up the integration MYOB to CartonCloud please reach out to our team via CartonCloud Help (with the requirements included - more information regarding the listed requirements the better!). The team will confirm requirements, and provide a quote and timeframe.

---

<a id="myob-invoice-bill-templates"></a>
## MYOB Invoice/Bill Templates

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/myob-invoice-bill-templates_

To change the template for Invoices/Bills Pdf that get downloaded from MYOB to CartonCloud, do the following:

- Login your MYOB Account Right Company File. From the tabs at the top, click on " Card File " and then click on " Card List " button. This will open a new window with all the customers/suppliers listed in it.
- Double click on the Customer/Supplier whose Invoice/Bill template is to be changed. From the window that opens up, do the following:
- Click on the " Sellings Details " tab,
- Select the option " Sale Layout " to be " Service ",
- Select the " Printed Form " to be the one desired.
- For Suppliers:
- Click on " Buying Details " tab,
- Select the option " Purchase Layout " to be " Service "
- Select the " Printed Form "  to be the one desired.
- Click "Ok". This will save the above configuration. From then onwards, all the Invoice/Bill(whichever is updated) will be downloaded with the selected template ( Printed Form ).

---

<a id="integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks"></a>
## Quickbooks Accounting Connector (Invoicing)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks_

### Table of Contents

- How it works
- How to set up the CartonCloud/Quickbooks integration

### How it works

CartonCloud can be integrated with QuickBooks to allow automated invoicing.

The above steps can be automated entirely for every invoicing cycle. See step 4 for instructions on automating the process.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-0.png?width=670&height=629&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-0.png)

### How to set up the CartonCloud / QuickBooks Integration:

**Connecting to QuickBooks can be broken into three main parts:**

1. Connecting CartonCloud to your QuickBooks Organisation
2. Linking each customer in CartonCloud with the appropriate Customers in QuickBooks
3. Pushing Invoices to QuickBooks
4. (optional) - Go Completely Automated

**1.****Connecting CartonCloud to your QuickBooks Organisation**

- Navigate to the Organisation Settings, **More**>**Organisation Settings.**
- Select the**Invoice**tab.
- Click **Connect to QuickBooks**.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-1.png?width=670&height=141&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-1.png)

- You will then log into your QuickBooks account, or if you are already logged in, click **Connect**.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-2.png?width=670&height=553&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-2.png)
![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-3.png?width=670&height=344&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-3.png)

- You'll then be redirected back to CartonCloud, and you'll be able to see the QuickBooks Connection is now active.
- To configure the QuickBooks Products and Services to the CartonCloud invoice class, click on **Modify Settings**.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-4.png?width=670&height=181&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-4.png)
![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-5.png?width=670&height=544&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-5.png)
Please note, that the Account Codes **must** be set up in order to connect QuickBooks to customers (step 2)

| **Name** | **Description** |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Name | The name of the Accounting Connection is shown in several places throughout the app. If you create multiple accounting connections (i.e., you are pushing invoices for different clients into different QuickBooks accounts), it's important to name them differently. i.e., "Company A", "Company B." |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Start Date for Invoice/Bills | This field sets the number of days which should be added to the Invoice Ending Date when uploaded to QuickBooks. For example, if you wanted the invoice to have the same date as the last day of the invoice, then you would enter the value 0, which would add 0 days to the End Date, making the Date "2021-11-27." By default, the number of days is set to 1; therefore, if an invoice covers the week: "2021-11-21" to "2021-11-27", then the invoice uploaded to QuickBooks will have an Invoice Date of "2021-11-28". Examples:         **Start Date for Invoice / Bills**   **Date of Invoice in QuickBooks**     2   2021-11-29     1   2021-11-28     0   2021-11-27     -1   2021-11-26     -7   2021-11-20 | **Start Date for Invoice / Bills** | **Date of Invoice in QuickBooks** | 2 | 2021-11-29 | 1 | 2021-11-28 | 0 | 2021-11-27 | -1 | 2021-11-26 | -7 | 2021-11-20 |
| **Start Date for Invoice / Bills** | **Date of Invoice in QuickBooks** |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 2 | 2021-11-29 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 1 | 2021-11-28 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 0 | 2021-11-27 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| -1 | 2021-11-26 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| -7 | 2021-11-20 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

- Once you have linked up each of your Products and Services, click **Save**.

**Currency**

In QuickBooks, you will have a Home Currency, the default currency. Therefore, when connecting your QuickBooks and CartonCloud account, it is assumed you will be using the same currency for both. However, if it is not the same, you will receive a message like the below:

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-6.png?width=670&height=64&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-6.png)

The invoice in QuickBooks will be created in the currency you have configured for the customer in QuickBooks. Therefore, it is recommended that you use the same currency against your QuickBooks and CartonCloud account for all your customers.

**Custom Number Transactions**

Quickbooks has an optional setting called 'Custom Number Transactions' which allows you to use the CartonCloud invoice number. This setting will also allow for references to be shown on the PDF Invoice within Quickbooks. Click [here](https://quickbooks.intuit.com/learn-support/en-uk/help-article/customise-forms/change-number-invoices-transactions/L45oIBEzJ_GB_en_GB) for information on how to set this up.

**2. Linking each customer in CartonCloud with the appropriate contact in QuickBooks**

You now need to link each of your customers in CartonCloud with QuickBooks Customers. This ensures the correct invoice is loaded against the appropriate customer.

- Navigate to the Customers page, **Contacts**>**Customers**.
- Select the **More** button and then **Bulk Link Customers to {the name of your QuickBooks Connection}.**

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-7.png?width=670&height=98&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-7.png)

- Use the **QuickBooks Customer search box** to find each **QuickBooks Contact**to connect the two**.** Select**Create New Contact in QuickBooks**if you can not find the contact.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-8.png?width=670&height=114&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-8.png)

- Once you have finished linking each of your **Customers in CartonCloud** to your **QuickBooks Customers**, click **Save** at the bottom of the page.
- If you ever need to change an individual customer's link to QuickBooks, navigate to the relevant **Customer Settings**and select **Invoice**>**Accounting Connector** tabs.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-9.png?width=670&height=307&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-9.png)
**3. Pushing Invoices to QuickBooks**

If you have existing invoices in CartonCloud that you want to upload to QuickBooks (invoices created in CartonCloud before linking the customer to QuickBooks), you can do so by manually pushing them to QuickBooks from CartonCloud.

- Navigate to the Invoices page, **More**>**Invoices**.
- Select the Invoices you wish to upload to QuickBooks using the tick box.
- Select **Link Accounting Connector**.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-10.png?width=670&height=292&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-10.png)

- Once this is completed, the invoice will appear with a faded QuickBooks logo. This means the invoice is set up to be sent to QuickBooks but has not yet been sent.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-11.png?width=670&height=276&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-11.png)

- Navigate to one of the individual Invoices you just selected to upload to QuickBooks and click **Upload to QuickBooks.**

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-12](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-12.png?width=670&height=303&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-12.png)

- Repeat this process for each invoice.
- Once the invoice has been uploaded, several more QuickBooks Actions will become available.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-13](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-13.png?width=670&height=316&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-13.png)

- You can email the invoice to the customer by clicking **Email Invoice to Customer.**

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-14](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-14.png?width=670&height=280&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-14.png)

- If the customer's email address is not auto-populating in the email field, you can add this into the customer's email settings (See section  4.3 in 'Go Completely Automated' below for more information).

**4. Go Completely Automated**
With CartonCloud, you can automate your invoicing process so that everything (charges, invoice generation, sending invoices to QuickBooks and emailing of invoices) is seamless and done automatically for you. Provided the invoice does not have any charge errors (requiring manual intervention), complete automation is possible and recommended.

CartonCloud invoices will only be uploaded to QuickBooks once the invoice is in Approved status.

The below set-up is done within the Customer Settings.

You should only move to complete automation once you're happy that your rates are correct that you have everything connected correctly between CartonCloud and QuickBooks.

**4.1. QuickBooks Invoice Due Date**

- Navigate to the relevant Customer Settings.
- Select the **Invoice** tab.
- Set the **QuickBooks Invoice Due Date.**

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-15](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-15.png?width=670&height=145&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-15.png)

**4.2. Turn on automatic Invoicing**

- Within the **invoice**>**Details** tab, enable **Automatically Upload Invoices to QuickBooks.**

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-16](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-16.png?width=670&height=259&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-16.png)

**4.3. Ensure you have your customer's email address set up to receive 'Invoice Notifications'**

For the email to be sent automatically, you need to have at least one email address set up to receive Invoice Notifications.

- Navigate to the **Email**>**Address** tab.
- Add a new email address to the **New email**field.
- Click **Add new email**.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-17](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-17.png?width=670&height=230&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-quickbooks-17.png)

- Enter the recipient's name and select the **Invoice Notification**.
- Click **Save**.

<a id="integrate-cartoncloud-with-reckon"></a>
## Reckon Accounting Connector (Invoicing)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/integrate-cartoncloud-with-reckon_

### To create Reckon configurations in CartonCloud

Note - CartonCloud does not connect to Reckon directly the way it does for MYOB and Xero. Currently, an instance of Reckon configuration is created in CartonCloud to export Reckon readable files from CartonCloud.

- Navigate to the Organisation Settings, More > Organisation Settings .
- Select the Invoice tab.
- Click on the Connect to Reckon button.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-reckon-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-reckon-0.png?width=670&height=194&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-reckon-0.png)

- CartonCloud will navigate back to the default tab, so you will need to select the Invoice tab again.
- A new Configuration row will appear for Reckon.
- Click Modify Settings to configure various fields for Reckon.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-reckon-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-reckon-1.png?width=670&height=107&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-reckon-1.png)

- Make sure the name and character case (upper/lower) for the fields are the same as in the Reckon application.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-reckon-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-reckon-2.png?width=508&height=621&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-reckon-2.png)

- Select Save .
