<a id="reckon-one-integration"></a>
## Reckon One Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/reckon-one-integration_

### Table of Contents

- What does the integration allow?
  - Pushing invoices from CartonCloud to Reckon One
    - How to get connected
    - Price
  - Pulling orders from Reckon One into CartonCloud as either sale orders or consignments
    - How to get connected
    - Price

### What does the integration allow?

CartonCloud allows you to download a file which can be uploaded into Reckon One for creating invoices within Reckon

In addition to this, we can also pull through orders from Reckon One as either Sale Orders or Transport Consignments into CartonCloud. This allows your clients to connect CartonCloud to their Reckon One, automating pulling orders into CartonCloud

**Pushing invoices from CartonCloud to Reckon One**

CartonClouds integration with Reckon One for billing is not as seamless as our [Xero](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Xero+Integration) or [MYOB](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/MYOB+AccountRight+Live+Integration) integrations. It requires you to download a file and upload it into Reckon One.

![reckon-one-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/reckon-one-integration-0.png?width=665&height=209&name=reckon-one-integration-0.png)

Our Reckon One connection is for invoicing allows you to link your CartonCloud account to Reckon One your own account, link your customers in CartonCloud to your customers in Reckon One.

**How to get connected**

You can set this up yourself, more info here: [Integrate CartonCloud with Reckon](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Integrate+CartonCloud+with+Reckon)

**Price**

There are no additional charges for using this integration.

**Pulling orders from Reckon One into CartonCloud as either sales orders or consignments.**

![reckon-one-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/reckon-one-integration-1.png?width=654&height=209&name=reckon-one-integration-1.png)

When new invoices are created in Reckon One they can be automatically passed through to CartonCloud. This entirely eliminates data entry that your customers need to do to create Sale Orders or Consignments within CartonCloud. Rules can also be configured to control which orders get sent through. For example, if you only wanted orders with a particular reference to go through to CartonCloud for picking, then this rule can be created.

Note: this purely one-way and does not support updating the status of the order within Reckon One, or providing any information back to Reckon One upon pack completion/delivery.

**How to get connected**

Connections to pull invoices from Reckon One need to be configured by the CartonCloud team. Please [contact us](https://support.cartoncloud.com/servicedesk/customer/portal/2/create/27) to get Reckon One connected.

**Price**

Pricing is available on application. For more information please [contact us](https://support.cartoncloud.com/servicedesk/customer/portal/2/create/27).

---

<a id="repeating-myob-invoice-numbers"></a>
## Repeating MYOB Invoice numbers

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/repeating-myob-invoice-numbers_

### Issue

There is a known issue with MYOB where it is possible to generate repeating invoice numbers that have already been assigned to historical records. If you have manually assigned or changed an invoice number within MYOB, the system will reset the assignment of numbers to start incrementing from this manual number. This can result in CartonCloud invoice numbers not being unique inside MYOB if the invoice reference is generated by the accounting software itself.

### Solution

To avoid this problem from occurring, use the CartonCloud Invoice number as the MYOB invoice number by following the below steps:

- Select More in the main menu, followed by Organisation Settings .
- Select the Invoice tab.
- Scroll down to the Invoice Defaults settings box.
- Then enable Use CartonCloud's Invoice Number as MYOB's Invoice Number.
- To apply the setting, scroll to the bottom of the page and select Save .

This will result in the CartonCloud reference being used within the Accounting Software's invoice, ensuring it is unique.

---

<a id="what-to-do-after-an-outage-with-your-accounting-connector"></a>
## What to do after an outage with your Accounting Connector

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/what-to-do-after-an-outage-with-your-accounting-connector_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to reconnect your accounting connector after an outage

### Purpose

If you experience an outage with your Accounting Connector due to an API/system outage with the accounting platform, you will need to reconnect to the service.

### How to reconnect your Accounting Connector after an outage

**Through Customer Settings**

- Navigate to the Organisation Settings, **More**>**Organisation Settings**.
- Click the **Invoice** tab.
- Under Accounting Connectors, select the **Reconnect**hyperlink under the status column.

![what-to-do-after-an-outage-with-your-accounting-connector-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/what-to-do-after-an-outage-with-your-accounting-connector-0.png?width=670&height=226&name=what-to-do-after-an-outage-with-your-accounting-connector-0.png)
**Through the individual Invoice**

- Navigate to the relevant Invoice, **More**>**Invoices**.
- Scroll down to the **Accounting Connector Partner App**box.
- Select Connect to Xero (or the name of the relevant Accounting Connector).

![what-to-do-after-an-outage-with-your-accounting-connector-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/what-to-do-after-an-outage-with-your-accounting-connector-1.png?width=670&height=349&name=what-to-do-after-an-outage-with-your-accounting-connector-1.png)
You will need to re-upload any invoices that did not upload during the outage. To do so, navigate to the relevant Invoice and select the **Re-upload to Xero** (or accounting connectors name) button at the bottom of the screen.

---

<a id="integrate-cartoncloud-with-xero"></a>
## Xero Accounting Connector (Invoicing)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/integrate-cartoncloud-with-xero_

### Table of Contents

- How it works
- How to set up the CartonCloud / Xero integration

### How it works

CartonCloud can be integrated with Xero to allow automated invoicing.

The above steps can be automated entirely for every invoicing cycle. See step 4 for instructions on automating the process.

### How to set up the CartonCloud / Xero Integration:

Connecting to Xero can be broken into three main parts:

1. Connecting CartonCloud to your Xero Organisation
2. Linking each customer in CartonCloud with the appropriate contact in Xero
3. Pushing Invoices to Xero
4. (optional) - Go Completely Automated

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/KxnyBGxmotA

**1.****Connecting CartonCloud to your Xero Organisation**

- Navigate to the Organisation Settings, **More**>**Organisation Settings.**
- Select the**Invoice**tab.
- Click **Connect to Xero**.
- Xero will now ask you to provide authorization to CartonCloud so it can access your Xero account. Select **Authorise**.
- You'll then be redirected back to CartonCloud, and you'll be able to see the Xero Connection is now active.
- To configure which "Account" from your General Ledger to use for each payment type, click on **Modify Settings**.

A description of the fields is provided in the table below.

| **Field** | **Description** | **Default** |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Name | The name of the Accounting Connection is shown in several places throughout the app. If you create multiple accounting connections (i.e., you are pushing invoices for different clients into different Xero accounts), it's important to name them differently. i.e., "Company A", "Company B." | Xero Partner App |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Start Date for Invoice/Bills | By default, if an invoice covers the week: "2016-11-21" to "2016-11-27", then the Invoice uploaded to Xero will have an Invoice Date of "2016-11-28". This field sets the number of days which should be added to the Invoice Ending Date when uploaded to Xero. For example, if you wanted the Invoice to have the same date as the last day of the Invoice, then you would enter the value 0, which would add 0 days to the End Date, making the Date "2016-11-27." Examples:     **Start Date for Invoice / Bills**   **Date of Invoice in Xero**     2   2016-11-29     1   2016-11-28     0   2016-11-27     -1   2016-11-26     -7   2016-11-20 | **Start Date for Invoice / Bills** | **Date of Invoice in Xero** | 2 | 2016-11-29 | 1 | 2016-11-28 | 0 | 2016-11-27 | -1 | 2016-11-26 | -7 | 2016-11-20 | 1 (the day after the Invoice is finished) |
| **Start Date for Invoice / Bills** | **Date of Invoice in Xero** |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 2 | 2016-11-29 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 1 | 2016-11-28 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 0 | 2016-11-27 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| -1 | 2016-11-26 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| -7 | 2016-11-20 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Chart of Accounts | CartonCloud uses various types of Income and Expenses, which can be mapped to specific accounts within Xero. Generally, you'll link these to your income accounts related to that particular type of charging. We suggest creating a unique account for each different revenue type as this allows you to report more accurately on where your revenue is coming from.   For example, in your Xero chart of accounts, you should have an account for "Storage Income", which is used only for recording revenue from the Storage of items in your warehouse. However, all Expenses (coming from Bills) are always linked to a single Expense Account.       The Chart of Accounts can also be overwritten for specific Customers / Suppliers within the Edit Customers / Edit Suppliers pages. **For WMS Premium accounts the CartonCloud Account can be mapped to the Accounting Connectors General Ledger codes. See [Custom General Ledger Mapping](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Custom-General-Ledger-Mapping) for more information.** | N/A |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

- Once you have linked up each of your accounts, click **Save**.

The chart of accounts is reloaded from Xero each time this page is reloaded, so if you make changes in your Chart of Accounts in Xero and want to show that on CartonCloud, refresh the page.

*Note, if you are connecting the same Xero account to multiple CartonCloud accounts, you will need to create a different Xero user for each CartonCloud account.*

*Note, the Invoice Date in Xero will always be the day after the invoice end date in CartonCloud.*

**2. Linking each customer in CartonCloud with the appropriate contact in Xero**

You now need to link each of your customers in CartonCloud with Xero contacts. This needs to be completed so CartonCloud knows which Contact in Xero the Invoice should be loaded against.

- Navigate to the Customers page, **Contacts**>**Customers**.
- Select the **More** button and then **Bulk Link Customers to {the name of your Xero Connection}.**

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-xero-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-xero-0.png?width=670&height=114&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-xero-0.png)

Note: The next page may take a while to load as it first downloads a list of all your Xero contacts and attempts to match as many as possible automatically.

- You can now see a list of all your CartonCloud customers and link them with the appropriate account in Xero.
- Use the **Xero Customer search box** to find each **Xero Contact**. Select Create New Contact in Xero if you can not find the contact.
- Once you have finished linking each of your **Customers in CartonCloud** to your **Xero Contacts**, click **Save** at the bottom of the page.
- If you ever need to change an individual customer's link to Xero, navigate the relevant Customer Settings and select **Invoice**>**Accounting Connector** tabs.

**3. Pushing Invoices to Xero**

Suppose you have existing invoices in CartonCloud that you want to upload to Xero (invoices created in CartonCloud before linking the customer to Xero). In that case, you can do so by manually pushing them to Xero from CartonCloud.

- Navigate to the Invoices page, **More**>**Invoices**.
- Select the Invoices you wish to upload to Xero using the tick box.
- Scroll down and select **Link Accounting Connector**.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-xero-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-xero-1.png?width=670&height=292&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-xero-1.png)

- Once this is completed, the Invoice will appear with a faded Xero logo. This means the Invoice is set up to be sent to Xero but has not yet been sent.

![integrate-cartoncloud-with-xero-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integrate-cartoncloud-with-xero-2.png?width=670&height=305&name=integrate-cartoncloud-with-xero-2.png)

- Navigate to one of the individual Invoices you just selected to upload to Xero and click **Upload to Xero.**
- Repeat this process for each Invoice.
- Once the Invoice has been uploaded, several more Xero Actions will become available.
- You can email the Invoice to the customer by clicking **Email Invoice to Customer.**
- Suppose the customer's email address is not auto-populating in the email field. In that case, you can add this into the customer's email settings (See section  4.3 in 'Go Completely Automated' below for more information).

**4. Go Completely Automated**

With CartonCloud, you can automate your invoicing process so that everything (charges, invoice generation, sending invoices to Xero and emailing of invoices) is seamless and done automatically for you. Provided the Invoice does not have any charge errors (requiring manual intervention), complete automation is possible and recommended.

Note if you choose to void an invoice in CartonCloud that has already been uploaded to Xero, the invoice in Xero will not be voided.

The below set-up is done within the Customer Settings.
You should only move to complete automation once you're happy that your rates are correct that you have everything connected correctly between CartonCloud and Xero.

**4.1. Xero Invoice Status to Approved**

Complete automation requires **Approved**invoices to be sent to Xero.

- Navigate to the relevant Customer Settings.
- Select the **Invoice** tab.
- Set the **Xero Invoice Status** to **Approved**.

**4.2. Turn on automatic Invoicing**

- Within the **Invoice**>**Details** tab, enable **Automatically Upload Invoices to Xero** and **Automatically Email Invoice (with Xero PDF attached), and Mark Invoice Approved**enabled.

**4.3. Ensure you have your customers email address set up to receive 'Invoice Notifications'**

For the email to be sent automatically, you need to have at least one email address set up to receive Invoice Notifications.

- Navigate to the **Email**>**Address** tab.
- Add a new email address to the **New email**field.
- Click **Add new email**.
- Enter the recipient's name and select the **Invoice Notification**.
- Select **Save**.

---

<a id="xero-403-authenticationunsuccessful-error"></a>
## XERO: 403 - AuthenticationUnsuccessful Error

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/xero-403-authenticationunsuccessful-error_

### Table of Contents

- The error message
- Reasons for why the error has occurred
- How to resolve the error

### The error message

When uploading an invoice to Xero you are met with the following error - From XERO: 403 - AuthenticationUnsuccessful .

### Reasons for why the error has occurred

This error means that the Xero and CartonCloud connection is no longer authenticated. This could have occurred because the user who set up the connection is no longer an active user.

### How to resolve the error

To resolve the error you will need to disconnect and then reconnect the connection. To do this you will need to:

- Navigate to Organisation Settings > Invoice .
- Against the Xero connection that is producing the error, click the Disconnect from Xero button. Do not click the Delete button .
- You will then need to reconnect the connection and log back in again to Xero - Xero Accounting Connector (Invoicing)

If you are still having issues after completing the above steps please lodge a case with our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

---

# Integrations > API

<a id="api-clients"></a>
## API Clients

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/api-clients_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use case and benefits
- Sandbox testing
- How to steps

### Purpose

Please note, to be able to create API Clients, you need to have the Administrator role enabled and the 'Allow this user to edit other Users' option selected.

![api-clients-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/api-clients-0.png?width=533&height=109&name=api-clients-0.png)

CartonCloud provides an API to facilitate integrations with third-party systems.

To use this API, you must first create an API Client in CartonCloud.

For more technical and detailed information on the CartonCloud API and how to use it, please see the [API Documentation](https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/).

### Use Case and Benefits

**Use Case**

Your Customer may wish to use the API to send and receive data from their internal system to CartonCloud. Data could include:

- Sending inbound and outbound orders (Purchase Orders and Sale Orders) to CartonCloud.
- Sending transport jobs (Consignments) to CartonCloud.
- Sending new or updating existing Products in CartonCloud.
- Retrieve stock on hand report from CartonCloud.

**Benefits**

- Allows users with the technical skills and knowledge to create their own integrations between CartonCloud and third-party systems.
- Enables the user to send data into CartonCloud from another system and retrieve information from CartonCloud.
- Greater control over data retrieved and sent between the two systems.
- Have access to the return messages to troubleshoot if issues do occur.
- You do not have to wait for a particular trigger to send and receive information, as you have the freedom to do so at any time.

### Sandbox Customer Testing (Optional)

Before using the API Client on a live Customer, it is highly recommended that you create a Sandbox Customer first to test the API.

A sandbox is a testing environment utilised to test API calls that will not impact the live Customer's account and data.

**To create a Sandbox Customer:**

- Duplicate the Customer you are giving API access to. See [Adding Customers and Duplicating Customers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Adding-Customers-and-Duplicating) for instructions on how to duplicate a Customer.
- Ensure the name of the Customer includes the word Sandbox to avoid confusion. For example, 'Coastal Coffee Company Sandbox'.
- Provide the API user with Customer access to the Sandbox Customer. See [Creating or Inviting New Users](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Creating-or-Inviting-New-Users) for instructions on how to add a new user.
- Provide the API user with the Sandbox Customer UUID, Tenant UUID and Warehouse UUID (if more than one warehouse). See the [UUID section](https://help.cartoncloud.com#UUID) of this article for more information.
- Optionally, you can create Products in the Sandbox Customer. See [Exporting and Importing Products](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Exporting-and-Importing-Products) for instructions on how to create new products in bulk.
- You can then create test orders to ensure the structure used to send the data to CartonCloud is correct.

If creating a Sale Order, ensure there is available stock (Purchase Order is in allocated status).

- Once testing is complete, you will update the API Client with access to the live Customer. See the [Going Live with the API Client](https://help.cartoncloud.com#going-live)  section of this article before updating the API Client with access to the live Customer.

See the [Going Live with the API Client](https://help.cartoncloud.com#going-live) section of this article before updating the API Client with access to the live Customer.

### How To Steps

**How to add an API Client**

- Navigate to **Contacts**>**API Clients**.
- Select **+Add API Client** in the top left corner.

![api-clients-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/api-clients-1.png?width=670&height=284&name=api-clients-1.png)

- Fill in the **Name** field with a descriptive name relating to the client.

If this is the first time creating an API Client for the Customer, it is highly recommended you create a sandbox customer first. Ensure you include the word sandbox in the name field when creating the sandbox customer. See the [Sandbox testing](https://help.cartoncloud.com#sandbox-testing) section of this article for more information.

- Select the Customers and Warehouses you wish to give the API access to.
- Select an API Role for the API Client. See [API Roles](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/API-Roles) for more information.

If the Customer only uses the Transport system, enable TMS Create Jobs.

If the Customer only uses the Warehouse system, enable WMS Create Jobs.

If the Customer uses both the Transport and Warehouse systems, you will need to select both TMS Create Jobs and WMS Create Jobs (as demonstrated in the image below).

Do not use API Full Access for Customers.

See [API Roles](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/API-Roles) for more information.

- Slide the **INACTIVE** toggle to **ACTIVE**.
- Select **Save**.

![api-clients-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/api-clients-2.png?width=494&height=337&name=api-clients-2.png)

- A pop-out window will be prompt you with information regarding generating credentials.
- Once you have read the information, tick both boxes and select **Generate Credentials**.

![api-clients-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/api-clients-3.png?width=447&height=242&name=api-clients-3.png)

- The Client ID and Client Secret will be displayed. Remember to store these credentials securely and don't lose them. You will need to provide these to the API user.

If you do lose the credentials, please see the [Generating New Credentials](https://help.cartoncloud.com#generating-new-credentials)section of this article.

![api-clients-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/api-clients-4.png?width=550&height=220&name=api-clients-4.png)

- In addition to the above information, you will also need to provide the API user with the **Customer UUID**, **Tenant UUID,** and, if applicable, the **Warehouse UUID** (if more than one warehouse).

Using the Copy button next to the Client ID and Client Secret allows you to easily transfer the data to the API user. You can also do this from the Edit API Client page.

![api-clients-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/api-clients-5.png?width=386&height=327&name=api-clients-5.png)

**Universally Unique Identifier (UUID)**

The Universally Unique Identifier identifies certain information in a computer system. It ensures that data is being sent and received from the correct Customer, Tenant and Warehouse.

You will need to provide the API user with the;

- Customer UUID (during testing, you will need to provide the Sandbox Customer UUID and then later the live Customer UUID).
- Tenant UUID
- Warehouse UUID (only if you have more than one warehouse)

**To locate the Customer UUID:**

If you are creating a Sandbox Customer, ensure you provide the Sandbox Customer UUID for testing, and once testing is complete, you provide the live Customer UUID.

- Navigate to the Customers page, **Contacts**>**Customers**.
- Select the applicable Customer.
- The UUID is within the Details box at the bottom of the screen.

![api-clients-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/api-clients-6.png?width=607&height=365&name=api-clients-6.png)

**To locate the Tenant UUID:**

- Navigate to Organisation Settings, **More**>**Organisation Settings**.
- Navigate to the **Organisation** tab.
- The UUID is within the Basic Organisation Information box at the bottom of the screen.

**To locate the Warehouse UUID:**

- Navigate to the Warehouses page by typing **Warehouses** into the Search for anything bar.
- Use the UUID column to find the UUID for the relevant Warehouse.

**Going Live with the new API Client**

If you tested the API Client with a Sandbox Customer, follow the below steps before going live with the new API Client:

- Delete all of the sandbox customers orders/consignments in CartonCloud.
- Deactivate the sandbox customer in CartonCloud.
- Edit the API Client and remove the sandbox customer and add the live customer.
- Provide the user with the live Customer UUID.

Once the API Client is updated with the live Customer, you can track their usage (the number of API calls made) using the API Client Usage Report. Please see the [API Client Usage Report](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/API-Client-Usage-Report)  page for more information.

**Generating New Credentials**

Note that the old credentials will become invalid if you generate new credentials, and any existing connections that use the old credentials will fail.

If the credentials of an existing API Client are misplaced, you can generate new credentials.

- Navigate to the API Clients page, **Contacts**>**API Clients.**
- Select the API Client.
- Select **Generate Credentials**.

![api-clients-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/api-clients-7.png?width=456&height=387&name=api-clients-7.png)
![api-clients-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/api-clients-8.png?width=493&height=271&name=api-clients-8.png)

- Carefully read the information provided before generating new Credentials, as creating new credentials will destroy the old credentials, which can break existing integrations.
- Once confirming you wish to proceed, the new Client ID and Client Secret will be displayed. Remember to store these credentials securely and don't lose them.

![api-clients-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/api-clients-9.png?width=533&height=213&name=api-clients-9.png)

- The developer will also need the Tenant UUID and Customer(s) UUID when advising of credentials.

**Postman Setup for API Access**

You can access our CartonCloud API Postman Collection here: [https://www.getpostman.com/collections/REDACTED](https://www.getpostman.com/collections/REDACTED)

Once imported into postman, you'll need to setup collection variables and then get an API token.

Clicking on the collection in postman will bring up the collection settings.

First, navigate to the "Variables" tab, and insert your tenantUuid, customerUuid, authClientId and AuthClientSecret into the "Current Value" column.

![api-clients-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/api-clients-10.png?width=556&height=243&name=api-clients-10.png)

If you don't know the tenantUuid and/or customerUuid, you can find this out once you have a working Access Token by making requests to: [https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#user](https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#user) and [https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#list-customers](https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#list-customers) respectively.

For more help with Variables refer to the [Postman Documentation](https://learning.postman.com/docs/sending-requests/variables/)

- With these variables filled out, jump to the "Authorization" tab and you'll be able to Get New Access Token:
- With the access token generated, click Use Token .

Please note excessive API usage charges apply, click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hubfs/API%20Clients%20FAQ.pdf) for more information.

---

When creating an API Client, you must select the applicable API roles for the Client. These roles will dictate the API Client's access to your account when using the API; therefore, it is important that you enable the correct Roles for each Client.

| **WMS Add Product** | Add, view Warehouse Products (Product Masters) Please note, even if you have the [setting](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Customer-Settings-Warehouse-Management-Product-tab) **Stop Customers from being able to add their own Products** enabled for the customer associated with the API Client, this will be ignored, and the customer using the API Client will still be able to add a WMS Product. | [https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#create-warehouse-product](https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#create-warehouse-product) [https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#get-product](https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#get-product) |
| **WMS Edit Product** | Edit, view Warehouse Products (Product Masters) | [https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#update-product-put](https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#update-product-put)  [https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#partial-product-update-patch](https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#partial-product-update-patch) [https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#get-product](https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#get-product) |

<a id="custom-fields-in-the-api"></a>
## Custom Fields in the API

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/custom-fields-in-the-api_

[Custom Fields](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Custom+Fields) are used extensively throughout CartonCloud for capturing and storing customised data.

This page explains how to interact with Custom Fields through our [Public API](https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/).

Custom fields are considered **properties**through the API.

A Purchase Order, for example, has Custom Fields at both the Order Level, and also at the Item Level (for defining which stock to select).

![custom-fields-in-the-api-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-fields-in-the-api-0.png?width=274&height=396&name=custom-fields-in-the-api-0.png)

Custom Fields are referenced through their "Mapped Field". For example, given the screenshot below, the "EComm ID" may be accessed through the field `ecommId` :

![custom-fields-in-the-api-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-fields-in-the-api-1.png?width=670&height=323&name=custom-fields-in-the-api-1.png)

`{`
`  ``"type"``: ``"OUTBOUND"``,    .....`
`    ``"properties"``: {        ``"ecommId"``: ``"456ad1e1-9aef-42b9-8520-9d96493187c1"`    `},`
`    ``...`
`}`

If you do not have access to the Custom Fields section of CartonCloud (for example, you are a Customer of a 3PL building your own integration), please contact the account owner to find out exactly which fields are available, and what you need to provide.

# Integrations > Carrier Connections

<a id="carrier-account-mapping"></a>
## Carrier Account Mapping

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/carrier-account-mapping_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How Carrier Account Mapping works
- How to set up Carrier Account Mapping
- Example Carrier Account Mapping

### Purpose

This functionality is currently rolling out and may not be available on your account yet

Carrier Account Mapping allows you to define a set of rules that automatically update the Carrier, Delivery Run, and Service Type on a Consignment after a shipment is booked through a [Carrier Connection](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-carrier-connections). This removes the need to manually update these fields on every Consignment after booking a shipment, saving time and reducing the risk of errors.

### How Carrier Account Mapping works

When a shipment is booked via a Carrier Connection, CartonCloud looks for a matching Carrier Account Mapping rule based on the Carrier Provider, Carrier Account, and Service used to book the shipment. If a match is found, the Consignment is automatically updated with the Carrier, Delivery Run, and Service Type defined in that rule.

CartonCloud uses the following priority order to find a matching rule:

- Exact match — CartonCloud first looks for a mapping that exactly matches both the Carrier Account and the Service used to book the shipment.
- Carrier Account match with 'All' Services — If no exact match is found, CartonCloud looks for a mapping that matches the Carrier Account but has 'All' selected for the Service.
- 'All' Carrier Accounts — If still no match is found, CartonCloud uses any mapping configured with 'All' for the Carrier Account (which applies regardless of the account or service used).

If no matching rule is found, the Consignment is not updated. The shipment booking still completes successfully — only the Carrier, Delivery Run, and Service Type fields on the Consignment are unaffected.

**Carrier Account Mapping and Transport Lanes**

[Zone Sets](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/zone-sets) and [Transport Lanes](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/transport-lanes) are processed **before** Carrier Account Mapping. This means the Carrier and Delivery Run assigned by the Transport Lane configuration are already set on the Consignment by the time the Carrier Account Mapping runs.

This also means you can reference those values in your [Carrier Selection Rules](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/carrier-selection-rules). For example, if your Zone Set determines that a Consignment should use Direct Couriers, you can create a Carrier Selection Rule that preselects the Direct Couriers rate on the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/pack-screen) by default.

### How to set up Carrier Account Mapping

- Navigate to More > Organisation Settings .
- Select the Transport > Carrier Account Mapping tab.
- Add a mapping by selecting a Carrier Account , Service , Carrier , Delivery Run and Service Type .
- Click Save .
- To add another mapping, click the plus icon .

![2026-04-22_15-04-26](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-22_15-04-26.png?width=670&height=287&name=2026-04-22_15-04-26.png)

### Example Carrier Account Mapping

![2026-04-29_12-43-56](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-29_12-43-56.png?width=670&height=167&name=2026-04-29_12-43-56.png)

<a id="carrier-selection-rules"></a>
## Carrier Selection Rules

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/carrier-selection-rules_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How Carrier Selection Rules Work
- How to set up Carrier Selection Rules
- Example Carrier Selection Rules

### Purpose

This functionality is currently rolling out and may not be available on your account yet

Carrier Selection Rules allow you to automatically preselect the most suitable carrier when packing an order on the Pack Screen. Rather than manually choosing a carrier each time, you can configure rules based on order details such as destination, customer, or consignment type — and CartonCloud will apply the first matching rule to auto-select a carrier rate for you.

Carrier Selection Rules are used in conjunction with [Self-Managed Carrier Connections](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-carrier-connections). To use this feature, you must first have at least one Self-Managed Carrier Connection configured. See the [Self-Managed Carrier Connections](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-carrier-connections) article for more information.

### How Carrier Selection Rules Work

Carrier Selection Rules are evaluated in priority order when carrier rates are fetched on the Pack Screen. The first rule with conditions that match the current order is used to auto-select a carrier rate.

You can configure Carrier Selection Rules based on:

- Destination
- Weight and dimensions
- Service type
- Customer
- Cost (eg: Cheapest)
- + More

Each rule consists of two parts:

- Conditions: When the rule should apply — one or more criteria based on fields from the Address, Consignment, or Sale Order. All conditions within a rule must be met for it to match.
- Action: What CartonCloud does when the rule matches.

**Key behaviours to understand:**

- Priority order: Rules are evaluated from top to bottom. The first rule that matches is applied. You can reorder rules to adjust their priority.
- Catch-all rule: You can create one rule with no conditions. This rule acts as a catch-all and is always placed at the bottom of the list. It applies when no other rule matches.
- Auto-selected rate: The rate determined by the matching rule is automatically selected on the Pack Screen.
- Remaining rates: All other rates that are not auto-selected are listed in order from cheapest to most expensive, so packers can still choose an alternative if needed.
- Carrier and service availability: If a rule is set up to use a specific carrier and service, but the carrier or service is not available when rates are loaded on the Pack Screen, the rule is skipped. For example, if a rule is configured to use Australia Post Express when the service type is Express but Australia Post Express is unavailable for the shipment due to weight or volume restrictions, that rule is ignored and the next matching rule is applied instead.

**Use cases for Carrier Selection Rules include:**

- Automatically routing fragile or urgent orders to a premium carrier service.
- Sending orders for specific customers via their preferred carrier.
- Routing deliveries to certain regions or postcodes via a specific carrier.
- Applying a default catch-all rule that selects the cheapest available rate for all remaining orders.

### How to set up Carrier Selection Rules

**Adding a new Rule:**

- Navigate to More > Organisation Settings .
- Select the Transport > Carrier Selection Rules tab.
- Click + Add Rule .

![2026-04-22_12-03-27](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-22_12-03-27.png?width=670&height=313&name=2026-04-22_12-03-27.png)

- Enter a Rule name and ensure it is Active if you wish for it to apply straightaway.
- Apply Conditions to the Rule. These Conditions will dictate when and if the rule is applied. You can add one or more Conditions to a Rule. All Conditions must be met for the Rule to match.
  - Select a Field . Fields are available from the following categories:
    - Address
    - Consignment
    - Sale Order
  - Select the Operator .
  - Enter the Value to compare against.
  - Repeat these steps to add additional Conditions to the Rule if required.

![2026-04-22_12-11-14](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-22_12-11-14.png?width=338&height=518&name=2026-04-22_12-11-14.png)

- Apply Actions to the Rule. This dictates the Action that will take place when the Conditions are met.
  - Action type:
    - Rate comparison : you can choose which rate will appear when the Conditions are met, either the cheapest or fastest rate.
    - Specific carrier: you can define a certain carrier and service to be selected when the Conditions are met.

![2026-04-22_12-11-59](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-22_12-11-59.png?width=350&height=538&name=2026-04-22_12-11-59.png)

**Creating a Catch-All Rule:**

A catch-all Rule has no Conditions and applies to any order that does not match the previous rule. You can only have one catch-all Rule, and it is always placed at the bottom of the Rules list. For example, you may have a catch-all Rule that selects the cheapest rate.

![2026-04-22_10-56-04](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-22_10-56-04.png?width=380&height=480&name=2026-04-22_10-56-04.png)

**Reordering Rules:**

Rules are evaluated in the order they appear on the list. To change the priority of a Rule:

- On the Carrier Selection Rules page, locate the Rule you wish to update the priority of.
- Use the up and down arrows next to the Rule to move it higher or lower in the list.

![2026-04-22_12-13-05](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-22_12-13-05.png?width=670&height=232&name=2026-04-22_12-13-05.png)

- The Catch-All Rule (no conditions) always remains at the bottom of the list and cannot be moved above other rules.

**Activating Rules:**

Rules will only be applied if they are active. To ensure they are active:

- Select the Active button when creating the Rate and/or
- Enable it by toggling it on from the Carrier Selection Rules page.

![2026-04-22_12-13-05 (1)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-22_12-13-05%20(1).png?width=670&height=232&name=2026-04-22_12-13-05%20(1).png)

### Example Carrier Selection Rules

- Example #1 - send orders below a weight threshold with a certain carrier

![2026-04-30_14-27-28](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-30_14-27-28.png?width=333&height=511&name=2026-04-30_14-27-28.png)

- Example #2 - send orders using the service type to determine the carrier

![2026-04-29_12-50-45](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-29_12-50-45.png?width=335&height=518&name=2026-04-29_12-50-45.png)

- Example #3 - route fragile items via a certain carrier

![2026-04-22_11-58-25](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-22_11-58-25.png?width=311&height=464&name=2026-04-22_11-58-25.png)

- Example #4 - send orders for a specific state/area via a certain carrier

![2026-04-30_14-25-18](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-30_14-25-18.png?width=333&height=516&name=2026-04-30_14-25-18.png)

<a id="self-managed-australia-post-carrier-connection"></a>
## Self-Managed Australia Post Carrier Connection

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-australia-post-carrier-connection_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Considerations
- Benefits
- Cost
- How to create a Self-Managed Australia Post Carrier Connection
- Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed Australia Post Carrier Connection
- Recommended Next Steps

### Overview

This functionality is currently rolling out and may not be available on your account yet

The Self-Managed Australia Post Carrier Connection allows you to connect your own Australia Post account to CartonCloud. This enables you to manage shipments, access live rates and generate shipping labels directly within CartonCloud using your negotiated carrier rates.

### Considerations

- You will require a Australia Post account.
- Carrier Selection Rules allow you to automatically assign the most suitable carrier during packing. These rules will need to be set up once the connection is enabled.See here for details.
- Carrier Account Mapping allows you to define a set of rules that automatically update the Carrier, Delivery Run, and Service Type on a Consignment after a shipment is booked through a Carrier Connection.Carrier Account Mapping will need to be set up once the connection is enabled. See here for details.
- Y ou need to use the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/pack-screen) to access Carrier Connections.

### Benefits

- Manage Australia Post shipments from within CartonCloud - book shipments and print labels all from the Pack Screen.
- Streamline the packing process.
- Use your existing Australia Post agreement and pricing.
- Consolidate workflows into a single system.

### Cost

- There is no CartonCloud connection fee per connection.

### How to create a Self-Managed Australia Post Carrier Connection

**At the Customer level:**

- Navigate to Self-Managed Integrations by typing Self-Managed Integrations into the Search for anything.
- Select the Customer you wish to set the integration up for.
- Select AusPost .

![2026-04-27_10-01-07](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-27_10-01-07.png?width=670&height=295&name=2026-04-27_10-01-07.png)

- Click Configure .

![2026-04-27_10-02-08](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-27_10-02-08.png?width=670&height=296&name=2026-04-27_10-02-08.png)

- Enter your AusPost account API Key , API Secret and Account number .
- Click Connect .

![2026-04-27_10-52-48](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-27_10-52-48.png?width=670&height=286&name=2026-04-27_10-52-48.png)

- You will receive a pop-up message confirming the connection was successful. A green number will appear against the AusPost Carrier, indicating the number of accounts connected.

**At the Organisation level:**

- Navigate to Self-Managed Integrations by typing Self-Managed Integrations into the Search for anything.
- Under My Organisation, select Edit Integrations .

![2026-04-27_09-40-00](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-27_09-40-00.png?width=670&height=200&name=2026-04-27_09-40-00.png)

- Select **AusPost**.

![2026-04-27_10-51-11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-27_10-51-11.png?width=670&height=199&name=2026-04-27_10-51-11.png)

- Click **Configure**.

![2026-04-27_10-52-02](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-27_10-52-02.png?width=670&height=240&name=2026-04-27_10-52-02.png)

- Enter your AusPost account API Key , API Secret and Account number .
- Click Connect .

![2026-04-27_10-52-48](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-27_10-52-48.png?width=670&height=286&name=2026-04-27_10-52-48.png)

You will now see AusPost shipping rates appear on the Pack Screen when packing orders.

### Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed Australia Post Carrier Connection

- Navigate to Self-Managed Integrations by typing Self-Managed Integrations into the Search for anything.
- To disconnect an Organisation level connection, select Edit Integrations .
- To disconnect a Customer level connection, select the relevant Customer .
- Select AusPost .
- Select the bin icon to remove the connection.

![2026-04-27_11-34-02](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2026-04-27_11-34-02.png?width=670&height=286&name=2026-04-27_11-34-02.png)

### Recommended Next Steps

- Set up Carrier Selection Rules .
- Set up Carrier Account Mapping .

<a id="self-managed-carrier-connections"></a>
## Self-Managed Carrier Connections

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-carrier-connections_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Benefits
- Available Carriers
- How it works
  - Pack Screen
  - Walleted Rates vs BYO Rates
  - Carrier Selection Rules
  - Carrier Account Mapping
- How to set up Self-Managed Carrier Connections
- Cost

### Overview

This functionality is currently rolling out and may not be available on your account yet

Self-Managed Carrier Connections allow you to connect your own carrier accounts to CartonCloud using EasyPost, Shippit, or supported direct carrier integrations.

Once connected, you can access live rates, book shipments and print shipping labels directly within CartonCloud using your BYO carrier rates and/or via the walleted rates from EasyPost / Shippit.

### Benefits

- Manage all shipments from within CartonCloud - compare rates, book shipments and print labels all from the Pack Screen.
- Use your existing carrier agreements and pricing.
- Access rate shopping across multiple carriers.
- Avoid separate subscriptions to EasyPost, Shippit or other Shipping software.
- Consolidate workflows into a single system.

### Available Carriers

Supported carriers depend on the integration platform you are using:

- Direct Connections:

### How it works

You can connect carrier connections at two levels:

**Organisation Level**

- Carrier accounts are available across all customers
- Rates can be used across all Customers within your CartonCloud account

**Customer Level**

- Carrier accounts are specific to an individual customer
- Rates are only available when processing that customer’s orders

From the[Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/pack-screen)**,** you can compare rates across both levels.

#### Pack Screen

Carrier Connections are used directly within the Pack Screen, allowing you to view and select freight options during the packing process. Within the Shipping Rate window on the Pack Screen, you can:

- Compare live shipping rates
- Select a carrier and service
- Book freight
- Print shipping labels

See the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/pack-screen) Knowledge Base article for more information.

#### Walleted Rates vs BYO Rates

**Walleted Rates**

- Pre-negotiated rates with carriers provided by EasyPost and Shippit directly.
- Requires payment details to be entered into those platforms.

**BYO Rates**

- BYO rates are rates you already have established with the carrier outside of EasyPost or Shippit.

#### Carrier Selection Rules

Carrier Selection Rules allow you to automatically assign the most suitable carrier during packing. This reduces manual decision-making and ensures consistent carrier selection.

See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/carrier-selection-rules) on how to set up Carrier Selection Rules.

#### Carrier Account Mapping

Carrier Account Mapping allows you to define a set of rules that automatically update the Carrier, Delivery Run, and Service Type on a Consignment after a shipment is booked through a Carrier Connection.

See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/carrier-account-mapping) on how to set up Carrier Account Mapping.

### How to set up Self-Managed Carrier Connections

See instructions for each integration platform:

- Self-Managed EasyPost Carrier Connection
- Self-Managed Shippit Carrier Connection
- Self-Managed Australia Post Carrier Connection
- Self-Managed United States Postal Service (USPS) Post Carrier Connection (coming soon)

### Cost

A fee is charged per connected platform:

- Each EasyPost or Shippit connection counts as one billable connection
- Connections can exist at both the organisation and customer levels

Example:

| **Account** | **Platform & Carriers** | **Connections Charged** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Your 3PL Company | Shippit - TNT, Dragonfly, Aramex | 1 |
| Customer A | Shippit - DragonFly, Couriers Please | 1 |
| Customer B | EasyPost - UPS, DHL, FedEx | 1 |
| Total billable connections | 3 |  |

Please reach out to our[Service Desk team](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/contactsupport) for pricing.

---

<a id="self-managed-easypost-carrier-connection"></a>
## Self-Managed EasyPost Carrier Connection

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-easypost-carrier-connection_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Considerations
- Benefits
- Limitations
- Cost
- How to create a Self-Managed EasyPost Carrier Connection
- Understanding and Using EasyPost
- Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed EasyPost Carrier Connection
- Recommended Next Steps

### Overview

This functionality is currently rolling out and may not be available on your account yet

The Self-Managed [EasyPost](https://www.easypost.com/) Carrier Connection allows you to connect your own carrier accounts to CartonCloud. This enables you to book and manage shipments, access live rates and generate shipping labels within CartonCloud using your BYO carrier rates and/or via the walleted rates from EasyPost.

EasyPost is recommended for North American and Global carriers.

### Considerations

- You will require a EasyPost account. This can be created on demand directly from within CartonCloud when you enable the integration. See the steps below.
- Carrier Selection Rules allow you to automatically assign the most suitable carrier during packing. These rules will need to be set up once the connection is enabled. See here for details.
- Carrier Account Mapping allows you to define a set of rules that automatically update the Carrier, Delivery Run, and Service Type on a Consignment after a shipment is booked through a Carrier Connection.Carrier Account Mapping will need to be set up once the connection is enabled. See here for details.
- This is a paid integration; please ensure you read the included costs below .
- You need to use the Pack Screen to access Carrier Connections.

### Benefits

- Manage all shipments from within CartonCloud - book shipments, compare rates and print labels all from the Pack Screen.
- Streamline the packing process.
- Use your existing carrier agreements and pricing (BYO) or use EasyPost’s Prenegotiated Carrier Rates (Walleted Rates).
- Access rate shopping across multiple carriers.
- Avoid paying for a separate EasyPost subscription.
- Consolidate workflows into a single system.

### Limitations

If you have an existing EasyPost account, there is currently no way to connect it to CartonCloud. If you have an existing EasyPost account and want to move to one provided by CartonCloud refer to the steps [below](https://help.cartoncloud.com#how-to).

### Cost

- No EasyPost subscription or label fee.
- CartonCloud fee per connection. The fee is charged per EasyPost account, not the number of carriers connected to that account.

### How to create a Self-Managed EasyPost Carrier Connection

**At the Customer level:**

- Navigate to Self-Managed Integrations by typing Self-Managed Integrations into the Search for anything.
- Select the Customer you wish to set the integration up for.
- Select EasyPost .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-48-9220-AM.png?width=670&height=299&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-48-9220-AM.png)

- Click Configure .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-48-4763-AM.png?width=665&height=296&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-48-4763-AM.png)

- An EasyPost account will be automatically created for you.

- You will receive a pop-up message confirming the connection was successful. A green number will appear against the EasyPost Carrier, indicating the number of accounts connected.
- Click Reconfigure to access your EasyPost account.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-57-9023-AM.png?width=639&height=325&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-57-9023-AM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-57-3444-AM.png?width=632&height=320&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-57-3444-AM.png)

**At the Organisation level:**

- Navigate to Self-Managed Integrations by typing Self-Managed Integrations into the Search for anything.
- Under My Organisation select Edit Integrations .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-31-2034-AM.png?width=649&height=194&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-31-2034-AM.png)

- Select EasyPost .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-30-7256-AM.png?width=646&height=293&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-30-7256-AM.png)

- Click Configure .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-30-2391-AM.png?width=638&height=285&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-30-2391-AM.png)

- An EasyPost account will be automatically created for you.
- You will receive a pop-up message confirming the connection was successful. A green number will appear against the EasyPost Carrier, indicating the number of accounts connected.
- Click Reconfigure to access your EasyPost account.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-40-1155-AM.png?width=639&height=276&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-40-1155-AM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-41-0789-AM.png?width=632&height=314&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-41-0789-AM.png)

You will now see shipping rates appear on the Pack Screen when packing orders.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-40-5517-AM.png?width=646&height=311&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-40-5517-AM.png)

### Understanding and Using EasyPost

To access your EasyPost account use the Reconfigure button on the Carrier Connection setup.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-24-40-2759-AM.png?width=630&height=272&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-24-40-2759-AM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-24-39-7485-AM.png?width=634&height=315&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-24-39-7485-AM.png)

From here you can:

- Add or remove carriers
  - Select Carriers from the side navigation and either enable carriers in the Wallet Carrier Accounts section or scroll down and select Add Carriers .
  - For the BYO carriers (carriers not included in the Wallet Carrier Accounts with EasyPost) you will need to enter your account information. For more information see here .
- Add payment details to pay for freight:
  - Navigate to Wallet in the side navigation.
  - Click Setup Wallet .
  - When using Wallet rates from EasyPost, you will be billed directly from EasyPost for these shipments at the end of each week. This is not charged or managed by CartonCloud, and is a direct commercial relationship between EasyPost and your company.

If you need help with EasyPost itself please contact their support team [here](https://support.easypost.com/hc/en-us/requests/new) or visit their [Help Center.](https://support.easypost.com/hc/en-us)

### Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed EasyPost Carrier Connection

- Navigate to Self-Managed Integrations by typing Self-Managed Integrations into the Search for anything.
- To disconnect an Organisation level connection, select Edit Integrations .
- To disconnect a Customer level connection, select the relevant Customer .
- Select EasyPost .
- Select the bin icon to remove the connection.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-25-21-0189-AM.png?width=670&height=313&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-25-21-0189-AM.png)

### Recommended Next Steps

- Set up Carrier Selection Rules .
- Set up Carrier Account Mapping .

### How to create a Self-Managed EasyPost Carrier Connection

**At the Customer level:**

- Navigate to Self-Managed Integrations by typing Self-Managed Integrations into the Search for anything.
- Select the Customer you wish to set the integration up for.
- Select EasyPost .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-48-9220-AM.png?width=670&height=299&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-48-9220-AM.png)

- Click Configure .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-48-4763-AM.png?width=665&height=296&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-48-4763-AM.png)

- An EasyPost account will be automatically created for you.

- You will receive a pop-up message confirming the connection was successful. A green number will appear against the EasyPost Carrier, indicating the number of accounts connected.
- Click Reconfigure to access your EasyPost account.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-57-9023-AM.png?width=639&height=325&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-57-9023-AM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-57-3444-AM.png?width=632&height=320&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-22-57-3444-AM.png)

**At the Organisation level:**

- Navigate to Self-Managed Integrations by typing Self-Managed Integrations into the Search for anything.
- Under My Organisation select Edit Integrations .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-31-2034-AM.png?width=649&height=194&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-31-2034-AM.png)

- Select EasyPost .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-30-7256-AM.png?width=646&height=293&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-30-7256-AM.png)

- Click Configure .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-30-2391-AM.png?width=638&height=285&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-30-2391-AM.png)

- An EasyPost account will be automatically created for you.
- You will receive a pop-up message confirming the connection was successful. A green number will appear against the EasyPost Carrier, indicating the number of accounts connected.
- Click Reconfigure to access your EasyPost account.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-40-1155-AM.png?width=639&height=276&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-40-1155-AM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-41-0789-AM.png?width=632&height=314&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-41-0789-AM.png)

You will now see shipping rates appear on the Pack Screen when packing orders.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-40-5517-AM.png?width=646&height=311&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-23-40-5517-AM.png)

### Understanding and Using EasyPost

To access your EasyPost account use the Reconfigure button on the Carrier Connection setup.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-24-40-2759-AM.png?width=630&height=272&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-24-40-2759-AM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-24-39-7485-AM.png?width=634&height=315&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-24-39-7485-AM.png)

From here you can:

- Add or remove carriers
  - Select Carriers from the side navigation and either enable carriers in the Wallet Carrier Accounts section or scroll down and select Add Carriers .
  - For the BYO carriers (carriers not included in the Wallet Carrier Accounts with EasyPost) you will need to enter your account information. For more information see here .
- Add payment details to pay for freight:
  - Navigate to Wallet in the side navigation.
  - Click Setup Wallet .
  - When using Wallet rates from EasyPost, you will be billed directly from EasyPost for these shipments at the end of each week. This is not charged or managed by CartonCloud, and is a direct commercial relationship between EasyPost and your company.

If you need help with EasyPost itself please contact their support team [here](https://support.easypost.com/hc/en-us/requests/new) or visit their [Help Center.](https://support.easypost.com/hc/en-us)

### Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed EasyPost Carrier Connection

- Navigate to Self-Managed Integrations by typing Self-Managed Integrations into the Search for anything.
- To disconnect an Organisation level connection, select Edit Integrations .
- To disconnect a Customer level connection, select the relevant Customer .
- Select EasyPost .
- Select the bin icon to remove the connection.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-25-21-0189-AM.png?width=670&height=313&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-25-21-0189-AM.png)

### Recommended Next Steps

- Set up Carrier Selection Rules .
- Set up Carrier Account Mapping .

<a id="self-managed-shippit-carrier-connection"></a>
## Self-Managed Shippit Carrier Connection

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-shippit-carrier-connection_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Considerations
- Benefits
- Limitations
- Cost
- How to create a Self-Managed Shippit Carrier Connection
- Understanding and Using Shippit
  - Shippit Account Structure
  - Shippit Merchant Accounts and Warehouses
  - Using Shippit Wallet Rates
  - Support with Shippit
- Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed Shippit Carrier Connection
- Recommended Next Steps

### Overview

This functionality is currently rolling out and may not be available on your account yet

The Self-Managed [Shippit](https://www.shippit.com/) Carrier Connection allows you to connect your own carrier accounts to CartonCloud. This enables you to book and manage shipments, access live rates and generate shipping labels within CartonCloud using your BYO carrier rates and/or via the walleted rates from Shippit.

### Considerations

- You will require a Shippit account. If you do not have one, you can create one during the setup process by submitting a form. See the steps below .
- Carrier Selection Rules allow you to automatically assign the most suitable carrier during packing. These rules will need to be set up once the connection is enabled. See here for details.
- Carrier Account Mapping allows you to define a set of rules that automatically update the Carrier, Delivery Run, and Service Type on a Consignment after a shipment is booked through a Carrier Connection.Carrier Account Mapping will need to be set up once the connection is enabled. See here for details.
- This is a paid integration; please ensure you read the included costs below .
- You need to use the Pack Screen to access Carrier Connections.

### Benefits

- Manage all shipments from within CartonCloud - book shipments, compare rates and print labels all from the Pack Screen.
- Streamline the packing process.
- Use your existing carrier agreements and pricing (BYO) or use Shippit’s Prenegotiated Carrier Rates (Walleted Rates).
- Access rate shopping across multiple carriers.
- Avoid paying for a separate Shippit subscription.
- Consolidate workflows into a single system.

### Limitations

When configuring [Carrier Selection Rules](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/carrier-selection-rules), all carriers and service types available within Shippit are displayed, irrespective of whether those carriers are enabled within your Shippit account(s).

### Cost

- No Shippit subscription or label fee. If using Shippit Wallet Carriers and Rates, those will be billed directly to you from Shippit.
- CartonCloud fee per connection. The fee is charged per Shippit Merchant Account , not the number of carriers connected to that account. Please reach out to our Service Desk team for pricing.

### How to create a Self-Managed Shippit Carrier Connection

**At the Customer level:**

- Navigate to Self-Managed Integrations by typing Self-Managed Integrations into the Search for anything.
- Select the Customer you wish to set the integration up for.
- Select Shippit .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-43-9291-AM.png?width=2048&height=996&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-43-9291-AM.png)

- Select Configure .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-42-2630-AM.png?width=2048&height=999&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-42-2630-AM.png)

- If you have a Shippit account, enter the API key . If you do not, select Request a Shippit account and fill out the form.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-40-6635-AM.png?width=902&height=690&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-40-6635-AM.png)

- You will receive a pop-up message confirming the connection was successful. A green number will appear against the Shippit Carrier, indicating the number of accounts connected.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-42-8361-AM.png?width=2048&height=1000&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-42-8361-AM.png)

**At the Organisation level:**

- Navigate to Self-Managed Integrations by typing Self-Managed Integrations into the Search for anything.
- Under My Organisation, select Edit Integrations .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-40-2855-AM.png?width=2048&height=692&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-40-2855-AM.png)

- Select Shippit.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-41-7605-AM.png?width=2048&height=911&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-41-7605-AM.png)

- Select Configure .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-43-3498-AM.png?width=2048&height=1042&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-43-3498-AM.png)

- If you have a Shippit account, enter the API key and select the Warehouses the connection will apply for. If you do not, select Request a Shippit account .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-40-9399-AM.png?width=764&height=878&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-40-9399-AM.png)

- You will receive a pop-up message confirming the connection was successful. A green number will appear against the Shippit Carrier, indicating the number of accounts connected.
- You will now see shipping rates appear on the Pack Screen when packing orders.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-41-2575-AM.png?width=2048&height=986&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-14-41-2575-AM.png)

### Understanding and Using Shippit

#### Shippit Account Structure

Shippit uses a two-tier account structure made up of a single **Company account** and one or more **Merchant accounts**.Carrier connections live at the Merchant level only.

- Company account — represents the 3PL (your CartonCloud tenancy). Users added at this level have visibility across the Company level and all Merchant accounts beneath it. Company accounts do not hold any carrier connections.
- Merchant account — represents each of the 3PL's customers. Each Merchant holds its own carrier connections and rates, and users added at this level can only view their own merchant account. A Merchant account can also be created for the 3PL itself, and connected to CartonCloud at the Organisation Level, providing carrier connections to all customers.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-15-56-0485-AM.png?width=2048&height=1092&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-15-56-0485-AM.png)

#### Shippit Merchant Accounts and Warehouses

Each Shippit Merchant account holds a single collection address, so every shipment booked through it must originate from the same physical location. This means a separate Merchant account is required for each shipping location (each Warehouse in CartonCloud) — even when the same merchant operates across multiple warehouses.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-16-02-7354-AM.png?width=2048&height=887&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-16-02-7354-AM.png)

***Note:****If consignments from multiple warehouses are collected from a single location, you can*

#### Using Shippit Wallet Rates

When using Wallet rates from Shippit, you will be billed directly from Shippit for these shipments at the end of each week. This is not charged or managed by CartonCloud, and is a direct commercial relationship between Shippit and your company.

#### Support with Shippit

Please visit the [Shippit support site](https://support.shippit.com/en-US/shippit/directories) for more information.

### Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed Shippit Carrier Connection

- Navigate to Self-Managed Integrations by typing Self-Managed Integrations into the Search for anything.
- To disconnect an Organisation level connection, select Edit Integrations .
- To disconnect a Customer level connection, select the relevant Customer .
- Select Shippit .
- Select the bin icon to remove the connection.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-May-01-2026-06-16-34-8637-AM.png?width=1010&height=688&name=undefined-May-01-2026-06-16-34-8637-AM.png)

### Recommended Next Steps

- Set up Carrier Selection Rules .
- Set up Carrier Account Mapping .

# Integrations > Integrations with other software

<a id="australia-post-integration"></a>
## Australia Post Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/australia-post-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- What does the integration allow?
- What you need to get started
- Next steps to get connected

### Overview

Australia Post (AusPost) is an Australian carrier and has the ability to integrate with CartonCloud

### What does the integration allow?

**A CartonCloud Sale Order or Consignment creates a shipment within AusPost**

**![australia-post-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/australia-post-integration-0.png?width=670&height=86&name=australia-post-integration-0.png)**

- Delivery address and items with respective weights are transferred from CartonCloud to the new shipment record in AusPost
- Select when the shipment is created, for example, once the order is packed or dispatched

**Pulling tracking information from Australia Post to CartonCloud**

**![australia-post-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/australia-post-integration-1.png?width=670&height=83&name=australia-post-integration-1.png)**

- Two way integration allowing the courier tracking number to be pulled from AusPost to the CartonCloud order
- The tracking details can be sent to other application such as Shopify when marking orders as fulfilled.

**Printing Australia Post labels**

**![australia-post-integration-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/australia-post-integration-2.png?width=670&height=335&name=australia-post-integration-2.png)**

- AusPost labels can be configured to print directly from within CartonCloud.
- Printing of the labels can occur automatically by selecting an order or consignment status event such as when the order is marked as packed or by clicking a Custom Buttons.
- This limits the need to continually switch between applications when packing an order

### What you need to get started

- The customer must be created in CartonCloud with products set up (product codes should match the product codes set up in AusPost)
- Your customer requires a AusPost account

### Next steps to get connected

- Read the [Australia Post Requirements](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Australia-Post-Requirements)
- Send an integration request via a [New Ticket](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket)[https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport)(with the requirements included - more information regarding the listed requirements the better!). The team will provide you with a quote upon sending through your request.

---

<a id="australia-post-requirements"></a>
## Australia Post Requirements

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/australia-post-requirements_

### Table of Contents

- Integration requirements
  - Requirements from the CartonCloud Tenant (the 3PL, owner of the CartonCloud account)
  - Requirements from the Australia Post account holder

### Integration requirements

If you have decided you would like to integrate CartonCloud with Australia Post, we require you to send through an integration request via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) with the below information.

**Pricing will be provided upon sending through your request.**

### Requirements from the CartonCloud Tenant (the 3PL, owner of the CartonCloud account)

- The customer the integration is for must be set up in CartonCloud
- Please confirm the trigger you would like to set to determine when an order is sent to Australia Post. For example, when a Sale Order reaches the status of Packed or Dispatched.

### Requirements from the Australia Post account holder

- Complete and submit a CartonCloud Integrations Request Form .
- Please confirm:
  - If only specific orders should be sent to Australia Post, such as orders going to a particular state.
  - If you use AusPost services such as EParcel or Startrack
  - If you need/have an AusPost Merchant account
  - If you want to access the AusPost portal or prefer to action everything from within the CartonCloud aoo
  - What data you would like to send from CartonCloud to AusPost
  - What information you would like to receive back from AusPost to CartonCloud.
  - If you do require a summary report printed, or labels printed

<a id="automated-sms-notifications"></a>
## Automated SMS Notifications

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/automated-sms-notifications_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How it works
- What we need from you to set up the integration
- Setting up a Twilio account
- Account SID and Auth Token
- Twillo phone number

### Purpose

CartonCloud has the capability to integrate with SMS services such as

Twilio

to send out automated SMS notifications to your customers.

By integrating automated SMS notifications directly into CartonCloud it’s possible to:

- Store a mobile number against a Consignment or Address that you wish to send notifications to
- Send an automated SMS when a Consignment’s Status is updated - such as when it’s marked ‘In Transit’
- Send another automated SMS when the consignment is delivered, then email the POD directly to a selected email address.

Our integrations team will guide you through the setup process. Once completed, your notifications will go out displaying the information you want at the time you need.

### How it Works

Initially, you will need to sign up to an SMS service such as [Twilio](https://www.twilio.com/) and send us a few pieces of information about that account in an integrations ticket [here](https://support.cartoncloud.com/servicedesk/customer/portal/2/create/27).

As you hold the account with Twilio they will charge you directly for the messages being sent.

We then set up Custom Fields within CartonCloud to allow mobile numbers to be stored against the Consignment or alternatively we can use the telephone number provided within the Address.

[Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parsers) can also be adjusted if required to allow data to be imported directly into these fields.

Our integrations team will also discuss the finer details with you, such as when you would like the notifications to take place and what information you would like them to include.

### What we need from you to set up the Integration

We require 3 key pieces of information from you to set up the integration,

- The Twilio Account SID
- Auth Token
- Twilio Phone Number

Steps on how to obtain these are provided below.

### Setting up a Twilio Account

Twilio is a communications platform that CartonCloud integrates with to allow messages to automatically be sent when an event is triggered in the system.

To set up your own Twilio account, navigate to [https://www.twilio.com/](https://www.twilio.com/)

- Once there, select the Sign up button at the top right of the home page.
- Fill in the required form with your details. Then submit.
- Check your email to verify your account. Be sure to check your junk mail if you do not receive it.
- When confirming the verification email you will need to provide your phone number with Twilio
- They will then send you a confirmation number in a text message which you will need to enter to verify the mobile number.
- Twilio will then ask you some personalisation questions. Once answering these you will land on the Dashboard.

### Account SID and Auth Token

As shown below (blacked out for security reasons). These need to be copied using the icon on the right and pasted directly into your [integration request](https://support.cartoncloud.com/servicedesk/customer/portal/2/create/27).

### Twilio Phone Number

This is the phone number the notification messages will appear to be coming from, however, we are also able to set a contact name against it that receivers will see.

- To get a Twilio number, begin by selecting Get a Trial Number on the dashboard.
- Initially, a US number will be suggested, however, you will need a number for the country you are in, so select Search for a different number .
- On the next page, select your Country, then click Search .
- Select a Mobile type number with SMS capabilities and an Address requirement of "Any".
- To claim the number, you will need to comply with regulatory requirements. Twilio provides its own documentation on how to complete this .
- Once you have completed buying the number please include it in your integration request .
- And that's it! Our integrations team will guide you through any further configuration that may be required for your Twilio account.

---
