## Available Integrations

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/available-integrations_

### Table of Contents

- Available Integrations
- Zapier
- Outgoing webhooks

### Available Integrations

Please see our website [here](https://www.cartoncloud.com/integrations) for a list of available integrations. If the platform you wish to integrate with isn't listed, please reach out to the team with your request [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) .

### Zapier

We're integrated with [Zapier](https://zapier.com/apps/cartoncloud/integrations), so you can build your own integration into CartonCloud via Zapier.

Please be sure to checkout our [Zapier Integration FAQ](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Zapier+Integration+FAQ)

### Outgoing Webhooks

We're able to fire webhooks from CartonCloud to your application on event triggers.

Currently, we need to configure these internally, so if you need one constructed then please reach out to the team via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) .

<a id="bigcommerce-integration"></a>
## BigCommerce Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/bigcommerce-integration_

### Table of Contents

- What does the integration allow?
  - Pulling sale orders from BigCommerce into CartonCloud
  - Updating orders as shipped in BigCommerce
  - Update inventory levels in BigCommerce
- How to get connected
- BigCommerce integration requirements
  - From the CartonCloud 3PL
  - From the BigCommerce store owner
- One-way and two-way integration

### What does the integration allow?

CartonCloud is integrated with BigCommerce allowing orders created in BigCommerce to automatically flow into CartonCloud as Sale Orders.

**Pulling Sale Orders from BigCommerce into CartonCloud**

![bigcommerce-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bigcommerce-integration-0.png?width=455&height=182&name=bigcommerce-integration-0.png)

This is a one-way integration in which a new order in BigCommerce creates a new Sale Order within CartonCloud. It transfers the delivery address, reference, and all of the ordered items.

The integration is designed to be flexible with the option to include some additional custom fields that can be pushed through from BigCommerce. Additionally, we can configure rules to control which orders within BigCommerce should be transferred to CartonCloud (so not everything goes through and you have control over which are transferred).

**Updating Orders as shipped in BigCommerce**

![bigcommerce-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bigcommerce-integration-1.png?width=440&height=176&name=bigcommerce-integration-1.png)
This is a two-way integration in which orders that have originated from BigCommerce will then be marked as shipped once the CartonCloud Sale Order has reached a chosen status (Packed or Dispatched).

Additionally, if [Shippit](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Shippit+Integration) or [StarShipit](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Starshipit+Integration) is also integrated with your CartonCloud account, then tracking numbers can also be returned to BigCommerce.

**Update Inventory Levels in BigCommerce**

As an optional extra, an automatic processor can be built to send stock on hand information back to BigCommerce. This requires the BigCommerce store to install and configure the [stock-sync plugin](https://www.bigcommerce.com.au/apps/stock-sync/).

### How to get connected

Connections to BigCommerce need to be configured by the CartonCloud team.

**This integration requires you to have:**

- A BigCommerce Account
- A BigCommerce user for CartonCloud to use for pulling orders.

To get this setup, please contact your Implementation Manager or [contact us](https://support.cartoncloud.com/servicedesk/customer/portal/2/create/27).

### BigCommerce Integration Requirements

To successfully integrate CartonCloud with a BigCommerce store we first require some additional information as outlined below.

**From the CartonCloud 3PL**

To integrate CartonCloud with your customer's BigCommerce store we require the following to be sent before we begin the build,

**One-Way Integration**

- [The Customer must be set up in CartonCloud](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+a+Customer)
- [The Customer must have some Products set up](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Products). Having this ready before we complete the build allows for a smooth testing process.
- CartonCloud Product Codes must align with the customer's SKU codes in BigCommerce. This is so the system knows which products to add on orders
- Please confirm whether a POD should be sent to the end receiver or not (if an email address is supplied in BigCommerce).

**Two-Way Integration**

- If you have chosen to have a 2-way integration, please also confirm at which stage you would us to mark the order shipped in BigCommerce. We can use either of the statuses of Packed or Dispatched. *Please note the 'Packed' status can only be used for orders which do not have tracking information sent back.*
- If we are sending tracking information back to BigCommerce, please let us know the list of carriers that might be used. This is so we can map those carriers to the specific carrier code accepted by the BigCommerce API.

**From the BigCommerce Store Owner**

To integrate your BigCommerce account with CartonCloud, we require the following to be set before we begin the build,

**One-Way and Two-Way Integration**

A one-way integration is having orders flow in from BigCommerce to CartonCloud only.

- Complete and submit a [CartonCloud Integrations Request Form](https://forms.gle/E7piEToNwGLCJmmb8).
- A store API account must be set up for CartonCloud. [The BigCommerce website provides instructions to assist with this process](https://support.bigcommerce.com/s/article/Store-API-Accounts).
- Once the API account is set up, we require the following to be sent through in copied text format (not a screenshot).
  - API Path
  - API Credentials (Client ID, Client Secret, Access Token)
- 3 or more paid, unfulfilled orders within BigCommerce for us to use as test data during set-up. These can be real or test orders for mapping purposes
- The trigger you would like us to set. This will determine when an order is sent to CartonCloud. For example: Once a BigCommerce order is placed and or once a BigCommerce order is placed and in a paid status.
- If only specific orders or products should be sent to CartonCloud, such as orders going to a particular state. Please let us know these conditions with as much detail provided as possible.
- If orders will be going to addresses outside of Australia please let us know.
- An email address where we can send notifications, in the event that an order does not make it to CartonCloud.

---

<a id="cin7-integration"></a>
## Cin7 Omni (formerly known as Cin7) Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/cin7-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- What does the integration allow?
- What you need to get started
- Next steps to get connected

### Overview

Cin7 Omni (formerly known as Cin7) is a cloud based inventory management software and has the ability to integrate with CartonCloud.

### What does the integration allow?

**A new order in Cin7 Omni creates a new order in CartonCloud**

**![cin7-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/cin7-integration-0.png?width=400&height=200&name=cin7-integration-0.png)**

- The delivery address, customer reference and all ordered items is transferred to the new Sale Order in CartonCloud from the Cin7 Omni order
- Rules can be configured to control what orders from Cin7 Omni are sent across to CartonCloud
- Ability to include some additional information from Cin7 Omni and map them to Custom Fields in CartonCloud

**Marking Sale Orders or Purchase Orders as Completed in Cin7 Omni**

**![cin7-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/cin7-integration-1.png?width=400&height=200&name=cin7-integration-1.png)**

- Orders that have originated from Cin7 Omni will be marked as dispatched (for Sale Orders) or received (for Purchase Orders) once the CartonCloud Sale Order has reached a chosen status (e.g Packed or Dispatched Sale Orders or Verified or Allocated Purchase Orders)

### What you need to get started

- The [customer must be created in CartonCloud](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Setting-up-a-Customer) with [products set up](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Setting-up-Products) (product codes should match the product codes set up in Ciny Omni)
- The customer requires a Cin7 Omni account

### Next steps to get connected

- Read the integration requirements [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Cin7)
- Send an integration request via a[New Ticket](https://help2.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) (with the requirements included - the more information regarding the listed requirements the better!). The team will provide you with a quote upon sending through your request.

---

<a id="cin7"></a>
## Cin7 Omni (formerly known as Cin7) Requirements

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/cin7_

### Table of Contents

- Integration Requirements
  - Requirements from the CartonCloud Tenant (the 3PL, owner of the CartonCloud account)
  - Requirements from the Cin7 Omni account holder

### Integration Requirements

If you have decided you would like to integrate CartonCloud with Cin7 Omni, we require you to send through an integration request via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) with the below information. Pricing will be provided upon sending through your request.

### Requirements from the CartonCloud Tenant (the 3PL, owner of the CartonCloud account)

- The customer the integration is for must be set up in CartonCloud
- The customer must have products set up and the product codes must align with the customer’s product codes in Cin7 Omni.
- Please confirm:
  - Invoices are to be attached to Sale Orders
  - If a two way integration, which Sale Order status (Packed or Dispatched) in CartonCloud will be the trigger for the Cin7 Omni order to be marked as completed.

### Requirements from the Cin7 Omni account holder

- Please advise the type(s) of integration(s) you would like to be provided. For example :
  - Sales Orders         - Direction 1 way ( Cin7 Omni to CartonCloud )               OR
  - Sales Orders         - Direction 2 way ( Cin7 Omni to CartonCloud to Cin7 Omni )
  - Purchase Orders  - Direction 1 way ( Cin7 Omni to CartonCloud )               OR
  - Purchase Orders  - Direction 2 way ( Cin7 Omni to CartonCloud to Cin7 Omni )
  - Transfer Orders  - Direction 1 way ( Cin7 Omni to CartonCloud )               OR
  - Transfer Orders  - Direction 2 way ( Cin7 Omni to CartonCloud to Cin7 Omni )
- Complete and submit a CartonCloud Integrations Request Form
- Contact the Cin7 Omni team:
  - For new Cin7 Omni customers contact onboarding@Cin7 Omni.com![](https://static.hsstatic.net/BlogImporterAssetsUI/ex/missing-image.png)
  - For existing Cin7 Omni customers contact upgrades@Cin7 Omni.com and create a support ticket.
  - If you need to filter by BranchID please let the Cin7 Omni team know
  - If you have non-pickable items to be filtered out
  - If you have Batch/Lot, Expiry Date, or Partial Fulfilment requirements let the Cin7 Omni team know
- Please advise your CartonCloud Tenant (the 3PL provider)
  - To ensure all the SKUs to come from Ciin7 align with the product SKUs in CartonCloud
  - If orders will be going to addresses outside of Australia
  - An email address where notifications can be sent to if an order does not successfully import to CartonCloud
  - Specify any specific requirements you have in detail

<a id="detrack-integration"></a>
## Detrack Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/detrack-integration_

### Table of Contents

- What does the integration allow?
  - Pushing sale orders from CartonCloud to Detrack
- Connection requirements
- How to get connected

### What does the integration allow?

CartonCloud is integrated with Detrack allowing jobs picked in the CartonCloud WMS to be automatically transferred into the Detrack POD system.

**Pushing Sale Orders from CartonCloud to Detrack**

![detrack-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/detrack-integration-0.png?width=480&height=192&name=detrack-integration-0.png)

While there are various ways the integration can be configured, the most common way is to trigger a new transport job to be created within Detrack once a Sale Order is packed within CartonCloud.

Once this is done, orders automatically appear in Detrack with the status "Info Received". The delivery address and sale order products are transferred across.

(Note: you can configure it to create the job on Sale Order approval or other statuses too).

In addition, rules can be created to control which orders are sent to Detrack. For example, you may use a [Custom Field](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Custom+Fields)within your Sale Order to track whether or not the order should be sent to Detrack.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/IWSAsBYQ63U

### Connection Requirements

To connect Detrack with CartonCloud we require your API Key. This can be accessed within Detrack from Settings > API Key.

![detrack-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/detrack-integration-1.png?width=526&height=330&name=detrack-integration-1.png)

### How to get connected

Connections to Detrack need to be configured by the CartonCloud team.

Please contact us to get Detrack connected.

---

<a id="gosweetspot-integration"></a>
## GoSweetSpot Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/gosweetspot-integration_

### Table of Contents[#what-does-the-integration-allow](https://help.cartoncloud.com#what-does-the-integration-allow)

- Overview
- What does the integration allow?
- What you need to get started
- Next steps to get connected

### Overview

GoSweetSpot is a freight management software and has the ability to integrate with CartonCloud.

### What does the integration allow?

**A CartonCloud Sale Order or Consignment creates a Consignment within GoSweetSpot**

![gosweetspot-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/gosweetspot-integration-0.png?width=581&height=176&name=gosweetspot-integration-0.png)

- A one-way integration in which a CartonCloud Sale Order or Consignment creates  a Consignment within GoSweetSpot.
- If created from a Sale Order in CartonCloud you can transfer the delivery address and items with respective weights to the Consignment record in GoSweetSpot.
- If created from a Consignment in CartonCloud you can additionally transfer required dimensions, Dangerous Goods and other relevant information to the Consignment in GoSweetSpot.

**Tracking information can be pulled from GoSweetSpot to CartonCloud**

![gosweetspot-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/gosweetspot-integration-1.png?width=670&height=67&name=gosweetspot-integration-1.png)

- A two-way integration that allows for the Courier Tracking Number and Tracking URL to be pulled from GoSweetSpot back into the CartonCloud Sale Order or Consignment.
- Tracking details can then be sent to other applications such as Shopify when marking orders as fulfilled.
- GoSweetSpot also allows Tracking Status, Shipping Cost, Residential and Rural Indicators to be pulled back into CartonCloud Consignments and Sale Orders.

**Printing GoSweetSpot Labels**

- GoSweetSpot labels can be configured to print directly from within CartonCloud.
- Printing of labels can occur automatically be selecting an order or Consignment status event such as when the order is marked as packed or by clicking a Custom Buttons . This limits the need to continually switch between applications when packing an order.

### What you need to get started

- The customer must be created in CartonCloud with products set up (product codes should match the product codes set up in GoSweetSpot).
- Your customer requires a GoSweetSpot account.
- Dangerous Good parameters will need to be set up (have a chat with our Onboarding or Business Analyst who can advise).

### Next steps to get connected

- Read the [GoSweetSpot Requirements.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/GoSweetSpot-Requirements)
- Send an integration request via a[New Ticket](https://help2.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) (with the requirements included - the more information regarding the listed requirements the better!). The team will provide you with a quote upon sending through your request.

---

<a id="gosweetspot-requirements"></a>
## GoSweetSpot Requirements

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/gosweetspot-requirements_

### Table of Contents

- Integration requirements
  - Requirements from the CartonCloud Tenant (the 3PL, owner of the CartonCloud account)
  - Requirements from the GoSweetSpot account holder

### Integration requirements

If you have decided you would like to integrate CartonCloud with GoSweetSpot, we require you to send through a integration request via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) with the below information.

**Pricing will be provided upon sending through your request.**

### Requirements from the CartonCloud Tenant (the 3PL, owner of the CartonCloud account)

- The customer the integration is for must be set up in CartonCloud.
- The warehouse or warehouses must be set up in GoSweetSpot (we will need the account id or ids).
- Will the Sale Order or Consignment in CartonCloud drive the creation of the Consignment in GoSweetSpot.
- If information such as Carrier names are sent from CartonCloud, they will need to align with those in GoSweetSpot.
- If Dangerous Goods are being used, or will soon be used, Dangerous Good parameters will need to be set up.
- Before labels are printed, do GoSweetSpot Consignments need to be pending un-manifested or manifested.
- The trigger to determine when an order is to be sent to GoSweetSpot. For example, when a Sale Order reaches the status of Packed or Dispatched, when a Consignment reaches 'In Warehouse' or when a Custom Buttons is selected.

### Requirements from the GoSweetSpot account holder

- Complete and submit a CartonCloud Integrations Request Form .
- Please confirm:
  - If only specific orders should be sent to GoSweetSpot, such as orders going to a particular state.
  - If there will be a need for overpacking.
  - If there might be Dangerous Goods.
  - If there is a need for labels and/or Consignment Notes printed from CartonCloud or if this will be done our of GoSweetSpot.
  - How much work is expected to be done in GoSweetSpot (e.g % of Consignments to be edited in GoSweetSpot - 0 - 100%).
  - If the addresses will be commercial or residential.
  - How authority to leave is to be managed (if utilised).
  - If the trigger will be on a status change or a button (or buttons for re-requesting/re-printing).
  - What information is required from GoSweetSpot back into CartonCloud.

<a id="icos-live-integration"></a>
## iCOS LIVE Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/icos-live-integration_

### Table of Contents

- What does the integration allow?
  - Pushing sale orders from CartonCloud to iCOS LIVE
  - Creating consignments automatically in CartonCloud
- How to get connected
- Price

### What does the integration allow?

CartonCloud is integrated with iCOS LIVE, allowing jobs picked in the CartonCloud WMS to automatically be transferred to iCOS live.

Additionally, when the carrier is set on a consignment in iCOS Live and that carrier uses the CartonCloud TMS, that consignment can be sent directly to the carrier's CartonCloud account.

**Pushing Sale Orders from CartonCloud to iCOS LIVE**

![icos-live-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/icos-live-integration-0.png?width=670&height=168&name=icos-live-integration-0.png)
While there are various ways the integration can be configured, the most common way is to trigger a new transport job to be created within iCOS LIVE once a Sale Order is packed within CartonCloud.

Once this is done, orders automatically appear in iCOS LIVE with the status "EDI".

Note: The integration can be configured to also trigger on a Sale Order status change, such as when a Sale Order is marked as Approved or Dispatched.

In addition, filters can be applied to control which orders are sent to iCOS LIVE. For example, you may use a [Custom Field](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Custom+Fields)within your Sale Order to track whether or not the order should be sent to iCOS.

**Creating Consignments automatically in CartonCloud**

![icos-live-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/icos-live-integration-1.png?width=670&height=168&name=icos-live-integration-1.png)
When consignments created in iCOS live are being delivered by a carrier that utilises the CartonCloud TMS, that consignment can automatically be sent to CartonCloud to be created in that carrier's account.

See it in action

Teressa from Dunedin-based [Southern Furniture Movers](http://www.southernmovers.co.nz/) explains how it works in this video:

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/rrgJnw2U1VE

### How to get connected

Connections to iCOS LIVE need to be configured by the CartonCloud team. Please [contact us](https://support.cartoncloud.com/servicedesk/customer/portal/2/create/27) to get iCOS LIVE connected.

### Price

Pricing is available on application. For more information please [contact us](https://support.cartoncloud.com/servicedesk/customer/portal/2/create/27).

---

<a id="integration-with-other-software"></a>
## Integration with other Software

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/integration-with-other-software_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How do integrations work?
- Available integrations
- Different ways in which you can integrate with CartonCloud
  - API (direct)
  - File upload
  - Zapier connections
  - Outward
  - Custom integrations/EDI

### Purpose

The ability to seamlessly integrate with other providers and platforms allows you to better meet your customer's needs and automate more of your operations. With CartonCloud, you can integrate and connect with numerous accounting software, inventory systems, shipping/dispatch systems and e-commerce platforms.

### How do Integrations work?

Software integrations allow data exchange between two different applications. Integrations can be as simple as a manual file upload to create data in an application or as complex as synchronous data sharing between two different applications.

![integration-with-other-software-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integration-with-other-software-0.png?width=670&height=235&name=integration-with-other-software-0.png)

Integrations can either be **one way** or **two way**:

**One Way**
Sending date from software A to software B.

**Example:**When a new order creates in Shopify, a new Sale Order (outbound) creates in CartonCloud for processing.

![integration-with-other-software-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integration-with-other-software-1.png?width=670&height=145&name=integration-with-other-software-1.png)

**Two Way**
When data updates in Software A, the change replicates in Software B, and when data updates in Software B, the change replicates in Software A.

**Example:**Orders in Shopify create new Sale Orders (outbound) in CartonCloud and are marked as fulfilled in Shopify once the order in CartonCloud has reached a certain status.
![integration-with-other-software-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integration-with-other-software-2.png?width=670&height=139&name=integration-with-other-software-2.png)

### Available Integrations

To see a list of currently available integrations, please click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Available-Integrations).

### Different ways in which you can integrate with CartonCloud

![integration-with-other-software-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integration-with-other-software-3.png?width=670&height=336&name=integration-with-other-software-3.png)

**API (direct)**

API (Application Programming Interface) acts as a contract between applications which defines how data can be exchanged, allowing them to connect and share data. The API creates the platform or environment in which the applications can integrate and mediates their connection. CartonCloud has a public API that enables other applications to build their own integrations into CartonCloud. This allows you and your customers to integrate your in-house software with CartonCloud.

**For information on how to use CartonCloud's API (and create an API Client), please see [API Clients](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/API-Clients)**

**For more technical and detailed information on the CartonCloud API and how to use it, please see the [API Documentation](https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/).**

For more information please lodge a case via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) to speak with the Integrations team.

**File Upload**

**Parsers**

Parsers can read data and then import the data into CartonCloud in a format the system can understand. Then, using the data, the Parser can create or update a record in CartonCloud, for example, a Sale Order or Consignment.

You can use our **standard Parser templates**, which you can access [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/List-of-Parsers) (at no extra cost), or our Integrations team can create a **custom parser** (at cost). If you wish to have a custom parser created, please reach out to the integrations team via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

If a custom parser is required (we match your customer document format), please use the below guide to send in the correct information to the Integrations team:

**My customer wants to send a spreadsheet or CSV**

![integration-with-other-software-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integration-with-other-software-4.png?width=420&height=391&name=integration-with-other-software-4.png)
**What do we need from you?**

Lodge a case via via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) with the below information:

- 3 sample files in the format that your customer will send into CartonCloud.
- What process do you need to be automated in CartonCloud? (e.g.: Purchase Order, Sale Order, Consignment)
- If not clear, an explanation of what information needs to show where in CartonClound (e.g.: Column L Titled 'Exp5' is the Expiry Date)
- If any further clarification is needed, we will reach out to you. Once clear, we will confirm the quotation, which will require approval.

**My customer wants to send a document (PDF or other) to attach to a transaction**

![integration-with-other-software-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integration-with-other-software-5.png?width=433&height=405&name=integration-with-other-software-5.png)

**What do we need from you?**

Lodge a case via via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) with the below information:

- 3 sample files in the format that your customer will send into CartonCloud.
- Would you like the document attached to a Sale Order or Consignment? (Do you want the Warehouse Floor staff to print this or the Driver/Run Manager?).
- What information on the document or in the file name is the customer reference in CartonCloud?  (we use this to match the document to transactions).
- Will the files received be multipage? (ie, More than one document per attachment)
- If any further clarification is needed, we will reach out to you. Once clear, we will confirm a quotation that will require approval.

**Zapier Connections**

[Zapier](https://zapier.com/)is a third-party integrations platform that provides a way of connecting web apps automatically. With Zapier, we can create integrations between different applications and CartonCloud. These connections are called 'Zaps' and allow seamless data sharing and automated workflows between CartonCloud and other software utilised by you and your customers.

You have the option of using your own Zapier account to create your own integrations or our Integrations team can set them up for you. For more information on creating your own Zapier integrations with our Public Zapier please see [Public Zapier Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Public-Zapier-Integrations)

Please check out our [Zapier Integration FAQ](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Zapier+Integration+FAQ) for more information.

**My customer wants to send orders from a Zapier API enabled application e.g.: Shopify, Unleashed, Xero etc**

**![integration-with-other-software-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integration-with-other-software-6.png?width=221&height=432&name=integration-with-other-software-6.png)**

**What do we need from you?**

Lodge a case via via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) with the below information:

- An indication of how orders are determined (e.g.: How do you separate orders in your system for different warehouses). A filter must always be added to ensure that the correct orders are sent to the right warehouse.
- What information on the document or file name is the customer reference in CartonCloud? (NB!! As we use this to match the document to transactions)
- Will the files received be multipage? (i.e.: More than one document per attachment)
- If any further clarification is needed, we will reach out to you. Once clear, we will confirm a quotation that will require approval.

**Outward**

CartonCloud can trigger notifications upon sale order/purchase order/consignment event milestones in CartonCloud. For example:

- When a consignment is delivered
- When a sale order is dispatched

**We/My customer wants CartonCloud to return information to their system or a third-party system.**

![integration-with-other-software-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/integration-with-other-software-7.png?width=670&height=311&name=integration-with-other-software-7.png)

**What do we need from you?**

- We will book a scoping call between the interested and affected parties (note, this is chargeable time).
- Please make available any information, such as system receiving, transmission method, file format and samples, so we can keep scoping time to a minimum.
- Once the scope has been agreed upon, we will confirm the quotation which will require approval.

**Email Notification**

CartonCloud already has a set of email notifications you can choose to enable for yourself and your customers. For more information please click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Customer-Settings-Email-Notifications).

**Custom Integrations /EDI**

If you require a custom integration that does not fit into our standard integration capabilities above, please reach out to our Integrations team via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) with the below information to investigate your requirements and document scope (paid service), after which can provide a quote and schedule for the development work. This can include proprietary systems integrations or industry-standard integrations such as EDIFACT.
For custom integrations that do not fit into any of the above categories please reach out to the team via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

---

<a id="magento-integration"></a>
## Magento Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/magento-integration_

### Table of Contents

- What does the integration allow?
  - Pulling sale orders from Magento into CartonCloud
- How to get connected

### What does the integration allow?

CartonCloud is integrated with Magento allowing orders created in Magento to automatically flow into CartonCloud as Sale Orders.

**Pulling Sale Orders from Magento into CartonCloud**

![magento-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/magento-integration-0.png?width=670&height=187&name=magento-integration-0.png)

This is a one-way integration in which a new order in Magento creates a new Sale Order within CartonCloud. It transfers the delivery address, reference, and all of the ordered items.

The integration is designed to be flexible with the option to include some additional custom fields that can be pushed through from Magento. Additionally, we can configure rules to control which orders within Magento should be transferred to CartonCloud (so not everything goes through and you have control over which are transferred).

### How to get connected

Connections to Magento need to be configured by the CartonCloud team.

This integration requires you to have:

- A Magento Account
- A Magento user for CartonCloud to use for pulling orders.

To get this setup, please contact your implementation manager or [contact us](https://support.cartoncloud.com/servicedesk/customer/portal/2/create/27).

<a id="mainfreight-freman-integration"></a>
## Mainfreight (Freman) Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/mainfreight-freman-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- What does the integration allow?
- What you need to get started
- Next steps to get connected

### Overview

Mainfreight (Freman) is a freight management system that has the ability to integrate with CartonCloud.

### What does the integration allow?

![mainfreight-freman-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/mainfreight-freman-integration-0.png?width=670&height=134&name=mainfreight-freman-integration-0.png)

- CartonCloud is able to push Consignments to Mainfreight. Please discuss the trigger options available to you with your CartonCloud integration consultant.

**What CartonCloud receive from Mainfreight**

- CartonCloud is able to receive Consignment status updates from Mainfreight.
- Mainfreight PODs can also be automatically uploaded back into CartonCloud.
- CartonCloud is able to retrieve an estimated freight cost break-down, excluding GST from Mainfreight.

![mainfreight-freman-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/mainfreight-freman-integration-1.png?width=670&height=115&name=mainfreight-freman-integration-1.png)

### What you need to get started

- You or your customer will require a Mainfreight (Freman) account.

### Next steps to get connected

- Read the integration requirements -[Mainfreight (Freman) Requirements](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/mainfreight-freman-requirements)
- Integration is file based EDI using the Mainfreight SFTP
- Send an integration request via a[New Ticket](https://help2.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) (with the requirements included - the more information regarding the listed requirements the better!). The team will provide you with a quote upon sending through your request.

---

<a id="mainfreight-freman-requirements"></a>
## Mainfreight (Freman) Requirements

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/mainfreight-freman-requirements_

### Table of Contents

- Integration requirements
  - Requirements from the CartonCloud Tenant (the 3PL, owner of the CartonCloud account)
  - Requirements from the Mainfreight (Freman) account holder

### Integration requirements

If you have decided you would like to integrate CartonCloud with Mainfreight (Freman), we require you to send through an integration request via[CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) with the below information. Pricing will be provided upon sending through your request.

### Requirements from the CartonCloud Tenant (the 3PL, owner of the CartonCloud account)

- Please enable the CartonCloud TMS Module.
- Please discuss with your CartonCloud integration consultant the options available to trigger a Consignment to Mainfreight.

### Requirements from the Mainfreight (Freman) account holder

- Complete and submit a [CartonCloud Integration Request Form.](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSepD8faSiRe009U3t0f9BHU1IBeVF-cYHTCuyHNixbtyORfpA/viewform)
- CartonCloud will need to know the below which are allocated by Mainfreight
  - Sender Id
  - MFTID
  - ProfileName(s)
  - ServiceType(s)
  - Mainfreight Carrier codes (eg MF, CC)
  - Mainfreight Service codes (eg M2H, LCL)
  - FreightTerms (eg D2D)

- And also if there is any Dangerous Goods &/or Pallet Hire requirements (Chep/Loscam).

<a id="neto-integration"></a>
## Neto Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/neto-integration_

### Table of Contents

- What does the integration allow?
  - Pulling sale orders from Neto in CartonCloud
  - Updating sale orders in Neto
- How to get connected
- Price
- Neto integration requirements
  - From the CartonCloud 3PL
  - From the Neto account holder

### What does the integration allow?

CartonCloud is integrated with Neto allowing orders created in Neto to automatically flow into CartonCloud as Sale Orders.

**Pulling Sale Orders from Neto into CartonCloud**

![neto-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/neto-integration-0.png?width=545&height=190&name=neto-integration-0.png)
This is a one-way integration in which a new order in Neto creates a new Sale Order within CartonCloud. It transfers the delivery address, reference, and all of the ordered items.

The integration is designed to be flexible with the option to include some additional custom fields that can be pushed through from Neto. Additionally, we can configure rules to control which orders within Neto should be transferred to CartonCloud (so not everything goes through and you have control over which are transferred).

**Updating Sale Orders in Neto**

![neto-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/neto-integration-1.png?width=568&height=198&name=neto-integration-1.png)
This is a two-way integration in which orders that have originated from Neto will then be marked as completed once the CartonCloud Sale Order has reached a chosen status (Packed or Dispatched).

Inventory information can also be sent back to Neto based on stock levels in CartonCloud.

Additionally, if [Shippit](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Shippit+Integration) or [StarShipit](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Starshipit+Integration) is also integrated with your CartonCloud account, then tracking numbers can also be returned to Neto.

### How to get connected

Connections to Neto need to be configured by the CartonCloud team.

To get this setup, please contact your Implementation Manager or contact us.

### Price

Pricing is available on application. For more information please [contact us](https://support.cartoncloud.com/servicedesk/customer/portal/2/create/27).

### Neto Integration Requirements

To successfully integrate CartonCloud with Neto we first require some additional information as outlined below.

**From the CartonCloud 3PL**

To integrate CartonCloud with your or your's customers Neto account we require the following to be set before we begin the build,

**One-Way Integration**

- [The Customer must be set up in CartonCloud](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+a+Customer)
- [The Customer must have some Products set up](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Products). Having this done before we complete the build allows for a smooth testing process.
- CartonCloud Product Codes must align with the customer's SKU codes in Neto. This is so the system knows which products to add on orders.
- Please confirm whether a POD should be sent to the end receiver or not (if an email address is supplied in Neto).

**From the Neto Account Holder**

To integrate your Neto account with CartonCloud, we require the following to be set before we begin the build,

**One-Way or Two-Way Integration**

- Complete and submit a [CartonCloud Integrations Request Form](https://forms.gle/E7piEToNwGLCJmmb8).
- [An API user set up](https://www.netohq.com/support/s/article/add-an-api-user-account). Once set up please supply us with the**API username and password, API Key and API URL**
- Which status an order should be in to create a Sale Order in CartonCloud (**New**, **Pick** or **Pack**)
- 3 or more orders created within Neto sitting in the status chosen above for us to use as test data during set up. These can be real or test orders for mapping purposes
- If only specific orders should be sent to the CartonCloud, such as orders going to a particular state. Please let us know these conditions with as much detail provided as possible.
- If orders will be going to addresses outside of Australia please let us know.
- An email address where we can send notifications to, in the event that an order does not make it to CartonCloud.

---

<a id="public-zapier-integrations"></a>
## Public Zapier Integrations

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/public-zapier-integrations_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- How to access CartonCloud's public Zapier
- Most common connections
- How to set up a Zapier integration with CartonCloud
- API Clients for Zapier

### Purpose

Zapier allows you to integrate other applications with CartonCloud. Using your own Zapier account and CartonCloud's Public Zapier Integration, you can connect applications straight into CartonCloud yourself.

### Prerequisites

- You will need your own Professional Zapier Account (if you are using Premium apps).
- You will need to create a CartonCloud API Client for each integration you wish to set up in Zapier (e.g. if you want to set up a Shopify integration for one customer and another Shopify integration for another customer, you would need to create two different API Clients or if you want to set up a Shopify integration and a Starshipit integration for a customer you would need to set up two different API Clients).
- Meet the integration requirements linked in the below table.
- Access your customer's connection account (e.g. full access to the customer's Shopify account).

### How to access CartonCloud's Public Zapier

You can access CartonCloud's Public Zapier [here](https://zapier.com/apps/cartoncloud/integrations).

### Most common connections

Please note, these are just the most common ones we see users building. You can use Zapier to easily build an integration between CartonCloud and thousands of other applications.

| **Connection** | **Link to template** | **Requirements to set up the integration** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Xero pushing Purchase Orders into CartonCloud | [Template in Zapier](https://workflows.zapier.com/?attempt_id=0307c199-4e81-4fdf-85a8-8c133ccd6675&template=857867) | [Xero Integration Requirements](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Xero-Integration) |
| Starshipit pushing Sale Orders into CartonCloud | [Template in Zapier](https://workflows.zapier.com/?attempt_id=87823599-665f-4c44-9ff2-dae65b68559f&template=841677) | [Starshipit Integration Requirements](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Starshipit-Integration) |
| Xero pushing Sale Orders into CartonCloud | [Template in Zapier](https://workflows.zapier.com/?attempt_id=99eaf49d-481a-4124-bb76-2043b2b85d99&template=70199) | [Xero Integration Requirements](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Xero-Integration) |
| Shopify pushing Sale Orders into CartonCloud | [Template in Zapier](https://workflows.zapier.com/?attempt_id=5ff955f1-56d4-4508-9ec6-7aadb7d190d1&template=841627) | [Shopify Integration Requirements](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Shopify-Integration) |

For applications not mentioned above, please see the [Available Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Available-Integrations) section of the Knowledge Base to check the integration requirements for the specific application.

### How to set up a Zapier Integration with CartonCloud

**Note, this is only applicable to one-way integrations into CartonCloud.**

- Navigate to the CartonCloud Public Zapier (through your Zapier account login).
- Select one of our Templates or search for an app to connect to.

![public-zapier-integrations-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/public-zapier-integrations-0.png?width=670&height=342&name=public-zapier-integrations-0.png)

![public-zapier-integrations-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/public-zapier-integrations-1.png?width=670&height=342&name=public-zapier-integrations-1.png)

- Once you have selected an application or template, Zapier will guide you through the steps to set up the connection.

![public-zapier-integrations-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/public-zapier-integrations-2.png?width=670&height=304&name=public-zapier-integrations-2.png)

![public-zapier-integrations-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/public-zapier-integrations-3.png?width=670&height=342&name=public-zapier-integrations-3.png)

- Most of the information will be pre-filled if you are using a template.
- When you get to the ' Connect to CartonCloud ' step, you need to have the API Clients Credentials (the Client ID and the Client Secret). Please see the API Clients section of this article for more information.

### API Clients for Zapier

To create a Zapier connection with CartonCloud, you require an API Client (created in CartonCloud). Each Zapier integration you create requires its own API Client. For example, if you are creating a Shopify connection for one customer and a Starshipit and Shopify integration for another customer, you would need three different API Clients.

Once you have created the API Client, you will need to use the credentials to connect your CartonCloud account.

**Connecting CartonCloud in Zapier:**

![public-zapier-integrations-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/public-zapier-integrations-4.png?width=571&height=377&name=public-zapier-integrations-4.png)

**CartonCloud API Client credetials:**

![public-zapier-integrations-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/public-zapier-integrations-5.png?width=544&height=208&name=public-zapier-integrations-5.png)
**How to create an API Client in CartonCloud**

When creating the API Client in CartonCloud, it is recommended that you name the Client something that is easily associated with the Zapier connection. For example, if you create a Shopify integration for Coastal Coffee Company, you would call the API Client 'Shopify Zapier Coastal Coffee Company'.
You can find steps on how to create an API Client [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/API-Clients).

**Credentials for the API Client**

When creating the Zapier integration and connecting your CartonCloud account, you must provide the appropriate API Client Credentials. Upon creating the API Client, you are provided with the Credentials; however, if you were to misplace the Credentials, you can follow the below steps to generate the Credentials again.

<a id="route-optimisation-software-integration"></a>
## Route Optimisation Software Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/route-optimisation-software-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How it works
- Exporting data from bulk allocations
- Import updates
- Setting up an import update parser
  - Uploading the file
  - Successful import
  - Unsuccessful import
  - Email notifications

### Purpose

From the bulk allocation page, it is possible to export data in a chosen format that can then be imported into route optimisation software such as MarketMotion.

This is ideal for operations who use CartonCloud as their TMS but want to use other software for route optimisation.

If you are interested in setting this integration up. Please contact our [Integrations team](https://support.cartoncloud.com/servicedesk/customer/portal/2/create/27).

### How it Works

CartonCloud exports the data of the consignments you wish to optimise in third party software. This data will be formatted to be compatible with the software.

The file exported from CartonCloud is then imported into the route optimisation software which calculates the best order for your deliveries. This data including the order of deliveries is saved in an updated file.

CartonCloud imports the updated file the order of deliveries, along with other allocation information such as the driver and run sheet is updated within the system.

Deliveries will now take place using CartonCloud in the order that was determined by your route optimisation software.

![route-optimisation-software-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/route-optimisation-software-integration-0.png?width=670&height=297&name=route-optimisation-software-integration-0.png)

### Exporting data from Bulk Allocations

Once our integrations team has configured your account to export data in the required format for the optimisation software you are using the following steps can be taken to export data.

- Navigate to the Bulk Allocations page by selecting **Transport** in the main menu, then **Bulk Allocations** in the drop-down menu.
- Select the consignments you wish to export data on. Then select**Export Selected to CSV**

![route-optimisation-software-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/route-optimisation-software-integration-1.png?width=670&height=417&name=route-optimisation-software-integration-1.png)

- A box will appear allowing you to select the format you wish to export the data in. This will be named as the Route optimisation software you use and will only appear after you have consulted with our integrations team.

![route-optimisation-software-integration-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/route-optimisation-software-integration-2.png?width=566&height=272&name=route-optimisation-software-integration-2.png)

- Select Export and the consignment data will be exported to the desired format, ready to be imported back into your route optimisation software.

### ​​​​​​​Import Updates

The import updates button allows you to parse in a file containing the order deliveries should take place and automatically allocate consignments to the appropriate run sheets and drivers as specified.

This button will only appear on your bulk allocation page if you already have a

parser

of the "Consignment Allocation" class set up.

### Setting up an Import Update Parser

Parsers must be set up to read in the format of the file sent from the specific route optimisation software you are using. Therefore if you wish to have one set up please contact our [integrations team](https://support.cartoncloud.com/servicedesk/customer/portal/2/create/27).

Once the Parser has been set up the button to import updates will appear as shown below.

![route-optimisation-software-integration-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/route-optimisation-software-integration-3.png?width=670&height=363&name=route-optimisation-software-integration-3.png)

Selecting this button will open a box as shown below.

![route-optimisation-software-integration-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/route-optimisation-software-integration-4.png?width=564&height=350&name=route-optimisation-software-integration-4.png)
If you only have one Parser type set up then it will automatically populate the dropdown menu. However, if you have multiple parsers set up you should select the appropriate one from the drop-down menu.

Once ready, you should then select **Choose File** to select the CSV file template containing the update information that you wish to process.

CSV file templates may look slightly different based on the optimisation software you are pulling data from. In the generic example below some of the key fields and the corresponding logic is explained.

**Import Update Fields**

![route-optimisation-software-integration-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/route-optimisation-software-integration-5.png?width=670&height=104&name=route-optimisation-software-integration-5.png)

| **Field** | **Details** |
| --- | --- |
| Consignment ID (required) | A consignment ID **MUST** be provided for the import to be successful. This means that all consignments must already be created before attempting to import updates for them.   Failing a single consignment ID will result in the entire import failing. |
| Run Sheet name **(required)** | You **MUST** provide a run sheet name in the template file.   If you provide a Run sheet name in the template a new run sheet with that name will be created in the system.   That is unless a run sheet with an identical name already exists for the same date.   If a run sheet name is not provided the import will fail and an error message will appear explaining why. |
| Driver Name | If a valid driver name is provided in this field then the file import will automatically allocate the corresponding consignment ID to that driver.   Supplying a non-valid driver name will result in the import failing and an error message will be displayed. |
| Run Sheet Date | If a run sheet date is provided it will be used to set the date of the run sheet being created.   If a run sheet date is not provided then the system will check the [Delivery Run schedule](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Delivery+Schedules+for+Addresses%2C+Delivery+Zones%2C+Delivery+Runs) and attempt to determine a run sheet date.   If no date is provided and a run sheet date cannot be determined from the [Delivery Run schedule](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Delivery+Schedules+for+Addresses%2C+Delivery+Zones%2C+Delivery+Runs) then the import will fail and an error message will appear explaining why. |
| Vehicle Name | If a valid vehicle name is provided the consignment will be allocated to that vehicle   A non-valid vehicle name will cause the import to fail and an error message will appear explaining why. |
| Sort Order | This will be determined by the third party route optimisation software you are using. In order for CartonCloud to accept the value given it must be a numeric value.    In the case where the third party software does not output a numeric value for the order consignments should be delivered in a run then we can manipulate the data given to turn it into a numeric field.   The sort order determined what order consignments should be delivered on a run sheet. For example in the example file on the Gold Coast AM Run: Consignment 1152 (sort order 1), then Consignment 1154 (sort order 2), then Consignment 1151 (sort order 3). |
| Arrive Time | This field is not required and will only appear if requested. This is just one example of the many scenarios that can be set up using [custom fields](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Custom+Fields). If you have other fields that need to be updated from your route optimisation software these can be accommodated. |
| Depart Time | See above. |

**Uploading the file**

Once the file with the appropriate data is ready click **Choose File** then select the file you wish to upload.

![route-optimisation-software-integration-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/route-optimisation-software-integration-6.png?width=596&height=365&name=route-optimisation-software-integration-6.png)
Once selected, click **Import**.

The results of the import will then be displayed.

**Successful Import**

On a successful import, the results of the import will be displayed, showing which consignment ID was allocated and any corresponding details.

![route-optimisation-software-integration-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/route-optimisation-software-integration-7.png?width=670&height=246&name=route-optimisation-software-integration-7.png)
**Unsuccessful Import**

On an unsuccessful import attempt, error messages will be displayed to explain what went wrong. In the example below a consignment ID was missing from the file, causing the entire import to fail.

This will need to be fixed by supplying a consignment ID of the consignment to be allocated then reuploading the file.

![route-optimisation-software-integration-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/route-optimisation-software-integration-8.png?width=670&height=115&name=route-optimisation-software-integration-8.png)

**Email Notifications**

Please note using this function will not trigger any email notifications.

---

<a id="sap-integration"></a>
## SAP Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/sap-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- What does the integration allow?
- What you need to get started
- Next steps to get connected

### Overview

SAP has various products including SAP ERP (formally R3), SAP Business One (SAP B1) and SAP S/4 HANA and each product depending available functionality and the business requirements can integrate with CartonCloud. This article focuses on XML iDocs. Enterprises that have a preference for / pre-existing Edifact and/or ANSI X1 2 messaging in place via a message broker / middleware can also be supported.

### What does the integration allow?

SAP is generally considered one of the most comprehensive Enterprise Resource Management Systems and therefore supports a comprehensive suite of functions and messaging relating to warehousing and distribution activities. These workflows include:

![sap-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sap-integration-0.png?width=400&height=200&name=sap-integration-0.png)

- Purchase Order, ASN, Stock Transfer, Returns in SAP creates a new Purchase Order in CartonCloud
- Sale Order, Packing Instructions, Deliveries, Shipments in SAP create a Sale Order in CartonCloud

![sap-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sap-integration-1.png?width=400&height=200&name=sap-integration-1.png)

- A Purchase Order confirmation in CartonCloud sends a goods receipt confirmation to SAP
- Sale Order pick confirmation in CartonCloud sends a Goods Issue Confirmation to SAP
- Product status change in CartonCloud creates an inventory status change in SAP
- Stock adjustment in CartonCloud creates a Warehouse Inventory Adjustment in SAP
- Stock on Hand Report in CartonCloud creates a Inventory Discrepancy Report in SAP

### What you need to get started

- The customer must be created in CartonCloud
- Your customer requires a SAP account. Generally enterprises using SAP will have an in house SAP specialist or third party SAP consultant to help set up the integration.
- SAP version (SAP ERP, SAP B1, SAP S/4 HANA)
- Message Framework (iDoc (xml), Edifact, X12, Custom xml, csv)

### Next steps to get connected

- Read the [SAP Requirements](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/SAP-Requirements)
- [/articles/Knowledge/SAP-Requirements](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/SAP-Requirements)Send an integration request via a[New Ticket](https://help2.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) (with the requirements included - the more information regarding the listed requirements the better!). The team will provide you with a quote upon sending through your request.[https://app.slack.com/team/USLACKBOT](https://app.slack.com/team/USLACKBOT)

---

<a id="sap-requirements"></a>
## SAP Requirements

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/sap-requirements_

### Table of Contents

- Integration requirements
  - Requirements from the CartonCloud Tenant (the 3PL, owner of the CartonCloud account)
  - Requirements from the SAP account holder

### Integration requirements

If you have decided you would like to integrate CartonCloud with SAP, we require you to send through a integration request via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) with the below information and one of our Integration Consultants will be in contact to arrange a scoping meeting.

Depending on complexity and availability of all parties, SAP integration projects can take between 2 - 5 months including scoping, analysis and mapping documentation, configuration and build, systems integration testing (SIT), user acceptance testing, Go-Live migration and support.

**Pricing will be provided upon sending through your request and after the initial scoping call.**

### Requirements from the CartonCloud Tenant (the 3PL, owner of the CartonCloud account)

- The customer the integration is for must be set up in CartonCloud
- Product attributes (Dangerous Goods, Temperate Controlled, Foodstuff, Fragile/sensitive, Apparel)
- Product tracking requirements (Batch, Lot, Manufacture, Expiry Date, Serial Numbers)
- Known / current workflows (Receiving, Picking, Returns, Re-works, Kitting, Damages)

### Requirements from the SAP account holder

- Complete and submit a CartonCloud Integrations Request Form .
- SAP version (SAP, ERP, SAP B1, SAP S/4 HANA)
- Message framework (iDoc (xml), Edifact, X12, Custom xml, csv)
- Specifications for messages
- Sample files
- Contact details for the customer's in-house / SAP partner specialist (name, email)

<a id="setting-up-shopify-stock-sync-by-email-or-ftp"></a>
## Setting up Shopify Stock Sync by FTP

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-shopify-stock-sync-by-email-or-ftp_

### Table of Contents

- StockSync
- Prerequisites
- Generic guide on how to set up StockSync file feed
  - Step 1 - Feed Manager
  - Step 2 - Matching Column
  - Step 3 - Filter
  - Step 4 - Advanced Settings
  - Step 5 - Turning on StockSync

### StockSync

The StockSync plugin for Shopify allows CartonCloud to send the onhand quantity from CartonCloud to Shopify to update Shopify inventory information.

This is useful if you require stock on hand in CartonCloud to update Shopify inventory.

The Shopify store owner is responsible for configuring the StockSync settings.

### Prerequisites

- Before setting up Stock Sync by FTP you must first ensure you have installed and paid for Shopify StockSync plugin.

### Generic guide on how to set up StockSync File Feed

- Log into your Shopify account.
- Using the top search bar, select Apps and then type in StockSync .
- Select StockSync .

![setting-up-shopify-stock-sync-by-email-or-ftp-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-shopify-stock-sync-by-email-or-ftp-0.png?width=670&height=95&name=setting-up-shopify-stock-sync-by-email-or-ftp-0.png)

- On the StockSync page, select +Setup New feed . Or if you have not created a feed before select +Create New.

![setting-up-shopify-stock-sync-by-email-or-ftp-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-shopify-stock-sync-by-email-or-ftp-1.png?width=670&height=163&name=setting-up-shopify-stock-sync-by-email-or-ftp-1.png)

- On the Create New Feed screen, from the Choose an action on how to import products from supplier drop down select Update - Existing products .
- On the Confirm to proceed prompt, select Yes .
- Edit the title Update Profile X to CartonCloud StockSync .
- Select the Connections menu and then FTP .
- On the Confirm to proceed prompt, select Yes .
- Edit the title Update FTP - X to CartonCloud StockSync .
- Update the fields specified as below:

- Step 1 - Feed Manager
  - FTP
    - Add username (provided by the CartonCloud Integrations team).
    - Add password (provided by the CartonCloud Integrations team).
    - Add Host: ftp.cartoncloud.com.
    - Add Directory and File name (only add the filename provided by the CartonCloud Integrations team).
    - For After Process - Select Delete My File .
    - Select Test Connection .
    - If everything is correctly set, this response should appear - Connection Successful .
  - File Setting
    - File Format : select CSV .
    - Column Separator : select the comma ,
    - File Encoding : select Auto .
    - First Row is Header : select Yes .
    - Skip feed rows : leave blank.
- Select Next .

- Step 2 - Matching Column
  - Note: if drop down values do not appear, zoom out to 30 - 50%.
  - Product Identifier :
    - Store field : select the field you utilised, most of the time this is SKU (Variant's SKU). In the box underneath the Store field, remove any value that may be here and select ProductCode .
    - Select the settings cog to see if any additional product identifier settings are required.
  - Store Product Fields :
    - Store field : select Availably Quantity. In the box under Store field, select AvailableQuantity .
    - Select the settings cog to see if any additional product identifier settings are required.

-
  - If you have multiple Locations (Location IDs) in your Shopify Store :
    - Navigate back to Shopify, select Settings > Locations and view the number of locations.
    - Under the Store Product Field(s), select the settings cog.
    - Select the Inventory Location for the warehouse
    - See here to check if any additional settings need to be configured for your store and workflow setup.
    - Note, if you believe Product Options (Variations), or Metafield are required to be able to sufficiently identify products, please contact the CartonCloud Integrations team here .

-
  - Select Next . The response, CartonCloud StockSync settings updated , should appear.

- Step 3 - Filter
  - Products can be filtered if you do not wish the StockSync process to update certain inventory values. You can leave the Store Product - Store Field Name as “Published” and leave the default value of “Any”. You can apply any rules to Store Products, or to data in the Incoming Feed.
  - The below settings can be configured to suit the setup you require:
    - Ignore variants with "Track inventory"
    - Ignore variants with zero quantity
    - Ignore variants with quantity

-
  - Select Next . The response, CartonCloud StockSync settings updated , should appear.

- Step 4 - Advanced Settings
  - Auto Publish/Unpublish:
    - Auto publish/ unpublish: can be left as Do not apply .
    - Auto archive products: can be left as Do not apply .
  - Out of Stock Strategy:
    - Note, the below settings have significant impact on your Shopify store set up and integration. Please ensure you follow the Download Export Product advice prior to turning on either of the below settings. It is also highly recommended that you read the following articles - [Out of Stock Strategy (OOS)](https://help.stock-sync.com/en/article/out-of-stock-strategy-oos-m5qjng/) and [Store Product Filter](https://help.stock-sync.com/en/article/store-product-filter-1uqbxfq/).
    - Set out of stock to ZERO quantity: can be turned on with care if the above articles are read, however, this setting is generally not turned on (note, it is highly recommended that the above articles are read before enabling this setting) .
    - Select Finish .

If any of the generic settings above do not meet your requirements, please read the article -[Setting up the feed with Stock Sync](https://support.stock-sync.com/support/solutions/44000814776). If a pop up window appears prompting you with links to articles, it is highly recommended that you read the articles.

- Step 5 - Turning on the StockSync
  - From the Dashboard, select the desired Feed Name to turn on.
  - If the Feed Name reads 'FTP - 1' change this to 'CartonCloud Sync'.
  - Select Turn on under the Schedule.
  - On the Feed Detail screen, select Preview Sync .
  - The Processing screen will appear until the preview is available.
  - Select Feed Details, select Activity Logs List .
    - Select the Details link > select the Change Logs > and click Not in Store links to download the test results.
    - Refresh the screen until you receive a file. If the file does not appear, it may be empty. This would indicate the SKUs in CartonCloud have not been identified via StockSync in Shopify, so an update to resolves this would be needed.
    - Explore the file to confirm:
      - The Before Qty (what is in Shopify) and
      - The After Qty (what will be updated from CartonCloud)
    - And confirm this is the desired outcome for Products and Variants (if applicable).
  - To set a schedule, first check what time zone your Shopify is in and what time zone CartonCloud are using in scheduling file creation.
  - The default time zone should be aligned with the Warehouse time zone.
  - Select Turn on here or Start Process .
  - On the Automate this feed screen , slide the Schedule is enabled toggle to turn it on.
  - Se the Schedule Frequency to Daily .
  - Update the Schedule Time to 11:50 .
  - Select Ok .
  - The Dashboard will now show an active Stock Feed with a frequency and time in the schedule.
  - Monitor to see Inventory On Hand Quantities in CartonCloud are reflected in Shopify as expected.

---

<a id="shippit-integration"></a>
## Shippit Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/shippit-integration_

### Table of Contents[#what-does-the-integration-allow](https://help.cartoncloud.com#what-does-the-integration-allow)

- Overview
- What does the integration allow?
- What you need to get connected
- Next steps to get connected

### Overview

Shippit is a multi-carrier shipping software that has the ability to integrate with CartonCloud.

### What does the integration allow?

**CartonCloud Sale Order creates a shipment within Shippit.**

![shippit-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/shippit-integration-0.png?width=400&height=200&name=shippit-integration-0.png)

- Transfers the delivery address and Sale Order items with the respective weights.
- Custom fields can be mapped to fields within Shippit.
- Choose if the shipment in Shippit is created once the Sale Order is packed or dispatched in CartonCloud.
- Confirm the packaging to match with your preferred carrier and generate the labels from within Shippit.

**Pull tracking information from Shippit to CartonCloud**

![shippit-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/shippit-integration-1.png?width=400&height=200&name=shippit-integration-1.png)

- The Shippit tracking ID or courier tracking number can be pulled from Shippit back into the CartonCloud Sale Order.
- These tracking details can then be sent to other applications such as Shopify when marking orders as fulfilled.

**Printing shipping labels**

![shippit-integration-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/shippit-integration-2.png?width=614&height=307&name=shippit-integration-2.png)

- By default, labels can be printed directly from within the Shippit application or you can choose to configure to print labels directly from within CartonCloud.
- Printing can occur automatically by selecting an order status event such as when an order is marked or packed or by clicking a custom button.
- This is useful as it eliminates the need to continually switch between platforms.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/AHALxanwNdU

### What you need to get connected

- Your customer requires a Shippit account.

### Next steps to get connected

- Read the integration requirements - Shippit Requirements
- Send an integration request via a New Ticket (with the requirements included - the more information regarding the listed requirements the better!). The team will provide you with a quote upon sending through your request.

---

<a id="shippit-requirements"></a>
## Shippit Requirements

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/shippit-requirements_

### Table of Contents

- Integration Requirements
  - Requirements from the CartonCloud Tenant (the 3PL, owner of the CartonCloud account)
  - Requirements from the Shippit account holder

### Integration Requirements

If you have decided you would like to integrate CartonCloud with Shippit, we require you to send through an integration request via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) with the below information. Pricing will be provided upon sending through your request.

### Requirements from the CartonCloud Tenant (the 3PL, owner of the CartonCloud account)

- The trigger you would like to set that will determine when an order is sent to Shippit. For example, when a Sale Order reaches the status of Packed or Dispatched.
- If only specific orders should be sent to Shippit, such as orders going to a particular state.

### Requirements from the Shippit account holder

- Complete and submit a CartonCloud Integration Request Form .
- Your Shippit API Key.
- If only specific orders should be sent to Shippit, such as orders going to a particular state.
- Confirm if you would like the Shippit tracking ID or the Courier Tracking Number sent back to CartonCloud.
- Please note if you wish for the Courier Tracking Number to be returned this must be checked using a scheduled processor. When this API call to obtain tracking details occurs Shippit will automatically update the shipment to 'Ready to Ship'. We therefore, recommend only checking for tracking details at chosen times when you know shipments will already be processed.

## ShipStation Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/shipstation-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- What does the integration allow?
- What you need to get started
- Next steps to get connected

### Overview

ShipStation is a shipping and fulfilment platform that has the ability to integrate with CartonCloud.

### What does the integration allow?

**ShipStation to CartonCloud (Sale Order creation)**

**![shipstation-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/shipstation-integration-0.png?width=400&height=200&name=shipstation-integration-0.png)**

- A new order in ShipStation creates a new Sale Order in CartonCloud.
- Delivery address, sale order items, weight, custom fields (if applicable) from CartonCloud can be transferred to the shipment in ShipStation.
- Select the Sale Order status in CartonCloud to trigger the creation of the shipment in ShipStation, for example packed or dispatched.
- Confirm packaging matches your preferred carrier and generate labels from within ShipStation.

**Confirm tracking from ShipStation to CartonCloud**

![shipstation-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/shipstation-integration-1.png?width=400&height=200&name=shipstation-integration-1.png)

- Tracking number from the shipment in ShipStation can be updated on the respective order in CartonCloud.
- The tracking number can be sent to other applications such as Shopify, when marking orders as fulfilled.

**Print ShipStation labels directly from within CartonCloud**

- ShipStation labels can be printed directly from within CartonCloud.

### What you need to get started

- A ShipStation account owned by the Tenant or Customer.
- Your ShipStation API Key and API Secret. This is unique to your company's ShipStation account and can be found inside of the ShipStation application under Settings > API Settings.
- If the Tenant's account, we need to know the child account name.

### Next steps to get connected

- Read the Integration Requirements - ShipStation Requirements
- Send an integration request via a New Ticket (with the requirements included - the more information regarding the listed requirements the better!). The team will provide you with a quote upon sending through your request.

<a id="shopify-integration-troubleshooting"></a>
## Shopify Integration Troubleshooting

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/shopify-integration-troubleshooting_

### Table of Contents

- [Issue](https://help.cartoncloud.com#issue)
- [What causes a Shopify order to fail and not be marked as fulfilled](https://help.cartoncloud.com#what-causes-a-shopify-order-to-fail-and-not-be-marked-as-fulfilled)
- [Resolution](https://help.cartoncloud.com#resolution) ​​​​​​​

### Issue

Order in Shopify has not been marked as fulfilled even if the Sale Order has been packed or dispatched from CartonCloud.

### What causes a Shopify order to fail and not be marked as fulfilled

CartonCloud is able to mark a Shopify order as fulfilled once it has been packed or dispatched in CartonCloud. When the order is created in Shopify and is sent to CartonCloud via API, a unique reference number is captured for each individual line of product on a Sale Order. This unique reference number needs to be sent back to Shopify (once the CartonCloud Sale Order is packed or dispatched) in order to fulfill the order in Shopify.

A Shopify order fulfilment will fail if the unique reference number against each product line is not sent back to Shopify correctly. This can occur if:

- You manually enter the order or parse through the order
- If you delete product lines from an order
- If an order is originally rejected (for example, due to not enough stock). Even if you are able to reprocess the order, the order will not be able to be fulfilled in Shopify.
- The product on an order is changed (removed and a new product added)
- The product code on an order is changed (the same product on the order but the code on the product in CartonCloud had been updated)
- The quantity of a product line has either increased or decreased

### Resolution

If the order has not been fulfilled in Shopify due to the above mentioned reasons you will need to manually go into Shopify and fulfill the order.

---
