<a id="transvirtual-integration"></a>
## Transvirtual Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/transvirtual-integration_

### Table of Contents

- What does the integration allow?
  - Pushing sale orders or consignments from CartonCloud to Transvirtual
    - How to get connected
  - Pushing proof of delivery (POD) from Transvirtual to CartonCloud consignments
    - How to get connected

### What does the integration allow?

CartonCloud is integrated with Transvirtual allowing jobs picked in the CartonCloud WMS to be automatically transferred into the Transvirtual transport management system.

**Pushing Sale Orders or Consignments from CartonCloud to Transvirtual**

![transvirtual-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/transvirtual-integration-0.png?width=670&height=176&name=transvirtual-integration-0.png)
While there are various ways the integration can be configured, the most common way is to trigger a new transport job to be created within Transvirtual once a Sale Order is packed within CartonCloud.

Once this is done, orders automatically appear in Transvirtual with the status "EDI".

(Note: you can configure it to create the job on Sale Order approval or other statuses too).

In addition, rules can be created to control which orders are sent to Transvirtual. For example, you may use a [Custom Field](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Custom+Fields)within your Sale Order to track whether or not the order should be sent to Transvirtual.

**How to get connected**

Connections to Transvirtual need to be configured by the CartonCloud team. Please contact us to get Transvirtual connected.

**Pushing Proof Of Delivery(POD) from Transvirtual to CartonCloud Consignments**

![transvirtual-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/transvirtual-integration-1.png?width=670&height=176&name=transvirtual-integration-1.png)
This integration is available for CartonCloud Consignments; on completion of a delivery in Transvirtual the POD is attached to the CartonCloud consignment and the consignment is marked delivered.

- This POD can then be automatically forwarded to your customer. See how to located [Customer Email Address Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Customer+Email+Address+Settings)

**How to get connected**

Connections to Transvirtual need to be configured by the CartonCloud team. Please contact us to get Transvirtual connected.

---

<a id="workwave-integration-for-allocating"></a>
## Workwave Integration for Allocating

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/workwave-integration-for-allocating_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- CartonCloud configuration to enable
  - Product type
  - Capacity
  - Custom fields setup to match workwave & using
- How to send to Workwave
- How to retrieve from Workwave
- Important steps / troubleshooting

### Overview

Workwave Integration is a paid feature that requires configuration to set up, for more information please use CartonCloud Help to lodge a case with our support team.

Information related to the Workwave Integration for Push/Pull allocating between CartonCloud and Workwave.

CartonCloud can use Workwave's allocation tools to create Run Sheets within CartonCloud.

CartonCloud as used as the source of consignments, then instead of allocating to drivers within in CartonCloud, pushing (all or selected) consignments to Workwave, using the tools there to allocate and produce Run Sheets in order of deliveries for the drivers. This ordering and allocation are pulled back into CartonCloud producing Runsheets with Drivers already allocated in the exact delivery ordering from Workwave for the consignments.

From there the drivers will have these deliveries on their CartonCloud App ready to deliver and record the PODs.

The integration with Workwave **supports time slots** to be used for allocation purpose, so that start and end of a timeslot can be assigned permanently to addresses or, assigning timeslots specifically to a consignment (which overrides address). This ensures timeslots are adhered to in the allocation process.

Workwave can be used to manually create allocations one by one using the map view, or by putting all consignments into Workwave and using its rules/setup to produce runs for drivers dynamically, i.e. using the capacity of the vehicle and timing of deliveries to create an optimum number of runs and drivers needed to deliver those consignments (auto-creating allocations variable to the consignments). Or a combination of both.

There are two main components within the integration:

- Pushing Consignments to Workwave (from Bulk Allocation screen).
- Pulling approved routes from Workwave (from Bulk Allocation screen).

### CartonCloud configuration to enable

Workwave integration is a paid feature, for details on pricing and information related to implementing this please contact the Service Desk by lodging a case at

CartonCloud Help

.

Turn on Workwave in

Organisation Settings

:

![workwave-integration-for-allocating-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/workwave-integration-for-allocating-0.png?width=670&height=447&name=workwave-integration-for-allocating-0.png)
This then brings up 2 additional fields - the API Key and Territory mappings. The territory mapping is the operation area in Workwave and typically you are linking a matching territory for the CartonCloud warehouse. This is the territory code from Workwave and the warehouse ID from CartonCloud. Both of these are found from Workwave itself, consult Workwave help on where to find. Enter the Key in and enter the Territory mappings in then hit save. Workwave will now be active.

An example of what the mappings should look like when populated, use as many territory links as needed:

![workwave-integration-for-allocating-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/workwave-integration-for-allocating-1.png?width=447&height=209&name=workwave-integration-for-allocating-1.png)

**Product Type**

Workwave has fields called Tags (Required), these match with CartonCloud [Product Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Product+Types), so configure the names to match for Workwave to successfully sync those fields. e.g. Chilled product type will match a Chilled Required Tag in workwave to segregate vehicles by what they accept etc.

**Capacity**

Workwave has fields in its Vehicles configuration which limits how much a vehicle can carry, these fields can be anything and match the CartonCloud consignment custom fields e.g. Pallet and Carton fields of a consignment. Simply configure both CartonCloud and Workwave names to match for them to sync when passing data back and forth. e.g. Pallet in CartonCloud should match Pallet capacity field in the vehicle setup for Workwave for everything to match. Common examples and use are Pallets, Cartons, Weight and Cubic to allow capacity to work well, either all or 1 or combinations can be utilised.

**Custom Fields Setup to match Workwave & Using**

Custom Fields are required to be configured in CartonCloud to support the integration with Workwave, these fields support the API link, and also allow the use of Service Time for address delivery length and Time Windows for delivery timeslots. 2 different timeslots can be configured per address and 1 overriding timeslot per consignment. The idea is that addresses where needed generally have permanent timeslots if they are not available to be delivered to all day during normal business hours. So by configuring timeslots against the address, these can be used to ensure when Workwave is used for allocation building, the timeslots are factored in and adhered to for the drivers to meet during their delivery schedule.

Navigate to Custom Fields using the Search for anything! box.

Configure in the Address section the 5 fields exactly as per below example, this is important to allow the integration to function correctly:
![workwave-integration-for-allocating-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/workwave-integration-for-allocating-2.png?width=670&height=190&name=workwave-integration-for-allocating-2.png)

Then configure the Consignment Data section 3 fields exactly as shown:

![workwave-integration-for-allocating-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/workwave-integration-for-allocating-3.png?width=670&height=225&name=workwave-integration-for-allocating-3.png)
![workwave-integration-for-allocating-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/workwave-integration-for-allocating-4.png?width=670&height=422&name=workwave-integration-for-allocating-4.png)

The address custom fields can be used by editing the [Addresses & Address Strings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/createpage.action?spaceKey=KB2&title=Addresses+%26+Address+Strings&linkCreation=true&fromPageId=532546184), populating a Service Time in minutes and the other fields by time start and end. Here is an example of what an address can look like. These fields are optional so populate or don't populate as you desire.
![workwave-integration-for-allocating-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/workwave-integration-for-allocating-5.png?width=261&height=328&name=workwave-integration-for-allocating-5.png)

The consignment custom fields again are optional, with time windows that if populated override the address time windows. Note the below warning.

**Important Note: Sent to Workwave is a field auto-populated by the system and is used to analyse whether consignments have been sent already or not. Do not use adjust manually unless you have advanced knowledge and need to.**

### How to send to Workwave

Navigate to [Bulk Allocation](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Bulk+Allocation) and using the selection tools there, either select all undelivered consignments requiring allocation or make a custom selection of consignments you would like to allocate in Workwave. Once selected, the use the Send to Workwave button highlighted below to send them to Workwave. If there are any issues an error message will appear, or potentially they may be missing in Workwave, always check you have a matching number of consignments in Workwave as there are in CartonCloud to send.
![workwave-integration-for-allocating-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/workwave-integration-for-allocating-6.png?width=608&height=346&name=workwave-integration-for-allocating-6.png)

If using type Delivery + Pickup, if 1 or both of the parts are selected, then both Pickup And Delivery consignments will be sent to Workwave for allocation.

A popup will appear with a count of selected Consignments. Clicking the **Send To WorkWave** button in the popup will push the data to WorkWave.

Once the push to WorkWave is complete a success message will show

### How to retrieve from Workwave

Once allocations complete in Workwave, mark the Routes that are finished as Approved Routes in Workwave, then CartonCloud will be able to pull those. It's important the routes are marked as Approved as CartonCloud will not pull any unapproved routes from Workwave, this is to allow pulling only finished allocations.

Navigate to [Bulk Allocation](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Bulk+Allocation) and use the Pull Approved Routes From Workwave button to load the consignments in Workwave back into CartonCloud. Nothing else is needed to be selected on the page, just use the button straight away. The typical use for this is to be used after sending to Workwave, allocating in Workwave, then using the Pull button to copy the allocations from Workwave into CartonCloud as the final step.

Once selected it will ask for the date you would like to retrieve from Workwave for → this is the date that consignments are loaded against in Workwave (i.e. this can be in advance, e.g. tomorrow's date). Click the choose date box:

![workwave-integration-for-allocating-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/workwave-integration-for-allocating-7.png?width=670&height=163&name=workwave-integration-for-allocating-7.png)
Select date from the calendar then uses the Pull Approved Routes button to pull the Routes from Workwave into CartonCloud.

![workwave-integration-for-allocating-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/workwave-integration-for-allocating-8.png?width=670&height=218&name=workwave-integration-for-allocating-8.png)
Then you will get a screen which shows how many routes were pulled back, how many Run Sheets were created if there were any fails. It will also show Errors like this example, which indicates a configuration error as no Workwave link is configured here. The other common Error is that there are no approved routes in Workwave for the date requested, either because they're on a different date or they are unapproved. This often happens because Workwave won't approve a Route if it has allocation issues.

![workwave-integration-for-allocating-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/workwave-integration-for-allocating-9.png?width=670&height=231&name=workwave-integration-for-allocating-9.png)
When the Pull process is complete you should have Runsheets (Transport menu→ Runsheets) matching your Workwave routes, with the consignments in the same order as Workwave had them too. If the Driver is also configured, congratulations you're finished. The drivers now have their runs allocated ready for loading and deliveries!

### Important steps / Troubleshooting

- For Workwave to create an approved Route the consignments need to be acceptable to the Vehicles tags such as Product Types of Chilled, Frozen etc, the capacities of Pallets and Cartons to match. WW back > CartonCloud
- Only approved Routes will be available to CC - WW will not approve a route if it has allocation issues
- Ensure the date is correct if you fail to upload any routes
- When pulling Routes back into CartonCloud the Vehicle name from Workwave must be set up in CartonCloud under the [Vehicles](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/createpage.action?spaceKey=KB2&title=Vehicles+-+Track+your+fleets+performance&linkCreation=true&fromPageId=532546184) section as well and match exactly.
- When pulling Routes back with drivers into CartonCloud the driver email details (or login as its used) must be set up in CartonCloud under the [Users](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Users) section as well and match exactly.

Notes:

1. Currently, only Pickup, Delivery and Pickup+Delivery consignment types are supported from CartonCloud when using this Workwave integration, others such as Point to Point are currently unsupported and will not work properly.
2. The Pull phase is currently limited to same-day dates in Workwave, so bear that in mind for the process. (Updated and now supports multiple dates).

---

<a id="zapier-integration-faq"></a>
## Zapier Integration FAQ

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/zapier-integration-faq_

### Frequently asked questions by those using Zapier to Integrate with CartonCloud

**I've received multiple emails for the same rejected order, why?**

When Zapier tries to create an order in CartonCloud, and it cannot, CartonCloud sends an error message to Zapier. For example: 400 - Order already Exists.
As this is seen as an error by Zapier, it uses its "Autoreplay" feature ( [https://zapier.com/help/autoreplay/](https://zapier.com/help/autoreplay/) ) to retry the order, a total of 5 times.

For this reason, you will receive 6 "rejection" messages for the same order.

**Can Zapier be used to send messages back from CartonCloud to my other systems?**

Yes, via our new Webhook system. Let us know what you're trying to achieve so we can assist in getting it up and running.

### **Xero Specific FAQ**

**What is the recommended workflow to get an order from Xero to CartonCloud?**

Orders created in Xero are sent to CartonCloud when Approved. This means you can create orders in a Draft status in Xero, and they will not be sent to CartonCloud until they are Approved. If you create and approve an order in one step, it'll be sent straight to CartonCloud (see the note on the delay below).

**After creating an invoice in Xero, it takes several minutes to show up in CartonCloud, why?**

From our experience, it can take anywhere from 1 to 5 minutes for orders created in Xero to appear in CartonCloud. This is due to the way in which Zapier integrates with Xero. Every 5 minutes Zapier polls Xero for new orders. It fetches the 100 most recent APPROVED invoices (using the "Date" Field to determine most recent), then looks through them looking for any it hasn't seen before and sends those which are new to CartonCloud.

**I Approved an order in Xero which never appeared in CartonCloud**

This can occur due to the way in which the Zapier / Xero connection works. As Zapier polls Xero for the 100 most recent APPROVED invoices (using the "Date" field to determine the most recent), Zapier may miss Invoices from Xero if you create more than 100 with the same Date, or, you approve an invoice whose date is more than 100 invoices old.

![zapier-integration-faq-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/zapier-integration-faq-0.png?width=670&height=340&name=zapier-integration-faq-0.png)

**Workarounds:**

1. If you're creating more than 100 invoices in a single day, we recommend adjusting the date to the next day after you hit 100.
2. If you're approving an old invoice, update the Date to today before approving.

**I created an invoice in Xero, then modified it - but CartonCloud received the modified version?**

Due to the delay in sending outlined above, the invoice is sent to CartonCloud in its current state when the outbound sending is performed.

This means, if you create an invoice, then modify it before Xero has sent it to CartonCloud, it ends up sending CartonCloud the modified version.

However, this doesn't mean you can modify orders in Xero and have the changes reflect in CartonCloud. If the order has already been sent to CartonCloud, changes made in Xero will not be reflected in CartonCloud.

**Can my Invoice PDF be sent to CartonCloud automatically as well?**

Yes. When you have us connect your Xero to CartonCloud, be sure to mention that you want this to be done.

Note that CartonCloud will receive the Invoice PDF in the Branding Theme selected at the time the order is sent to CartonCloud, which may be anywhere from 1-5 mins after the order is actually approved.

We've had a case where a client wanted to send one Branding Theme to CartonCloud, while they wanted another to be printed at their end. They were creating & approving the order in Xero with the branding theme they wanted to have appear in CartonCloud, then immediately editing the invoice to the branding theme they wanted to print. Due to the delay in the Xero API, when Xero sent the invoice to CartonCloud around 1-5 mins later, the Branding Theme selected was the one they wanted to print (not the one they wanted to send).

There are several workarounds for this:

1. Create the invoice with the Branding Theme you want to print, immediately print, then edit the order to the Branding Theme you want to send.
2. After creating the invoice, wait at least 5 minutes (or check that it's appeared in CartonCloud) before editing the Branding Theme
3. Don't automate the Invoice PDFs coming into CartonCloud, and instead email them from Xero into CartonCloud (this can be configured by our staff, just let us know).

---

# Integrations > Parsers

<a id="configuring-parsers-for-customers"></a>
## Configuring Parsers for Customers

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/configuring-parsers-for-customers_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Steps to configure Parsers for customers
  - Add Customer to the Parser
  - Download the Parser template
  - Provide the To Email Address to your customer

### Purpose

Parsers allow your customers to upload or email files into CartonCloud and the order be automatically created. In order for your customers to be able to do this, you will need to configure the Parser to the customer.

### Steps to configure Parsers for Customers

1. Add Customer to the Parser
2. Download the Parser template
3. Provide the To Email Address to your customer

### Add Customer to the Parser

- Navigate to the Parsers page by typing **Parsers** to the Search for Anything bar.
- Click **View** against the Parser you wish to connect to the Customer.

![configuring-parsers-for-customers-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-parsers-for-customers-0.png?width=670&height=229&name=configuring-parsers-for-customers-0.png)

- Click **Add Customer to Parser**.

![configuring-parsers-for-customers-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-parsers-for-customers-1.png?width=670&height=284&name=configuring-parsers-for-customers-1.png)

- Select the relevant Customer from the dropdown **Customer** menu.
- Click **Add**.

![configuring-parsers-for-customers-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-parsers-for-customers-2.png?width=670&height=147&name=configuring-parsers-for-customers-2.png)

Connecting the Customers Email Addresses to the Parser and setting up error email notification

You will now need to add the Customer's email address to the Parser. You can also optionally select if you wish the email address to receive an email if the Parser fails to upload.

It is recommended that you enable the Parser failure email notification. This will help ensure you are notified if an order fails to upload and are able to rectify it as soon as possible.

- Navigate to the Customers page, **Contacts**>**Customers**.
- Select the relevant Customer and click **Edit**.
- Select the **Email** tab.
- Type the email address into the**New email** field.
- Click **Add new email**.

If you don't wish to use a single email address and instead allow multiple email addresses with the same domain, such as '@cartoncloud.com.au', please see the [Wildcard Email Addresses](https://help.cartoncloud.com/#wildcard) section.

![configuring-parsers-for-customers-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-parsers-for-customers-3.png?width=670&height=156&name=configuring-parsers-for-customers-3.png)

- Enter the name for who will be using the email address into the **Name** field.

![configuring-parsers-for-customers-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-parsers-for-customers-4.png?width=670&height=257&name=configuring-parsers-for-customers-4.png)

- Tick the box next to the Parser you wish to associate to the email address. You can also tick Send Failure To if you wish the email address to receive an email if the Parser fails to upload.
- Click **Save**.

![configuring-parsers-for-customers-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-parsers-for-customers-5.png?width=670&height=222&name=configuring-parsers-for-customers-5.png)

![configuring-parsers-for-customers-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-parsers-for-customers-6.png?width=670&height=113&name=configuring-parsers-for-customers-6.png)

Never link two parsers to a single email address which have the same To Address.

This will cause problems because, upon import, the system will not know which Parser to use and will go with whichever Parser it finds first. This leads to unpredictability in how the data is parsed.

**Wildcard Email Addresses**

Wildcard email addresses allow you to configure a particular domain to work with a given parser.

For example, for the above customer Flower Fitness, several people in the business may need to send through the Parser from their email address. In this case, you could set up a wildcard email address for the domain @flowerfitness.com. With this setup, anyone from Flower Fitness with the domain @[flowerfitness.com](http://flowerfitness.com/) in their email address will be able to send through the Parser.

Wildcard email addresses are added by using a * character before the @ symbol. For example:

*@flowerfitness.com

![configuring-parsers-for-customers-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-parsers-for-customers-7.png?width=670&height=199&name=configuring-parsers-for-customers-7.png)

### Download the Parser template

Once you have set up the Parser for the customer, you will need to download and provide your customer with the Parser template. Your customer must use this template to be able to successfully parse an order into CartonCloud.

- Navigate to the Parser page by typing **Parsers** into the **Search for anything**bar.
- Click **View** against the relevant Parser.

![configuring-parsers-for-customers-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-parsers-for-customers-8.png?width=670&height=225&name=configuring-parsers-for-customers-8.png)

- Click the **Download** button.

### Provide the To email address to your Customer

Once you have provided the Parser template to your customers you will also need to provide them with the To Address and ensure their email address is listed in the Allowed From Address(es). Your customer must use the To Address to send through their parser file.

- Navigate to the relevant Customer, **Contacts**>**Customers**.
- Click **Edit**.
- Select the **Parser** tab.
- Within the relevant Parser, you will see the **Allowed From Address(es)**and **To Address**.
  - **Allowed From Address(es)**: the addresses that are allowed to send the Parser in.
  - **To Address**: the email address the user must send the Parser to.

![configuring-parsers-for-customers-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-parsers-for-customers-10.png?width=670&height=109&name=configuring-parsers-for-customers-10.png)

Understanding To Email Address Formats within Parsers:

Typically, email addresses for parsers are in the format:

{**type**}+{**slug**}@[in.cartoncloud.com.au](http://in.cartoncloud.com.au/)

i.e., sale_orders+bruce_transport@in.cartoncloud.com.au

type:

This is the type of email being loaded in. The type can be anything; however, we generally make it clear as to what the Parser is designed to import because this helps when you have multiple parsers, for example:

sale_orders+bruce_transport@in.cartoncloud.com.au
purchase_orders+bruce_transport@in.cartoncloud.com.au
manifests+bruce_transport@in.cartoncloud.com.au
invoices+bruce_transport@in.cartoncloud.com.au

For this reason, using a type such as "orders" would be a poor choice because when you have clients sending you both Sale Orders and Purchase Orders it is not apparent which email address to send to.

slug:

The slug is the tenant's name as specified in the URL at the top of the page. Email addresses are case-insensitive, so you can use whatever case you want in the email address.

In this example, the slug in the URL is Bruce_Transport. Therefore, the slug in the email address can be bruce_transport, Bruce_Transport, BRUCE_TRANSPORT or any other case variation.

---

<a id="email-setup-for-incoming-emails-parsers-auto-forward-emails"></a>
## Email Setup for Incoming Emails / Parsers / Auto Forward Emails

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/email-setup-for-incoming-emails-parsers-auto-forward-emails_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Setup instructions
- Email account which catches all outgoing emails
- Email account which gets sent a copy of all incoming emails

### Purpose

To set up your CartonCloud account to be able to receive emails with Parsers from Customers.

For example, a Purchase Order Parser can be emailed to the dedicated email address and the file will be imported into CartonCloud and the relevant Purchase Orders will be created in CartonCloud.

### Setup Instructions

Email Setup for Incoming Email (ie: Manifests, Purchase Orders, Sale Orders, Invoices)

You have two options when configuring the email for incoming emails.

1. The email can be sent to an **@[in.cartoncloud.com.au](http://in.cartoncloud.com.au/)** domain.
  - The configuration for emails needs to be anything then a + symbol then the name of the tenancy in CartonCloud, i.e the name top left of the screen then the CartonCloud domain. e.g. manifests+xyzlogistics@in.cartoncloud.com.au
  - Now customers can email files to that address and if setup on [Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parsers) the files will be imported using the parser.
2. The email can be sent to your own domain e.g. [xyzlogistics.com.au](http://xyzlogistics.com.au/)

-
  - If you want to use your own domain, ie: manifests@xyzlogistics.com.au, then you'll need to contact your IT department and have them set up an auto-forward keeping the **original sender's details intact.**manifests+xyzlogistics@in.cartoncloud.com.au
  - You will also need to add the email domain under Organisation Settings → Email → Receive incoming mail addressed to the domain ([xyzlogistics.com.au](http://xyzlogistics.com.au/))
  - Now files can be sent to the email of [xyzlogistics.com.au](http://xyzlogistics.com.au/) and they will forward to the CartonCloud email address in the background and be imported using the relevant [Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parsers)

Note, you will need to [add the Customer to the Parser and configure the Customer's email address to the Parser](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Configuring-Parsers-for-Customers)for the Customer to be able to email the Parser file into CartonCloud.

**We recommend creating the following email addresses:**

| **Local Email Address** | **Forward to Email Address** |
| --- | --- |
| manifests@xyzlogistics.com.au | manifests+xyzlogistics@in.cartoncloud.com.au |
| sale_orders@xyzlogistics.com.au | sale_orders+xyzlogistics@[in.cartoncloud.com.au](http://in.cartoncloud.com.au/) |
| purchase_orders@xyzlogistics.com.au | purchase_orders+xyzlogistics@[in.cartoncloud.com.au](http://in.cartoncloud.com.au/) |
| invoices@xyzlogistics.com.au | invoices+xyzlogistics@[in.cartoncloud.com.au](http://in.cartoncloud.com.au/) |

- Modify the existing parsers in the system to have the correct "to" address, as per the previous line.

### Email Account which Catches all outgoing emails:

When emails are going out of CartonCloud (to tenants-customers, for things like Invoices, Proof Of Delivery Notifications etc), the tenant themselves has no record of those emails, or nowhere they can go to see them. For this reason, an email address can be set up to receive a copy of all outgoing emails (via BCC). Normally a Gmail account should be used for this, it's easy to just set up something like xyzlogistics_cartoncloud@gmail.com. Staff from xyzlogistics can then log in and search/see the emails.

### Email Account which gets sent a copy of all incoming email:

If the tenant is using the @[in.cartoncloud.com.au](http://in.cartoncloud.com.au/) domain, then they have no way of seeing all incoming emails. For this reason, incoming emails can be forwarded to another email account, normally Gmail as per above. Note: only emails that CartonCloud can correctly identify are for the tenant will be forwarded.

If the tenant is forwarding from their own domain, ie: manifests@xyzlogistics.com.au → manifests+xyzlogistics@in.cartoncloud.com.au, then it's recommended they simply handle the forwarding within their own mail server to send it onto some other Gmail account (thereby forwarding to two different email addresses).

---

<a id="how-to-run-a-report-in-myob-that-lists-so-s-for-a-parser-and-includes-ship-to-address"></a>
## How to Run a Report in MYOB

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-run-a-report-in-myob-that-lists-so-s-for-a-parser-and-includes-ship-to-address_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to steps

### Purpose

This is a guide to extracting Sale from MYOB for import to CartonCloud through a Parser.

### How to steps

We can easily import your sales orders from MYOB through a parser.  To do this you can run an MYOB report, add additional columns to the report, then email it to the nominated parser email address.

Make sure you run the report 'Sales Item Detail Report'.

Click on the Insert/Modify Tab, then click on the Show/Hide button.

This will allow you to add the appropriate fields to the report.

Refresh report.

Then email the report to the nominated email address  e.g. Sales_Order_Clearwater+Tenant_Name@in.cartoncloud.com.au

![how-to-run-a-report-in-myob-that-lists-so-s-for-a-parser-and-includes-ship-to-address-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-run-a-report-in-myob-that-lists-so-s-for-a-parser-and-includes-ship-to-address-0.png?width=670&height=333&name=how-to-run-a-report-in-myob-that-lists-so-s-for-a-parser-and-includes-ship-to-address-0.png)

<a id="parse-a-file"></a>
## Parse a File

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/parse-a-file_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- How to parse a file
- Parser troubleshooting

### Purpose

Parsers are able to read data and then import the data into CartonCloud in a format the system can understand. Then, using the data, the Parser can create or update a record in CartonCloud, for example, a Sale Order or Consignment.

There are three ways a Parser can be used with CartonCloud:

1. Web application upload - the parser file can be uploaded directly to CartonCloud. For example, from the Consignments page, you can select More>Import Consignments and select the file you wish to parse, and the new Consignments will be created. You can also use the 'Parse a File' page to parse in new orders. Your customers can also use CartonCloud to upload the parser file. To do this, you will need to add the Customer to the Parser.
2. Email - the parser file can be uploaded via emailing the file to a set email address. See Parsers and Configuring Parsers for Customers for more information.
3. File Transfer Protocol (FTP) - please contact the CartonCloud team for more information.

This page will focus on **parsing a file by web application upload**.

### Prerequisites

Before you use the 'Parse a file' page to upload your parser, you will need to add the Customer to the Parser. Please see [Configuring Parsers for Customers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Configuring-Parsers-for-Customers) for more information.

You will also need to download the template associated with the Parser and use this to upload the data into CartonCloud. To download the template:

- Navigate to the relevant Parser by typing Parsers into the Search for anything bar. Click View against the relevant Parser.
- Click Download .

![parse-a-file-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/parse-a-file-0.png?width=670&height=202&name=parse-a-file-0.png)

- Alternatively, you can use this page to download the relevant file.

### How to parse a file

- Navigate to the Parse a file page, More>Parse a file.
- Select the Customer you wish to parse the file for.
- Select the relevant Parser.
- Select the file.
- Select if you wish to send an import email to the customer.
- Click Upload.

![parse-a-file-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/parse-a-file-1.png?width=670&height=277&name=parse-a-file-1.png)

### Parser Troubleshooting

Please see [Parser Troubleshooting](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/kAC-I) for steps on how to resolve Parser issues.

---

<a id="parse-a-file-as-customer"></a>
## Parse a File as a Customer

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/parse-a-file-as-customer_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Parser
- Benefits of using Parsers
- Use cases for Parsers
- Types of Parsers
- How to parse a file

### What is a Parser

Parsers are able to read data and then import the data into CartonCloud in a format the system can understand. Using the data, the Parser can create or update a record in CartonCloud, for example, a Sale Order or Consignment.

Parsers are usually in the format of an excel spreadsheet (xlsx, csv etc.), and the document will contain all the data pertaining to the orders. There are three ways in which Parsers can be uploaded to CartonCloud:

1. Web application upload - from the ‘Parse a file’ page on the web app, the parser file can be uploaded directly to CartonCloud.
2. Email - the parser file can be uploaded via emailing the file to a set email address. Once emailed in, the orders will be automatically created in CartonCloud.
3. File Transfer Protocol (FTP) - for this method, please contact the CartonCloud team for more information.

### Benefits of using Parsers

- Eliminates repetitive data entry
- Reduces time spent creating/sending through orders
- Data integrity - as the data only has to be entered once (as you can copy and paste the data into the file or use the file the data is already formatted in), you reduce the chances of error
- Reduce correspondence and admin time spent with your 3PL/CartonCloud account owner. Rather than having to speak with your 3PL/CartonCloud account owner you can instead email the order straight into CartonCloud.

### Use cases for using Parsers

- If you have a large number of orders which need to be entered.
- If the data for the orders already exist in the format (for example, the software that generates the orders exports them in a CSV format)

### Types of Parsers

Please see [List of Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/List-of-Parsers) for an extensive list of Parsers that can be utilised.

### How to Parse a File

*Please note, before uploading a file you need to ensure your CartonCloud account owner/3PL has set up a Parser for you and provided you with the template to use.*

- Navigate to the Parse a file page, Parse a File .
- Select the File Type (the type of order you are uploading, e.g Purchase Order).
- Select the relevant Parser.
- Select the file.
- Click Upload .

![parse-a-file-as-customer-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/parse-a-file-as-customer-0.png?width=670&height=290&name=parse-a-file-as-customer-0.png)
Another option to upload a Parser is to email the file in. To do this you need your CartonCloud account owner/3PL to have set this up for the email address you will be emailing from. In addition they will need to provide you with an email address to send the parser to.

---

<a id="parser-troubleshooting"></a>
## Parser Troubleshooting

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/parser-troubleshooting_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Troubleshooting steps
- Address Allocation and Parsers

### Purpose

This guide gives you suggested areas to investigate when a parser has failed.

If after following the below steps you can still not resolve the Parser issue, please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

### Troubleshooting Steps

**1. Check the Email [Import Log](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Parsing-Log).**

This is the best place to start when looking for what caused the error.

To navigate to the Import Log:

- Select More > Import Log .
- Here, you will see all the failed and successful import attempts.
- The below table steps through how to read the Import Log.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Dec-10-2025-01-18-45-2617-AM.png?width=670&height=313&name=image-png-Dec-10-2025-01-18-45-2617-AM.png)

| **Heading/Field** | **Explanation** |
| --- | --- |
| Type | How the file was imported. **Email:** the parser file was emailed to CartonCloud **Web Upload:** the parser file was uploaded through 'Parse a file' in CartonCloud. **API:** the file was sent through to CartonCloud via API. |
| Source | Either the email address the file was sent from (if the file was emailed in), the user who uploaded the file via CartonCloud (if it was uploaded via parse a file) or the API Client that sent the file (If using an API connection to transfer the file). |
| Recipient | If the file was uploaded via web upload or emailed in the recipient will be the 'To address' associated with the Parser. This will help you identify what Parser was used. |
| Logged at | The time the file was parsed in. |
| Status | Success (green tick): the order has been successfully processed with no issues  Success with warnings (green tick with yellow warning symbol): the order has been successfully imported, however, with minor issues such as an incorrect product code or insufficient stock.  Success with errors (green tick with red error symbol): the order has been successfully imported, however, with more serious issues, such as an invalid quantity or invalid warehouse location.  Failure (red cross): the order has failed and not been imported. There are major issues preventing the order from being successfully imported.   See [error code status mapping](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Parser-Troubleshooting#error-code-status-mapping) for more information. |

- To see more information relating to the parsing log, click on the parsing log to open the details.
- You can then break down the information to find out why the Parser failed and confirm the Parser being utilised is the Parser you expected to be using.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Dec-10-2025-01-25-21-7924-AM.png?width=670&height=245&name=image-png-Dec-10-2025-01-25-21-7924-AM.png)

- The below outlines common error messages received in the Import Log.

| **Common Issues and Error Messages** | **Where to Check** |
| --- | --- |
| Error Message: **"Parser can not be found with recipient email address"**   A customer is trying to parse a file to CartonCloud, and the email is incorrect | Check the 'Allowed From Address(es)' and 'To Address' email addresses set up against the Parser match the email addresses used. See [Check 2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parser+Troubleshooting#ParserTroubleshooting-check2) for more information. Often there can be typing issues, or the email is used to send the Parser is not in the 'Allowed From Address' list. Check that there are no spaces BEFORE the email address in the parser (this often happens when you are copying and pasting email addresses into the parser). |
| Error Message: **"No attachments found in email message!"** | The customer has not included the file in their email. |
| Error Message: "File ________ could not be Parsed. Attachment File Type: DAT is not supported by Parser. Supported file formats are: xls, ms-excel, xlsx" | An incorrect file type is being sent. This is because parsers are built to read only one specific file type. See [Check 3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parser+Troubleshooting#ParserTroubleshooting-check3) for more information. |
| Error Message: "The match number does not exist in the matches array" | This is a data issue. One of the required fields (normally the Product Code) does not match any current products in the system. |
| Calling the Wrong Parser Type - e.g. may have tried to send an invoice parser template to a SO parser | Look for the actual parser name (type) that the customer attempted to parse on the [Email Parsing Log](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Email+Parsing+Log). If the wrong file is being parsed, then go to customer as above, click on edit, email and tick the correct parser type to email. You can download the sample template that was used to build the parser following the steps in [Configuring Parsers for Customers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Configuring-Parsers-for-Customers). Using this file, compare the failed file from the [Email Parsing Log](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Email+Parsing+Log) to check if an incorrect file type is being used. |
| Error Message: "Failed to import anything from the file. Key field customer_reference cannot be empty" | This is a data issue. The required field (Customer Reference etc) has an empty cell in the file. Open the data file and check each entry to ensure that all data is populated. |
| No Stock Matching Conditions | Below this message will display the conditions specified for this parser. Common conditions are often "Expiry Date" Things to check:  Current stock in the warehouse and the expiry dates [Purchase Order](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Purchase+Orders) status for stock not fully received [Customer Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Edit+Customer+or+Customer+Settings) for "Minimum Purchase Order Product Status" |
| The order/consignment created by a Parser is missing a delivery address | See the article: [Address not appearing on a new Sale Order or Consignment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/address-not-appearing-on-a-new-sale-order-or-consignment-unallocated) |

#### **Error code status mapping**

**Sale Order**

| **Error** | **Status (Success with warning or error)** |
| --- | --- |
| Remove lines with blank product codes | Warning |
| Remove lines with not enough stock | Warning |
| Remove lines with zero quantity | Warning |
| Remove lines with failed conversions | Warning |
| Remove lines with invalid conversions | Warning |
| Unit of measure adjusted to default UOM | Warning |
| Remove lines with invalid UOM | Warning |
| Line item has expired | Warning |
| Before expiry threshold | Warning |
| After expiry threshold | Warning |
| Not enough stock use available stock | Warning |
| MLOR per address expiry multiple address for address code found | Error |
| MLOR address not found | Error |
| MLOR expiry threshold | Error |
| Unable to parse | Error |
| Multiple products found for line item | Error |
| Missing product code reject | Error |
| Not enough stock reject | Error |
| Invalid quantity (non-positive number) | Error |
| UOM conversion failed reject | Error |
| UOM invalid reject | Error |

**Purchase Order**

| **Error** | **Status (Success with warning or error)** |
| --- | --- |
| Product code available (item removed) | Warning |
| Product code available (reject order) | Error |
| Product expiry invalid | Error |
| Product quantity invalid | Error |
| PUOM unit invalid (item removed) | Warning |
| PUOM unit invalid (reject order) | Error |
| PUOM unit invalid (substitute with default UOM) | Warning |
| Warehouse location invalid | Error |
| Warehouse location cannot handle product type | Error |
| Custom field invalid type | Error |
| Custom field non unique | Error |

**2. Check the Parser's 'Allowed From Address(es)' and 'To Address' email addresses are correct**

If the Parser has been emailed in, you will need to check that:

- The email address it was sent from is associated with the Parser.
- The email address the file was emailed to is the correct email associated with the Parser.

**To check:**

- Navigate to the Parsers page by typing in Parsers into the Search for anything bar.
- Select the Parser you are utilising.
- Scroll down to the bottom and under Customers check the Allowed Email Addresses match the email address that emailed the Parser in.
- Under To Address , check the address matches the one to which the file was emailed.

![image2021-12-21_16-28-11.png](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/servlet/rtaImage?eid=ka05j000001a9bv&feoid=00N5j00000K0J4b&refid=0EM5j0000042PUt)

If the email address is not on the 'Allowed Email Addresses' list, please see [Configuring Parsers for Customers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/configuring-parsers-for-customers) step two.

**3. Ensure the parser file matches the sample file format**

To view the sample file associated with the Parser:

- Navigate to the Parsers page by typing in Parsers into the Search for anything bar.
- Select the Parser you are utilising.
- Select the blue Download button under Sample File .

![image2021-12-21_16-35-28.png](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/servlet/rtaImage?eid=ka05j000001a9bv&feoid=00N5j00000K0J4b&refid=0EM5j0000042PV8)

- Ensure the excel file is the correct Type; for example, the file is csv format.

![image2021-12-21_16-38-24.png](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/servlet/rtaImage?eid=ka05j000001a9bv&feoid=00N5j00000K0J4b&refid=0EM5j0000042PVI)

**4. Ensure the customer attempting to parse the file is associated with the Parser**

- Navigate to the Customers page, **Contacts**>**Customers**.
- Select the relevant Customer and click **Edit**.
- Select the **Parser** tab.
- Check that the Parser you or the Customer is attempting to use is listed on the Parser tab.

![image2021-12-21_16-49-35.png](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/servlet/rtaImage?eid=ka05j000001a9bv&feoid=00N5j00000K0J4b&refid=0EM5j0000042PVh)

If you can not see the Parser listed, you will need to add the Parser to the Customer. See [Configuring Parsers for Customers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/GAK_Hw)step one.

### Address Allocation and Parsers

When importing orders with addresses (for example, a Sale Order) via a Parser there is certain requirements that must be met in order for the address to allocate to an existing address. These requirements are listed below:

- The existing address record has to be active and not in a draft format.
- Street Address has to be specified in the Parser file and it must match the existing address record.
- Postcode has to be specified in the Parser file and it must match the existing address record.
- If the Country is specified in the Parser file, the existing address record has to be the same Country.
- If the Company name is specified in the Parser file, the existing address record has to be the same Company name.
- If the Contact name is specified in the Parser file, the existing address record has to be the same Contact name.
- Either the Company or Contact name has to be specified in the Parser file.
- If Street Address 2 is specified in the Parser file, the existing address record has to be the same Street Address 2.
- If Street Address 2 is not specified in the Parser file, the existing address record should not have a Street Address 2 Value.

<a id="parsers"></a>
## Parsers

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/parsers_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- How to set up a Parser
- Video overview
- How to use the Parser with CartonCloud
- How to navigate to the Parser page
- Available Parsers
- Parsers overview
- Parsing via email

### Purpose

Parsers are able to read data and then import the data into CartonCloud in a format the system can understand. Using the data, the Parser can create or update a record in CartonCloud, for example, a Sale Order or Consignment.  See [Parsers Overview](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parsers#Parsers-overview) for a more detailed description.

For information regarding non-parser Integrations, we suggest reading our guide: [Integration with other Softwar](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Integration+with+other+Software)e

### Benefits

Parsers take data or information you already have and turn it into a format CartonCloud can read. This means you do not have to manually re-enter the data into CartonCloud or adjust the way another software exports the data or the way you receive data from a customer. For example, if you receive a file from a customer with all their Sale Orders, rather than manually inputting this data into CartonCloud you can use the Sale Order Parser which will read the file and create the Sale Orders in CartonCloud.

### How to set up a Parser

To set up a Parser please [contact the CartonCloud team](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) . See [Available Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parsers#Parsers-parsers) for a complete list of Parsers that can be set up on your CartonCloud account.

### Video Overview

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/12iBaNv4KWo

### How to use the Parser with CartonCloud

There are three ways a Parser can be used with CartonCloud:

1. **[Web application upload](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Parse-a-File)**- the parser file can be uploaded directly to CartonCloud. For example from the Consignments page, you can select More>Import Consignments and select the file you wish to parse and the new Consignments will be created. Your customers can also use CartonCloud to upload the parser file. To do this, you will need to [add the Customer to the Parser.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Configuring-Parsers-for-Customers)
2. **Email** - the parser file can be uploaded via emailing the file to a set email address. To do this, you will need to:
  1. Add the Customer to the Parser. See [Configuring Parsers for Customers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Configuring-Parsers-for-Customers).
  2. Set up the email address for the incoming emails/Parsers.
3. **File Transfer Protocol** (FTP) - please [contact the CartonCloud team](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport)  for more information.

### How to navigate to the Parsers page

- Type **Parsers** into the Search for anything bar at the top of the application.

![2025-12-04 08_08_56-Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/2025-12-04%2008_08_56-Settings.png?width=670&height=130&name=2025-12-04%2008_08_56-Settings.png)

### Available Parsers

The following Parsers are currently available to be set up now by [contacting our team](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) .

Please see [List of Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/List-of-Parsers) for available parser templates.

| **Parser** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Sale Order | Allows a file type to be read into CartonCloud which will create a [Sale Order](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Sale+Orders) in the system. This Parser is ideal for when you have a large number of Sale Orders which need to be entered and the data for those Sale Orders already exists in some format. |
| Purchase Order | Allows a file type to be read into CartonCloud which will create a [Purchase Order](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Purchase+Orders) in the system. This Parser is ideal for when you have a large number of Purchase Orders which need to be entered and the data for those Purchase Orders already exists in some format. |
| Manifest | Allows a file type to be read into CartonCloud which will create a[Manifest](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Manifests) in the system. |
| Product | Allows a file type to be read into CartonCloud which will [create a Product](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Add+a+Product) in the system. |
| Consignment Invoice | Allows customer invoices to be uploaded and automatically attached to the relevant consignment. This works by scanning the uploaded document, using its reference number, and matching it against the consignment it is to be attached to. [This can be used in association with QR Codes to automatically attach consignment invoices to consignments.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Using+QR+codes+to+automatically+attach+a+POD+to+a+Consignment) |
| Stock Import | Allows a file type to be read into CartonCloud which will[import the stock](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Import+Stock) for Products already created in the system. The Stock Update parser supports filtering by POP ID, allowing more precise bulk updates on stock records. This helps target specific stock items even when multiple products share similar attributes such as product code, status, or expiry date. |
| Sale Order Invoice | Allows customer invoices to be uploaded and automatically attached to the relevant Sale Order. This works by scanning the uploaded document for its reference number and matching it against the Sale Order it is to be attached to. [This invoice can then flow onto a generated consignment if required.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Copying+Sale+Order+Customer+Invoices+to+Consignments) |
| Stock Update | Allows a file type to be read into CartonCloud which will[https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Import+Stock](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Import+Stock)update the quantity of stock in the system by updating the corresponding Purchase Order it came into the Warehouse on. |
| Consignment with Items | Allows a single file to be read which can create multiple Consignments, over multiple Customers, using zero or many Manifests. The parser can also be used to update existing Consignments for changes that have been made after the original Consignment was imported. If you are using another TMS to build Run Sheets and allocate jobs, you can use the Parser to import the Consignments into CartonCloud with the allocation information from the other systems. CartonCloud will then create the Run Sheets and allocation to match, therefore, removing the need for repeated manual work and Drivers can immediately perform the deliveries as scheduled. **Update functionality** By using the update functionality, any changes made in the other TMS can be easily replicated in CartonCloud using the Parser.  If you are using the Parser to update Consignments see the below fields which can be modified on the Consignment:   Service Type   Addresses   Consignment Data Custom Fields   Consignment Items (all fields including Code, Description, Item Custom Fields and item properties – Qty, Pal, Cub, Weight, Space, L, W, H.)   Driver   Run Sheet   Please note, only Consignments that are not associated with a Manifest can be updated using the Parser. |
| Manifest with Consignments items |  |

### Parsers Overview

The word "Parser" is a fancy name for a piece of software that simply knows how to take data in a given format, and read it so it can be loaded into the system.
For example, when Parsers are created for Excel files, we're simply telling CartonCloud which column is which, so the import will be completed successfully.

![parsers-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/parsers-1.png?width=670&height=308&name=parsers-1.png)

In this particular case a Parser would be created telling the system that the column labelled:
`customer_reference` maps to the `customer_reference field within the Sale Order`
`postcode` should be added to the Addresses Postcode
`qty` is the quantity of the product that we need, etc.

Once this Parser is added, we can reliably import files in the given format every time, completely automating the process of data entry.

Parsers can be set up for almost any type of file: csv, xls, txt, xml and many others. We do not support parsing PDF documents however, as the structure of the content is often unreliable and difficult to read.

### Parsing via Email

One of the most common uses of Parsers is automatically importing data from email attachments.

This allows clients to email files directly into CartonCloud, have them read, and then the jobs (Sale Orders, Consignments, Purchase Orders, and more) created automatically.

![parsers-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/parsers-2.png?width=340&height=554&name=parsers-2.png)

To learn how to set up this connection between email addresses and parsers, see our guide: [Configuring Parsers for Customers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Configuring+Parsers+for+Customers)

---

<a id="updating-consignments-via-parser"></a>
## Updating Consignments via Parser

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/updating-consignments-via-parser_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use case
- Fields that can be updated
- How to set up the parser
- How to upload the parser
- Workflow
  - Consignment item import parser workflow
  - Manifest with consignments items parser
- Settings to configure

### Purpose

Using the **Consignment Item Import Parser**or **Manifest With Consignment Items Parser,**you can update existing Consignments with changes made since the original Consignment was imported.

### Use case

For example, if you use another TMS to build Run Sheets and allocate jobs, you can use the Parser to import the Consignments (that already exist in CartonCloud) into CartonCloud with the allocation information from the other systems. CartonCloud will then create the Run Sheets and allocation to match, therefore, removing the need for repeated manual work, and Drivers can immediately perform the deliveries as scheduled.

Using the update functionality, any changes made in the other TMS can be easily replicated in CartonCloud using the Parser.

### Fields that can be updated

- Service Type
- Addresses
- Consignment Data Custom Fields
- Consignment Items (all fields including Code, Description, Item Custom Fields and item properties – Qty, Pal, Cub, Weight, Space, L, W, H.)
- Driver
- Run Sheet

Please note this Parser will only work for Delivery, Duplicate, Pickup and Point to Point Consignments.

This Parser does NOT support Return and Pickup + Delivery Consignments.

### How to set up the Parser

Please contact our Integrations Team -  via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) to set up your Parser.

Please use the below workflows and setting descriptions to determine which workflow you wish to use in your operations, this will assist our team to ensure the correct Parser is set up for your account.

### How to upload the Parser

To upload the Parser you can do so from the Consignments page in CartonCloud. Please see[Importing Consignments](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Importing-Consignments)for more information.

### Workflow

You can follow several different workflows when using the **Consignment Item Import Parser**or the **Manifest With Consignment Items Parser** to update existing Consignments or create new Consignments. Using the below workflows and [setting descriptions](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Updating+Consignments+via+Parser#UpdatingConsignmentsviaParser-settings), you can determine what workflow you wish to utilise in your operations.

Our Support/Integrations team will help ensure the correct settings are configured for your workflow; however, you can use the below as a guide when deciding what workflow you would like your Parser to follow.

**Consignment Item Import Parser Workflow**

*If a Manifest reference number is NOT provided on the file*

- The Manifest reference does not need to be included in the import file.
- Regardless if a Consignment is on a Manifest or not, the Consignment can be updated using the Consignment Item Import Parser; however, the *'Allow updates to Consignments and items via parsing'* **MUST**be enabled.

The max status function is controlled by our Integrations/Support team. If you are unsure if you wish to include this function in your workflow please reach out to the integrations team  via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport)

![updating-consignments-via-parser-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/updating-consignments-via-parser-0.png?width=670&height=412&name=updating-consignments-via-parser-0.png)

**Manifest with Consignments Items Parser**

*If a Manifest reference number IS provided on the file*

- The Consignment must already be on a Manifest to be updated.
- The customer and Manifest reference on the parser file must have the same customer reference and Manifest reference as the Consignment you wish to update.
- You must include the Manifest reference on the file.

![updating-consignments-via-parser-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/updating-consignments-via-parser-1.png?width=410&height=752&name=updating-consignments-via-parser-1.png)

### Settings to configure

Our Support/Integrations team will help ensure the correct settings are configured for your workflow; however, you can use the below as a guide when deciding what workflow you would like your Parser to follow.

To navigate to the settings:

- Navigate to the Customer Settings, Contacts > Customers and click Edit against the relevant Customer.
- Select the Transport Management tab.

| **Setting** | **Enabled** | **Disabled** | **Use Case** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Allow updates to Consignments and items via parsing  (only applies to the **Consignment Items Import Parser**) | Consignments either on a Manifest (the Manifest reference does not need to be included on the import file) or not a Manifest will be updated if the customer reference on the Consignment matches a Consignment already in CartonCloud. This will only apply if 'Allow multiple consignments to have the same reference' and 'Skip consignments with references that already exist' is DISABLED.      The Parser must also use the max status functionality for the setting to work and for the Consignments to be updated. | Consignments can not be updated. The only way Consignments can be updated with this setting disabled is using the Manifest with Consignments Items Parser, and the Consignment must be on a Manifest. | If you want to update existing Consignments on a Manifest, but the Manifest reference is not provided on the Parser file, or the Consignment is not on a Manifest, you need to ensure this setting is ENABLED.  If you are using the max status function on the Parser, you need to ensure this setting is ENABLED to update Consignments. |
| Allow duplicate Manifests to update existing Consignments and Items until the Manifest has been updated to any In-Warehouse status  (only applies to the **Manifest with Consignment Items Parser**) | You can update existing Consignments when parsing a file that contains the same Manifest reference. Note, the Manifest reference must be included in the file for this setting to work. | You are NOT able to parse a file containing duplicate Consignment references. | If you want to update existing Consignments on a Manifest, you must ensure this setting is ENABLED. You also need to ensure the import file contains the Manifest reference; otherwise, the setting will not apply. |
| Allow multiple consignments to have the same reference | You can add Consignments with duplicate references. | You are NOT able to add Consignments with duplicate references. Depending on other settings configured, the Consignment with the duplicate reference will either be created into a new Consignment, or the existing Consignment will be updated. | If you want to update existing Consignments, you need to ensure this setting is DISABLED. |
| Skip consignments with references that already exist | Consignments with references that already exist in CartonCloud will be skipped and not included in the import. | Consignments with references that already exist in CartonCloud will be included in the import. Depending on other settings configured, the Consignment with the duplicate reference will either be created into a new Consignment, or the existing Consignment will be updated. | If you want to update existing Consignments, you need to ensure this setting is **DISABLED**.          Note, the 'Allow multiple Consignments to have the same reference' setting can not be enabled whilst the 'Skip consignments with references that already exist' is enabled. This is because these two settings contradict each other, and thus only one of the settings can be enabled. |

---

# Integrations > Self-Managed Integrations

<a id="how-to-enable-customers-to-create-their-own-self-managed-integrations"></a>
## How to enable Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-enable-customers-to-create-their-own-self-managed-integrations_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Considerations
- How to enable every Customer to create their own Self-Managed Integrations (Organisation Settings)
- How to enable certain Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations (Customer Settings)
- How to set up a Self-Managed Integration as a Customer

### Purpose

Self-Managed Integrations allow you to create integrations from within your own CartonCloud account. Within the Self-Managed Integrations, you can choose the platform you wish to integrate with.

You can configure the integration yourself or you can have your customer set the integration up from their CartonCloud login. This allows for greater security as your customer doesn’t have to share their integration system login details with you. For your Customer to create their own Self-Managed Integration you **must first give them the permission to do so from within your CartonCloud account.** You can choose to enable all Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations or only particular Customers.

### Considerations

- Self-Managed Integrations are a paid integration and by allowing your Customer access to create their own Self-Managed Integrations, if they do create an Integration it will be billable to your account.

### How to enable every Customer to create their own Self-Managed Integrations (Organisation Settings)

To enable every Customer to create their own Self-Managed Integrations you must do so from the Organisation Settings.

- Navigate to the Organisation Settings, More > Organisation Settings .
- Select the Features & Options tab.
- Scroll down to the setting heading Self-Managed Integrations.
- Against the setting Allow Customer to access Self-Managed Integrations select Yes from the drop down menu.

![how-to-enable-customers-to-create-their-own-self-managed-integrations-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-enable-customers-to-create-their-own-self-managed-integrations-0.png?width=503&height=160&name=how-to-enable-customers-to-create-their-own-self-managed-integrations-0.png)

- Scroll down and select Save .
- This will allow every Customer within your CartonCloud account to create their own Self-Managed Integrations, unless you disable the setting from the Customer Settings for a particular Customer.

### How to enable certain Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations (Customer Settings)

To enable only particular Customers access to create their own Self-Managed Integrations you must do so from the Customer Settings.

- Navigate to the Customer page, Contacts > Customers .
- Select the relevant Customer and click Edit .
- Select the Integrations tab.
- Against the setting Allow access to configure Self-Managed Integrations , select Yes from the drop-down menu.

![how-to-enable-customers-to-create-their-own-self-managed-integrations-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-enable-customers-to-create-their-own-self-managed-integrations-1.png?width=670&height=187&name=how-to-enable-customers-to-create-their-own-self-managed-integrations-1.png)

- Scroll down and select Save .
- This will allow only that particular Customer to create their own Self-Managed Integrations (unless you have it enabled it for other customers as well).

### How to set up a Self-Managed Integration as a Customer

- Self-Managed Xero Integration (Customer)
- Self-Managed Shopify Integration (Customer)

---

<a id="managing-self-managed-integrations"></a>
## Managing Self-Managed Integrations

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/managing-self-managed-integrations_

### Table of Contents

- [Overview](https://help.cartoncloud.com#Overview)
- [Managing Self-Managed Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com#Managing-Self-Managed-Integrations)
- [Disconnecting a Self-Managed Integration](https://help.cartoncloud.com#Disconnecting-a-Self-Managed-Shopify-Integration)

### Overview

How to manage billing for your Self-Managed Integrations. It's important to understand that this is a paid integration.
Once the Self-Managed Integration is active, billing will begin automatically at $10 per week per integration billed weekly.
Billing for Self-Managed Integrations will stop automatically when the integration is disconnected.

### Managing Self-Managed Integrations

Because Self-Managed Integrations are a paid feature, it is important you are able to manage and keep track of the number of active integrations your customer's have. This is useful if you wish to pass on the cost to your customer and reconcile your invoices.

If a Customer has a live integration they will have a green dot icon against their name. It will also display the number of active integrations for that customer below their name.

![managing-self-managed-integrations-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/managing-self-managed-integrations-0.png?width=670&height=144&name=managing-self-managed-integrations-0.png)

### Disconnecting a Self-Managed Integration

If you need to cancel and disconnect the integration you will need to:

- Navigate to the **Self-Managed Integrations** page.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click the connected integration (Shopify, Xero, etc).
- Select the three-dot configuration icon and select **Delete** Integration.
- This will remove the integration and stop the billing of the integration to your account.

![managing-self-managed-integrations-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/managing-self-managed-integrations-1.png?width=261&height=286&name=managing-self-managed-integrations-1.png)

<a id="self-managed-etsy-integration"></a>
## Self Managed Etsy Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-etsy-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Prerequisites
- Limitations
- How to Set Up the Etsy Self-Managed Integration
- Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed Etsy Integration
- Editing an existing Self-Managed Integration
- Managing Self-Managed Integrations

### Overview

Self-Managed Integrations allow you to create and manage integrations directly within your CartonCloud account.

With the Self-Managed Etsy Integration, Etsy receipts in Paid status can create Outbound Orders in CartonCloud, and once dispatched, update the Etsy order to Completed while sending shipment tracking details back to Etsy (if fulfilment is enabled).

You can configure the integration yourself or you can have your customer set the integration up from their CartonCloud login. See [How to enable Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-enable-Customers-to-create-their-own-Self-Managed-Integrations).

### Prerequisites

- This is a paid integration, please ensure you read the included costs below.
- Your customer has an Etsy account and a configured Etsy shop.
- The SKU in Etsy matches the product codes in CartonCloud .
- The Customer in CartonCloud has access to the Warehouse the Etsy orders will be mapped to.
- If you are a Customer user, you must ensure your CartonCloud account owner has given you permission in your account to create your own Self-Managed Integrations. Please reach out to your account owner for this access.

### Limitations

- Changes to Etsy orders (e.g item quantity changes) will not be made in CartonCloud. Once CartonCloud has the order from Etsy, the order will not be updated if the order is changed within Etsy.
- Deleting a Sales Order in Etsy does not notify CartonCloud.
- Dates and datetimes are not converted between time zones.
- Mapping of requested batch numbers is not supported.
- Pickup orders are not currently supported. If this is important to your workflow, please reach out to the Service Desk team to discuss a possible workaround.

### Cost

We offer volume-based discounts—reach out to our support team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/contactsupport) to discuss pricing options.

### How to create a Self-Managed Etsy Integration

- Navigate to the Integrations page by typing in Integrations in the Search for Anything bar or More > Self-Managed Integrations.

- If an Admin user, select the customer you wish to create the integration for.
- Select Etsy from the Self-Managed Integrations menu selection.
- Click Configure .

- The configuration box will now appear, follow the below steps to configure the integration.

**(1) Initial Configuration**

- Fill in the Name field. ![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-23-2026-02-37-08-7113-AM.png?width=670&height=300&name=undefined-Mar-23-2026-02-37-08-7113-AM.png)
- Click Next.

**(2) Authentication**

- You will now need to connect CartonCloud to Etsy.
- Click Connect. ![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-23-2026-02-37-09-9876-AM.png?width=670&height=301&name=undefined-Mar-23-2026-02-37-09-9876-AM.png)

- You will be redirected to Etsy to authorize the connection.
- Once the connection is successful, you will see a confirmation screen. You can close the page and return to the CartonCloud Self-Managed Integration setup page.
- Click Next .

**(3) Order Creation**

- Here you will need to map which Etsy orders will go to which CartonCloud warehouse. ![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-23-2026-02-37-09-6251-AM.png?width=670&height=298&name=undefined-Mar-23-2026-02-37-09-6251-AM.png)

- Click Next.

**(4) Fulfilment**

- Complete Fulfilment through CartonCloud: When enabled Etsy Orders will be marked as Complete when the Sale Order is dispatched in CartonCloud.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-23-2026-02-37-08-3905-AM.png?width=670&height=296&name=undefined-Mar-23-2026-02-37-08-3905-AM.png)

- Click Finish.

### Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed Etsy Integration

If you need to cancel and disconnect the integration you will need to:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer .
- Click Etsy .
- Select the three-dot configuration icon and select Delete Integration.
- This will remove the integration and stop the billing of the integration to your account.

### Editing an existing Self-Managed Etsy Integration

To edit an existing Self-Managed Etsy Integration:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer .
- Click Etsy .
- Select Reconfigure .

### Managing Self-Managed Integrations

Because Self-Managed Integrations are a paid feature, it is important you are able to manage and keep track of the number of active integrations your customers have. This is useful if you wish to pass on the cost to your customer and reconcile your invoices.

If a Customer has a live integration they will have a green dot icon against their name. It will also display the number of active integrations for that customer below their name.

**![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-23-2026-02-37-09-0126-AM.png?width=670&height=145&name=undefined-Mar-23-2026-02-37-09-0126-AM.png)**
