<a id="self-managed-amazon-integration"></a>
## Self-Managed Amazon Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-amazon-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Prerequisites
- Key Considerations
- Cost
- How to create an Amazon Self-Managed Integration
- Amazon Address PII Handling
- Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed Amazon Integration
- Editing an existing Self-Managed Integration
- Managing Self-Managed Integrations

### Overview

Self-Managed Integrations allow you to create and manage integrations directly within your CartonCloud account.

With the Self-Managed Amazon Integration, Amazon orders automatically create Outbound Orders in CartonCloud, including customer details, products, and delivery requirements. Once the Outbound Order is dispatched in CartonCloud, shipment confirmation and tracking details are synced back to Amazon Seller Central.

You can configure the integration yourself or you can have your customer set the integration up from their CartonCloud login. See [How to enable Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-enable-Customers-to-create-their-own-Self-Managed-Integrations).

### Prerequisites

- This is a paid integration, please ensure you read the included costs below.
- Your customer has an Amazon Seller Central account.
- You know which Amazon Marketplace you are connecting (e.g. Australia, United States, Canada)
- The Seller SKU in Amazon matches the product codes in CartonCloud .
- The Customer in CartonCloud has access to the Warehouse the Amazon orders will be mapped to.
- If you are a Customer user, you must ensure your CartonCloud account owner has given you permission in your account to create your own Self-Managed Integrations. Please reach out to your account owner for this access.

### Key Considerations

- One Integration Per Marketplace
  - The authorisation process requires connecting the integration to a specific marketplace (e.g., Australia). However, order routing does not filter by the authorised marketplace. Instead, Supply Source Mapping is used to ensure that only the correct orders flow through to CartonCloud.
- Required Date Timezones
  - Amazon stores shipping dates as date and time values. CartonCloud converts these to a date by removing the time component when setting:

-
  -
    - Required Collection Date
    - Required Delivery Date
    - If your Amazon marketplace timezone differs from your CartonCloud warehouse timezone, the required date may appear one day earlier or later.

- Supported Marketplaces
  - We currently support Australia, United States and Canada marketplaces. If your marketplace is not listed above, please reach out to the Service Desk team for assistance.
- One-Time Fulfillment / Tracking Sync
  - The integration can only confirm a shipment once tracking details are available on the consignment. It will confirm a single package shipment back to Amazon for each consignment. Once confirmed, no further updates will be sent to Amazon for that shipment. This means no further updates are sent once the fulfillment sync has occurred — i.e., the first time tracking details are available and the Sale Order is in Dispatched status.

### Cost

We offer volume-based discounts—reach out to our support team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/contactsupport) to discuss pricing options.

### How to create a Self-Managed Amazon Integration

- Navigate to the Integrations page by typing in Integrations in the Search for Anything bar or More > Self-Managed Integrations.

- If an Admin user, select the customer you wish to create the integration for.
- Select Amazon from the Self-Managed Integrations menu selection.
- Click Configure .

- The configuration box will now appear, follow the below steps to configure the integration.

**(1) Initial Configuration**

- Fill in the Name field

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-17-3381-AM.png?width=670&height=385&name=undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-17-3381-AM.png)

- Click Next .

**(2) Authentication**

- Select your Marketplace country, then click Connect .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-18-1057-AM.png?width=670&height=386&name=undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-18-1057-AM.png)

- You will be redirected to Amazon Seller Central to authorize the connection.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-19-6660-AM.png?width=670&height=426&name=undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-19-6660-AM.png)

- Once the connection is successful, you will see the below confirmation screen. You can close the page and return to the CartonCloud Self-Managed Integration setup page.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-17-7405-AM.png?width=670&height=955&name=undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-17-7405-AM.png)

- Click Next .

Do not change the Marketplace on an active connection, as this will cause an error. To switch to a different Marketplace, you must first disconnect the existing connection.

**(3) Order Creation**

- You will now need to map which Amazon orders will go to which CartonCloud warehouse.

- The below describes the different options you have to map the Amazon orders to CartonCloud:
  - Default Warehouse: Select a CartonCloud warehouse to use for Amazon orders that doesn't have a matching Supply Source to Warehouse Mapping.

If you choose to set a default warehouse all orders will go to this warehouse unless you add Supply Source to Warehouse Mapping. You can also choose to ignore the default warehouse and only apply the warehouse mappings. This means only orders with specific references specified in the warehouse  mapping will come across to CartonCloud.

-
  - Supply Source to Warehouse Mapping: You can configure Supply Source to Warehouse mapping to control where orders should be routed to.

For each Amazon Supply Source, select which CartonCloud warehouse matching Orders should be created in, or leave blank to use the selected default.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-19-1070-AM.png?width=670&height=381&name=undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-19-1070-AM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-18-6432-AM.png?width=670&height=385&name=undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-18-6432-AM.png)

- Click Next .

The supply source list may include **inactive supply sources.** Please ensure you only select **active supply sources** when mapping to a CartonCloud warehouse.

**(4) Fulfilment**

- Fulfilment is enabled by default, but you can disable it if you do not want CartonCloud to send shipment confirmations and tracking information back to Amazon.

- When fulfilment is enabled, CartonCloud automatically updates the shipment confirmation status in Amazon when Sale Orders are dispatched in CartonCloud and tracking details are available on the Consignment.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-20-3039-AM.png?width=670&height=385&name=undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-20-3039-AM.png)

- Click Finish .

### Amazon Address PII Handling

CartonCloud automatically removes personally identifiable information (PII) from delivery addresses that originate from Amazon.

This ensures your integration remains compliant with Amazon’s data handling policies.

This functionality only applies to addresses originating from Amazon.

#### **When is address information cleared?**

CartonCloud removes personal details from Amazon addresses once all related activity is complete.

This happens when both order and delivery activity meet the conditions below:

**Sale Order Criteria**

All sale orders associated with the address must meet **at least one** of the following:

- The sale order was dispatched 30 or more days ago , or
- The sale order is in a rejected state and was last modified 7 or more days ago

**Consignment Criteria**

All consignments associated with the address must meet **at least one** of the following:

- The consignment delivery run date was 30 or more days ago , or
- The consignment is cancelled and was last modified 7 or more days ago

#### **What Address Fields Are Removed?**

When PII is cleared, the following fields are permanently removed:

- Contact Name
- Company Name
- Street Address
- Street Address Line 2
- Telephone
- Email
- Latitude and Longitude (geocoded coordinates)

Once cleared:

- The address remains inactive
- The address stays hidden from searches
- The data cannot be restored

### Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed Amazon Integration

If you need to cancel and disconnect the integration you will need to:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click Amazon.
- Select the three-dot configuration icon and select Delete Integration.
- This will remove the integration and stop the billing of the integration to your account.

### Editing an existing Self-Managed Amazon Integration

To edit an existing Self-Managed Amazon Integration:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click Amazon.
- Select Reconfigure.

### Managing Self-Managed Integrations

Because Self-Managed Integrations are a paid feature, it is important you are able to manage and keep track of the number of active integrations your customers have. This is useful if you wish to pass on the cost to your customer and reconcile your invoices.

If a Customer has a live integration they will have a green dot icon against their name. It will also display the number of active integrations for that customer below their name.

**![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-16-7838-AM.png?width=670&height=145&name=undefined-Mar-03-2026-01-54-16-7838-AM.png)**

<a id="self-managed-cin7-core-integration"></a>
## Self-Managed Cin7 Core Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-cin7-core-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Prerequisites
- Key Considerations
- Cost
- How to create a Self-Managed Cin7 Core Integration
- Disconnecting a Self-Managed Cin7 Core Integration
- Editing a Self-Managed Cin7 CoreIntegration
- Managing a Self-Managed Cin7 Core Integration

### Overview

Self-Managed Integrations allow you to create and manage integrations directly within your CartonCloud account.

The Cin7 Core Integration connects CartonCloud with your Cin7 Core account to automatically create Sale Orders and sync fulfilment and tracking information back to Cin7 (if fulfilment is enabled). When a sale is authorised in Cin7 Core, the integration automatically creates the corresponding sale order in CartonCloud.

You can configure the integration yourself or you can have your customer set the integration up from their CartonCloud login. See [How to enable Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-enable-Customers-to-create-their-own-Self-Managed-Integrations).

### Prerequisites

- You have an active Cin7 Core account.
- You have created a Cin7 API Client in Cin7 via External API setup. These can be created on the API setup page inside the Cin7 Core application: https://inventory.dearsystems.com/ExternalAPI .
- You have the following Cin7 Core API credentials:
  - Account ID
  - Application Key
- Your Cin7 subscription includes the Automation Module
- The Product SKUs in Cin7 Core match the product codes in CartonCloud.
- The Customer in CartonCloud has access to the Warehouse used in the integration.
- You have permission to create Self-Managed Integrations in CartonCloud.

### Cost

We offer volume-based discounts—reach out to our support team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/contactsupport) to discuss pricing options.

### Key Considerations

- Cin7 requires a Carrier to be supplied when creating a shipment. If the carrier does not already exist in Cin7, it will be created automatically when the fulfilment is created or updated. Tracking numbers and tracking URLs are sent from the CartonCloud consignment when available. If tracking details are not available, the carrier will be set to Undefined in Cin7.

### How to create a Self-Managed Cin7 Core Integration

- Navigate to the Integrations page by typing in Integrations in the Search for Anything bar or More > Self-Managed Integrations .
- If an Admin user, select the customer you wish to create the integration for.
- Select Cin7 Core from the Self-Managed Integrations menu selection.

- Click Configure .

- The configuration box will now appear, follow the below steps to configure the integration.

**(1) Initial Configuration**

- Fill in the Name field.
- Click Next .

**![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-22-2026-10-08-44-9298-PM.png?width=670&height=477&name=undefined-Mar-22-2026-10-08-44-9298-PM.png)**

**(2) Authentication**

- You will now need to connect CartonCloud to Cin7 Core.
- Enter the Account ID and th e Application Key from Cin7 Core. These can be created on the API setup page inside the Cin7 Core application: https://inventory.dearsystems.com/ExternalAPI .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-22-2026-10-08-44-6027-PM.png?width=670&height=474&name=undefined-Mar-22-2026-10-08-44-6027-PM.png)

- Click Next.

**(3) Order Creation**

- Here you will need to map which Cin7 Core orders will go to which CartonCloud warehouse.
- The below describes the different options you have to map the Cin7 Core orders to CartonCloud:
  - Default Warehouse: Select a CartonCloud warehouse to use for Cin7 Core orders that doesn't have a matching Location to Warehouse Mapping. If you choose to set a default warehouse, all orders will go to this warehouse unless you add Location to Warehouse Mapping. You can also choose to ignore the default warehouse and only apply the warehouse mappings. This means only orders with specific references specified in the warehouse mapping will come across to CartonCloud.
  - Location to Warehouse Mapping: You can configure Location to Warehouse Mapping to control where orders should be routed to. For each Location, select which CartonCloud warehouse Sale Orders should be created in, or leave blank to use the selected default.

Only top-level locations are displayed. Bin and sublocations will not appear.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-22-2026-10-08-46-0529-PM.png?width=670&height=477&name=undefined-Mar-22-2026-10-08-46-0529-PM.png)

- Click Next.

**(3) Fulfillment**

- Complete Fulfilment through CartonCloud: When enabled Cin7 Core Orders will be marked as complete when the Sale Order is dispatched in CartonCloud.

- Tracking Information: Tracking information will be sent to Cin7 Core when the order is dispatched, and will be updated when tracking details change.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-22-2026-10-08-45-5528-PM.png?width=670&height=475&name=undefined-Mar-22-2026-10-08-45-5528-PM.png)

- Click Finish.

### Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed Cin7 Core Integration

If you need to cancel and disconnect the integration you will need to:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click Cin7 Core .
- Select the three-dot configuration icon and select Delete Integration.
- This will remove the integration and stop the billing of the integration to your account.

### Editing an existing Self-Managed Cin7 Core Integration

To edit an existing Self-Managed Cin7 Core Integration:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer .
- Click Cin7 Core .
- Select Reconfigure .

### Managing Self-Managed Integrations

Because Self-Managed Integrations are a paid feature, it is important you are able to manage and keep track of the number of active integrations your customers have. This is useful if you wish to pass on the cost to your customer and reconcile your invoices.

If a Customer has a live integration they will have a green dot icon against their name. It will also display the number of active integrations for that customer below their name.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-22-2026-10-08-44-3242-PM.png?width=670&height=145&name=undefined-Mar-22-2026-10-08-44-3242-PM.png)

<a id="self-managed-ebay-integration"></a>
## Self-Managed eBay Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-ebay-integration_

### Table of Contents

- [Overview](https://help.cartoncloud.com#overview)
- [Prerequisites](https://help.cartoncloud.com#prerequisites)
- [Key Considerations](https://help.cartoncloud.com#key-considerations)
- [How to create a Self-Managed eBay Integration](https://help.cartoncloud.com#How-to-create-a-Self-Managed-eBay-Integration)
- [eBay Address PII Handling](https://help.cartoncloud.com#ebay-address-pii-handling)
- [Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed eBay Integration](https://help.cartoncloud.com#Disconnecting-an-existing-Self-Managed-eBay-Integr)
- [Editing an existing Self-Managed Integration](https://help.cartoncloud.com#Editing-an-existing-Self-Managed-eBay-Integration)
- [Managing Self-Managed Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com#managing-self-managed-integrations)

### Overview

Self-Managed Integrations allow you to create and manage integrations directly within your CartonCloud account.

With the Self-Managed eBay Integration, eBay orders automatically create Sale Orders in CartonCloud. Once the Sale Order is dispatched in CartonCloud, shipment confirmation and consignment tracking details are synced back to eBay (if configured).

You can configure the integration yourself or you can have your customer set the integration up from their CartonCloud login. See [How to enable Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-enable-Customers-to-create-their-own-Self-Managed-Integrations).

### Prerequisites

- This is a paid integration, please ensure you read the included costs below.
- Your customer has an eBay account.
- The SKU in eBay matches the [product codes in CartonCloud](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Add-a-Product).
- The Customer in CartonCloud has access to the [Warehouse](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Customer-Settings-Warehouse) the eBay orders will be mapped to.
- If you are a Customer user, you must ensure your CartonCloud account owner has given you permission in your account to create your own Self-Managed Integrations. Please reach out to your account owner for this access.

### Key Considerations

- **Warehouse Mapping**The integration provides the ability to map only to a single Warehouse. This means all orders are going to be attempted to be accepted into CartonCloud.
- **Carrier Tracking Updates**eBay has strict validation on the carrier tracking details supplied to fulfillment. If tracking information is invalid, the service may retry creating the fulfillment without the tracking information supplied from the CartonCloud consignment.
- **Order Change Notifications**eBay does not currently send automatic notifications when orders are updated. The integration identifies new or modified orders by polling the eBay API every 30 minutes. Only orders with a fulfillment status of NOT_STARTED that were either created after the integration was deployed or modified since the last sync will be retrieved.

### Cost

We offer volume-based discounts—reach out to our support team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/contactsupport) to discuss pricing options.

### How to create a Self-Managed eBay Integration

- Navigate to the Integrations page by typing in **Integrations**in the **Search for Anything bar** or **More > Self-Managed Integrations.**

- If an Admin user, select the customer you wish to create the integration for.

- Select eBay from the Self-Managed Integrations menu selection.
- Click **Configure**.

- The configuration box will now appear, follow the below steps to configure the integration.

**(1) Initial Configuration**

- Fill in the Name field.

**![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-57-2767-AM.png?width=670&height=444&name=undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-57-2767-AM.png)**

- Click Next.

**(2) Authentication**

- You will now need to connect CartonCloud to eBay.
- Click Connect.

**![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-56-8482-AM.png?width=670&height=442&name=undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-56-8482-AM.png)**

- You will be redirected to eBay to authorize the connection.

- Once the connection is successful, you will see the below confirmation screen. You can close the page and return to the CartonCloud Self-Managed Integration setup page.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-58-4865-AM.png?width=325&height=464&name=undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-58-4865-AM.png)

**![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-58-8387-AM.png?width=670&height=477&name=undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-58-8387-AM.png)**

- Click Next .

**(3) Order Creation**

- Here you will need to map which eBay orders will go to which CartonCloud warehouse.

**![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-59-4154-AM.png?width=670&height=478&name=undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-59-4154-AM.png)**

- Click Next.

**(4) Fulfilment**

- Complete Fulfilment through CartonCloud: when enabled, eBay Orders will be marked as complete when the Sale Order is dispatched in CartonCloud.
- If fulfilment information is updated after the order is dispatched, CartonCloud will update the eBay tracking details.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-57-9205-AM.png?width=670&height=474&name=undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-57-9205-AM.png)

- Click Finish.

### eBay Address PII Handling

CartonCloud automatically removes personally identifiable information (PII) from delivery addresses that originate from eBay.

This ensures your integration remains compliant with eBay’s data handling policies.

This functionality only applies to addresses originating from eBay.

**When is address information cleared?**

CartonCloud removes personal details from eBay addresses once all related activity is complete.

This happens when both order and delivery activity meet the conditions below:

#### **Sale Order Criteria**

All sale orders associated with the address must meet **at least one** of the following:

- The sale order was dispatched 30 or more days ago , or
- The sale order is in a rejected state and was last modified 7 or more days ago

#### **Consignment Criteria**

All consignments associated with the address must meet **at least one** of the following:

- The consignment delivery run date was 30 or more days ago , or
- The consignment is cancelled and was last modified 7 or more days ago

**What Address Fields Are Removed?**

When PII is cleared, the following fields are permanently removed:

- Contact Name
- Company Name
- Street Address
- Street Address Line 2
- Telephone
- Email
- Latitude and Longitude (geocoded coordinates)

Once cleared:

- The address remains inactive
- The address stays hidden from searches
- The data cannot be restored

### Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed eBay Integration

If you need to cancel and disconnect the integration you will need to:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click eBay.
- Select the three-dot configuration icon and select Delete Integration.
- This will remove the integration and stop the billing of the integration to your account.

### Editing an existing Self-Managed eBay Integration

To edit an existing Self-Managed eBay Integration:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click eBay.
- Select Reconfigure.

### Managing Self-Managed Integrations

Because Self-Managed Integrations are a paid feature, it is important you are able to manage and keep track of the number of active integrations your customers have. This is useful if you wish to pass on the cost to your customer and reconcile your invoices.

If a Customer has a live integration they will have a green dot icon against their name. It will also display the number of active integrations for that customer below their name.

**![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-57-6754-AM.png?width=670&height=145&name=undefined-Mar-11-2026-02-32-57-6754-AM.png)**

## Self-Managed Integrations

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-integrations_

### Table of Contents

- What are Self-Managed Integrations?
- How to access Self-Managed Integrations
  - As an Admin User
  - As a Customer User
- What Self-Managed Integrations are available?

### What are Self-Managed Integrations?

Self-Managed Integrations allow you to create integrations from within your CartonCloud account. You can configure the integration yourself, or your customer can do so from their own CartonCloud login.

Please note that this is a paid integration and will be billable to your CartonCloud account.

### How to access Self-Managed Integrations

#### As an Admin user

- Navigate to the Integrations page by typing in **Integrations** in the **Search for Anything** bar or **More**>**Self-Managed Integrations**.
- Click on the customer you wish to create the integration for.

![self-managed-integrations-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-integrations-0.png?width=670&height=280&name=self-managed-integrations-0.png)

- Select the app you wish to connect to or the integration you wish to view.

![self-managed-integrations-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-integrations-1.png?width=670&height=337&name=self-managed-integrations-1.png)

#### As a Customer user

- Navigate to the Integrations page **More** > **Self-Managed** **Integrations**.
- Select the app you wish to connect to or the integration you wish to view.

![self-managed-integrations-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-integrations-1.png?width=670&height=337&name=self-managed-integrations-1.png)

<a id="self-managed-shopify-integration"></a>
## Self-Managed Shopify Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-shopify-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Prerequisites
- Limitations
- Cost
- Available Workflow
- How to create a Self-Managed Shopify Integration
- Testing
- Disconnecting a Self-Managed Shopify Integration
- Editing an existing Self-Managed Shopify Integration
- Managing Self-Managed Integrations
- Troubleshooting Steps

### Overview

Self-Managed Integrations allow you to create integrations from within your CartonCloud account. With the Self-Managed Shopify Integration, orders from your Shopify account can create Sale Orders in CartonCloud and once packed, can mark the order in Shopify as fulfilled along with carrier tracking numbers (if configured).

You can set up multiple instances of the Self-Managed Shopify Integration for a Customer. Each instance creates a separate Shopify connection, which allows you to connect multiple Shopify stores or configure multiple integrations for the same customer where required. Each active instance is billed as a separate integration.

You can configure the integration yourself or you can have your customer set the integration up from their CartonCloud login. See [How to enable Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-enable-customers-to-create-their-own-self-managed-integrations).

### Prerequisites

- This is a paid integration, please ensure you read the included costs below.
- Your customer must have a Shopify account.
- You will need your customer’s Shopify store url and Shopify Store login credentials (which have the permission '*Manage and install apps and channels'* enabled). Alternatively, you can enable the permission for your Customer to create their own Shopify Integration.
- The product SKU in Shopify must match the [product codes in CartonCloud](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Add-a-Product).
- The following [Custom Fields](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Introduction-to-Custom-Fields)are optional, but should you wish to use them, they must be set up before building the integration and only Custom Fields with the "Field Type" Text are accepted:
  - Shopify Order Shipment Method Field : Sale Order Custom Field
- The following fields are automatically populated and created by the integration:
  - Carrier Name Field
  - Carrier Tracking Number Field
  - Carrier Tracking URL Field
- The Customer in CartonCloud must have access to the [Warehouse](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Customer-Settings-Warehouse) the orders are being mapped to from Shopify.
- If you are a Customer user, you must ensure your CartonCloud account owner has given you permission in your account to create your own Self-Managed Integrations. Please reach out to your account owner for this access.

### Limitations

- Once an order has been imported into CartonCloud from Shopify, it is generally not automatically updated if changes are made in Shopify. In cases where fulfilment groups or fulfilment IDs change, Shopify may treat the order differently, which can result in CartonCloud creating a new order rather than updating the existing one.
- If an order is originally from a location in Shopify that is not a CartonCloud mapped location, and it then changes to a CartonCloud mapped location, CartonCloud will not be notified of this order.
- The integration automatically identifies the whether the order is a Pick-up or Delivery. The Shopify store owner will need to ensure they have enabled "Pick-up" for the Shopify location: https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/fulfillment/setup/delivery-methods/pickup-in-store

### Cost

We offer volume-based discounts—reach out to our support team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/contactsupport) to discuss pricing options.

### Available Workflow

- A Shopify order creates a Sale Order in CartonCloud.
- When marked “Packed”, the Sale Order in CartonCloud marks the order as fulfilled in Shopify (with carrier tracking details if setup).

### How to create a Self-Managed Shopify Integration

- Navigate to the Integrations page by typing in **Integrations** in the **Search for Anything** bar or **More**>**Self-Managed Integrations**.
- If an Admin user, select the customer you wish to create the integration for.
- Select Shopify from the Self-Managed Integrations menu selection.

![self-managed-shopify-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-shopify-integration-0.png?width=670&height=260&name=self-managed-shopify-integration-0.png)

- Click **Configure**.

- The configuration box will now appear, follow the below steps to configure the integration.

**(1) Initial Configuration**

- Fill in the Name field. Ensure the name includes the name of the customer. If you are creating a Shopify integration for multiple customers you will need to be able to easily identify the different integrations.
- Click Next .

![self-managed-shopify-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-shopify-integration-1.png?width=670&height=245&name=self-managed-shopify-integration-1.png)

**(2) Authentication**

- You will now need to connect CartonCloud to the correct Shopify account.Click Connect against the CartonCloud tile. Once the status dot icon next to the CartonCloud logo has turned green the connection has been successful.

![self-managed-shopify-integration-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-shopify-integration-2.png?width=670&height=247&name=self-managed-shopify-integration-2.png)

- To connect Shopify, you will need your Customer’s Shopify store domain. This can be found in the url of the Shopify account. You will only need to include the url after store/. Replace YOUR-SHOPIFY-DOMAIN with your Shopify store domain.

![self-managed-shopify-integration-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-shopify-integration-3.png?width=670&height=149&name=self-managed-shopify-integration-3.png)

- Click **Connect**.
- You will be prompted to log into the Customer’s Shopify account. You will require the Customer’s Shopify login credentials.
- Once the status dot icon has turned green the connection has been successful.
- Click **Next**.

![self-managed-shopify-integration-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-shopify-integration-4.png?width=670&height=247&name=self-managed-shopify-integration-4.png)

**(3) Order Creation**

- Here you will need to set up configurations to enable order creation from Shopify to CartonCloud. In addition you will be able to map the Custom Fields set up in your CartonCloud account to the necessary fields in Shopify. This is an important step and if not done correctly the integration will not work. Ensure you have read the pre-requisites and have the required Custom Fields set up.
  - Require Payment Prior to Sale Order Creation: with this enabled only orders that are paid in Shopify will be created in CartonCloud.
  - Location to Warehouse Mapping: select the correct Shopify Location against each CartonCloud Warehouse. A Shopify Location is any physical place or app where you either sell products, shop or fulfil orders or stock inventory. By mapping the locations to your Warehouse Locations, Shopify will know what orders to send to which CartonCloud warehouses.
  - Shopify Order Shipment Method Field: select the correct Sale Order Custom Field that holds the shipment method information. This field is optional.
  - Shopify Order ID Field : select the correct Sale Order Custom Field from the drop down menu. This is the Sale Order Custom Field in CartonCloud that holds the Shopify Order ID.  This field is mandatory.
- Click Next .

![self-managed-shopify-integration-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-shopify-integration-5.png?width=670&height=247&name=self-managed-shopify-integration-5.png)

**(4) Fulfilment**

- Complete Fulfilment through CartonCloud: enabled this will create Fulfilments in Shopify once the Sale Order is packed in CartonCloud.
- Notify Customer of Fulfilment : with this enabled the order recipient will be notified by Shopify when the order has been fulfilled
- Carrier Name Field: select the correct Sale Order Custom Field that holds the carrier information. This field is optional.
- Carrier Tracking Number Field: select the correct Sale Order Custom Field that holds the carrier tracking number information. This field is optional.
- Carrier Tracking URL Field: Outbound Order custom field to retrieve the Carrier Tracking URL.

![self-managed-shopify-integration-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-shopify-integration-6.png?width=670&height=247&name=self-managed-shopify-integration-6.png)

### Testing

Once you have created the Self-Managed Shopify Integration it is suggested that you test the integration with a[test order](https://help.shopify.com/en/manual/checkout-settings/test-orders).

If you have any questions or issues please contact support via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket).

### Disconnecting a Self-Managed Shopify Integration

If you need to cancel and disconnect the integration you will need to:

- Navigate to the **Integrations** page.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click **Shopify**.
- Select the three-dot configuration icon and select **Delete** Integration.
- This will remove the integration and stop the billing of the integration to your account.

![self-managed-shopify-integration-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-shopify-integration-7.png?width=375&height=411&name=self-managed-shopify-integration-7.png)

### Editing an existing Self-Managed Shopify Integration

To edit an existing Self-Managed Xero Integration:

- Navigate to the **Integrations** page.
- Select the relevant **Customer**.
- Click **Shopify Orders**.
- Scroll down to Instances.
- Select **Reconfigure**.

![self-managed-shopify-integration-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-shopify-integration-8.png?width=296&height=353&name=self-managed-shopify-integration-8.png)

### Managing Self-Managed Integrations

Because Self-Managed Integrations are a paid feature, it is important you are able to manage and keep track of the number of active integrations your customer's have. This is useful if you wish to pass on the cost to your customer and reconcile your invoices.

If a Customer has a live integration they will have a green dot icon against their name. It will also display the number of active integrations for that customer below their name.

![self-managed-shopify-integration-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-shopify-integration-9.png?width=670&height=145&name=self-managed-shopify-integration-9.png)

### Troubleshooting Steps

If you are experiencing issues with your Self-Managed Integration and orders are not coming through to CartonCloud then you will need to check the Import Log for why the orders are failing. See [Import Log](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/parsing-log)[https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Parsing-Log](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Parsing-Log) for information on how to read the Import Log and diagnose the issue.

Other things to check include:

- Is the Warehouse to Shopify Location Mapping you have set up match the Location set up in Shopify? Is there a new Shopify Location that is not yet configured in your mapping?

For Shopify specific troubleshooting steps please see [Self-Managed Shopify Troubleshooting](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/shopify-integration-troubleshooting)

If you require further assistance with your Self-Managed Xero Integration please reach out to the team for assistance via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/contactsupport).

<a id="self-managed-shopify-troubleshooting"></a>
## Self-Managed Shopify Troubleshooting

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-shopify-troubleshooting_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Common Issues Check 1
- Common Issues Check 2
- Common Issues Check 3
- Requests for Support Help

### Purpose

This guide will provide troubleshooting steps to resolve common issues encountered when setting up your Self-Managed Shopify Integration that may be preventing orders from flowing through to Carton Cloud from Shopify.

### Common issues Check 1

Incorrect URL entered in Step 2 of the configuration. Make sure to double check that you have entered your Customers Shopify store domain correctly.

Replace YOUR-SHOPIFY-DOMAIN with your Shopify store domain into the Authorize URL, Host and Token URL field. The URL must exactly match what is shown in the URL when logged into the admin view of Shopify.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Dec-10-2025-09-42-16-1220-PM.png?width=587&height=411&name=image-png-Dec-10-2025-09-42-16-1220-PM.png)

### Common issues Check 2

Shopify Location to Carton Cloud Warehouse Mapping not complete in step 3 of the configuration. Make sure that you have selected a Carton Cloud Warehouse from the drop down for each Shopify Location listed.

If there is no Carton Cloud Warehouse selected for a listed Shopify Location, orders from this Shopify Location will not flow through to the Carton Cloud Warehouse.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Dec-10-2025-09-40-07-4929-PM.png?width=670&height=467&name=image-png-Dec-10-2025-09-40-07-4929-PM.png)

### Common Issues Check 3

When setting up the Location within Shopify a Delivery Method is selected. The only Delivery Methods supported at this time are as follows:

- pick_up: A delivery that a customer picks up at your retail store, curbside, or any location that you choose.
- shipping: A delivery to a customer using a shipping carrier.

If any other Delivery Method for the Location is selected, an error will be recieved (Delivery Method Not Supported Ignoring Fulfilment Order with unsupported delivery method) and the order will not flow through the integration.

### Requests for Support Help

If you have completed the above troubleshooting steps and the issue of orders flowing from Shopify to Carton Cloud has not resolved please reach out to our Support team and provide the following required information:

- A full page screenshot, from an Admin login, of a Shopify Sale Order which is not importing to CartonCloud
- Must show the URL, Order History (fully exposed) and Address Details

**![self-managed-shopify-troubleshooting-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-shopify-troubleshooting-2.png?width=482&height=41&name=self-managed-shopify-troubleshooting-2.png)**

**![self-managed-shopify-troubleshooting-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-shopify-troubleshooting-3.png?width=392&height=393&name=self-managed-shopify-troubleshooting-3.png)**

---

<a id="self-managed-unleashed-integration"></a>
## Self-Managed Unleashed Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-unleashed-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Prerequisites
- Limitations
- Cost
- How to create a Self-Managed Unleashed Integration
- Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed Unleashed Integration
- Editing an existing Self-Managed Unleased Integration
- Managing Self-Managed Integrations

### Overview

Self-Managed Integrations allow you to create integrations from within your CartonCloud account.

To use the Self-Managed Unleashed Integration, a Sales Order in Placed status and Sales Shipment must exist in Unleashed. CartonCloud will create the corresponding Sales Order and, once dispatched, mark the Sales Shipment as fulfilled with carrier tracking numbers (if configured).

You can configure the integration yourself or you can have your customer set the integration up from their CartonCloud login. See [How to enable Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-enable-Customers-to-create-their-own-Self-Managed-Integrations).

### Prerequisites

- This is a paid integration, please ensure you read the included costs below.
- Your customer must have an Unleashed account.
- You will need your customer’s Unleashed API ID and Private Key. Alternatively, you can enable the permission for your Customer to create their own Unleashed Integration. See[here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-enable-Customers-to-create-their-own-Self-Managed-Integrations) for more information.
- The product code in Unleashed must match the [product codes in CartonCloud](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Add-a-Product).
- The Customer in CartonCloud must have access to the [Warehouse](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Customer-Settings-Warehouse) the orders are being mapped to from Unleashed.
- If you are a Customer user, you must ensure your CartonCloud account owner has given you permission in your account to create your own Self-Managed Integrations. Please reach out to your account owner for this access.

### Limitations

- Changes to Unleashed orders (e.g. item quantity changes) will not be made in CartonCloud. Once CartonCloud has the order from Unleashed, the order will not be updated if the order is changed within Unleashed.
- Orders created via the Unleashed integration cannot be split.
- Fulfilments requires [Warehouse Fulfilments](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Consignment-Types-Warehouse-Fulfilments) to be enabled in CartonCloud.
- Deleting a Sales Order or Sales Shipment in Unleashed does not notify CartonCloud.
- Dates and datetimes are not converted between time zones.
- Mapping of requested batch numbers is not supported.
- Customer Reference mapping is currently unavailable.
- Pickup orders are not currently supported. If this is important to your workflow, please reach out to the Service Desk team to discuss a possible workaround.

### Cost

We offer volume-based discounts—reach out to our support team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/contactsupport) to discuss pricing options.

### How to create a Self-Managed Unleashed Integration

- Navigate to the Integrations page by typing in **Integrations** in the **Search for Anything** bar or **More**>**Self-Managed Integrations**.
- If an Admin user, select the customer you wish to create the integration for.
- Select **Unleashed**from the **Self-Managed Integrations** menu selection.

![self-managed-unleashed-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-unleashed-integration-0.png?width=670&height=242&name=self-managed-unleashed-integration-0.png)

- Click **Configure**.
- The configuration box will now appear, follow the below steps to configure the integration.

**(1) Initial Configuration**

- Fill in the Name field

![self-managed-unleashed-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-unleashed-integration-1.png?width=670&height=410&name=self-managed-unleashed-integration-1.png)

- Click **Next.**

**(2) Authentication**

- You will now need to connect CartonCloud to the correct Unleashed account.
- Enter the Unleashed **API ID** and **API Key**. You can find these in Unleashed under **Integration**→ **Unleashed API Access**.

![self-managed-unleashed-integration-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-unleashed-integration-2.png?width=670&height=398&name=self-managed-unleashed-integration-2.png)

- Click Next.

**(3) Order Creation**

- Here you will need to set up configurations to enable order creation from Unleashed to CartonCloud.
  - **Include Comments**: with this enabled. Comments from Unleashed Sales Order and Shipment will be passed through to CartonCloud **Packing instructions**.

![self-managed-unleashed-integration-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-unleashed-integration-3.png?width=670&height=399&name=self-managed-unleashed-integration-3.png)

- The CartonCloud Customer Reference field is automatically populated using Unleashed’s Order Number and Shipment Number, in the following format: **{order number} | {shipment number}**.

- You will now need to map which Unleashed orders will go to which CartonCloud warehouse. The below describes the different options you have to map the Unleashed orders to CartonCloud:
  - **Default Warehouse:** Select a CartonCloud warehouse to use for Unleashed Sales Shipment that doesn't have a matching Warehouse mapping If you choose to set a default warehouse all orders will go to this warehouse unless you add **Warehouse Mappings**. You can also choose to ignore the default warehouse and only apply the warehouse mappings. This means only orders with specific references specified in the warehouse  mapping will come across to CartonCloud.

![self-managed-unleashed-integration-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-unleashed-integration-4.png?width=670&height=399&name=self-managed-unleashed-integration-4.png)

- **Warehouse Mappings:**For each Unleashed Sales Shipments, select which CartonCloud warehouse matching Sales Shipments should be created in, or leave blank to use the selected **Default Warehouse**.

![self-managed-unleashed-integration-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-unleashed-integration-5.png?width=670&height=396&name=self-managed-unleashed-integration-5.png)

- Click **Next.**

**(3) Fulfillment**

- When enabled, Unleashed Sales Shipments will be marked as complete when the Sale Order is dispatched in CartonCloud.  If fulfilment information is updated after the order is dispatched, CartonCloud will update the Unleashed tracking details.

If the connected Unleashed account has **Order Management switched off**:

- **Sales Shipments cannot be updated** to a “Dispatched” Shipment Status by the integration when CartonCloud Sales Orders are dispatched. *(This is intended behavior, limited by Unleashed.)*
- The **dispatched date** and **number of packages** will still be updated on the Sales Shipment during the fulfilment sync.

![self-managed-unleashed-integration-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-unleashed-integration-6.png?width=670&height=395&name=self-managed-unleashed-integration-6.png)

- Click **Finish.**

### Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed Unleashed Integration

If you need to cancel and disconnect the integration you will need to:

- Navigate to the **Integrations** page.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click **Unleashed**.
- Select the three-dot configuration icon and select **Delete** Integration.
- This will remove the integration and stop the billing of the integration to your account.

### Editing an existing Self-Managed Unleashed Integration

To edit an existing Self-Managed Unleashed Integration:

- Navigate to the **Integrations** page.
- Select the relevant **Customer**.
- Click **Unleashed**.
- Select **Reconfigure**.

### Managing Self-Managed Integrations

Because Self-Managed Integrations are a paid feature, it is important you are able to manage and keep track of the number of active integrations your customers have. This is useful if you wish to pass on the cost to your customer and reconcile your invoices.

If a Customer has a live integration they will have a green dot icon against their name. It will also display the number of active integrations for that customer below their name.

![self-managed-unleashed-integration-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-unleashed-integration-7.png?width=670&height=145&name=self-managed-unleashed-integration-7.png)

---

<a id="self-managed-walmart-marketplace-us-integration"></a>
## Self-Managed Walmart Marketplace US Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-walmart-marketplace-us-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Prerequisites
- Cost
- Key Considerations
- How to create a Self-Managed Walmart Marketplace US Integration
- Disconnecting a Self-Managed Walmart Integration
- Editing a Self-Managed Walmart Integration
- Managing a Self-Managed Walmart Integration

### Overview

Self-Managed Integrations allow you to create and manage integrations directly within your CartonCloud account.

The Walmart Marketplace US Integration connects CartonCloud with your Walmart Marketplace US seller account to automatically create CartonCloud Sale Orders from Walmart orders. When a Walmart order is created, the integration creates the corresponding Sale Order in CartonCloud.

The integration will also sync fulfilment and tracking information back to Walmart when fulfilment is enabled. When the Sale Order is dispatched in CartonCloud and tracking details are added to the consignment, Walmart is updated with the shipment details and tracking information.

You can configure the integration yourself, or you can have your customer set the integration up from their CartonCloud login. See How to enable Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations.

### Prerequisites

- You have an active Walmart Marketplace US seller account.
- You have permission to connect apps or integrations in Walmart Marketplace.
- You have permission to create Self-Managed Integrations in CartonCloud.
- The Product SKUs in Walmart Marketplace match the product codes in CartonCloud.
- The Customer in CartonCloud has access to the Warehouse used in the integration.
- Your Walmart fulfilment centers are active and available in Walmart Marketplace.

### Cost

We offer volume-based discounts. Reach out to our support team to discuss pricing options.

### Key Considerations

- The Walmart Purchase Order ID is used as the CartonCloud customer reference .
- Orders are routed to CartonCloud warehouses using Walmart Fulfillment Center to CartonCloud Warehouse Mapping. If a matching fulfillment center is not mapped, the selected default warehouse will be used.
- The integration can acknowledge Walmart orders once the CartonCloud Sale Order progresses beyond early statuses such as Draft, Awaiting Stock, or Rejected.
- Fulfilment updates are sent to Walmart when the CartonCloud Sale Order is dispatched and tracking details are available.
- Tracking numbers and tracking URLs are sent to Walmart when available. Tracking details can also be updated in Walmart if they change after the initial dispatch.
- Walmart requires supported carrier information for shipment updates. If the carrier is not recognised, a tracking URL must be available so the carrier can be sent as an “other carrier”.
- Manually editing products & quantities on imported Sale Orders is not supported, as it breaks the link with Walmart’s references.

### How to create a Self-Managed Walmart Marketplace US Integration

- Navigate to the Integrations page by typing Integrations in the Search for Anything bar , or go to More > Self-Managed Integrations .
- If you are an Admin user, select the customer you wish to create the integration for.
- Select Walmart Marketplace US from the Self-Managed Integrations menu selection.
- Click Configure .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-15-2026-11-09-45-5376-PM.png?width=670&height=396&name=undefined-Jun-15-2026-11-09-45-5376-PM.png)

- The configuration box will now appear. Follow the steps below to configure the integration.

**(1) Initial Configuration**

- Fill in the Name field.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-15-2026-11-09-48-3415-PM.png?width=670&height=384&name=undefined-Jun-15-2026-11-09-48-3415-PM.png)

- Click Next .

**(2) Authentication**

- You will now need to connect CartonCloud to Walmart Marketplace US.
- Click Connect and log in to your Walmart Marketplace seller account.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-15-2026-11-09-46-6745-PM.png?width=670&height=386&name=undefined-Jun-15-2026-11-09-46-6745-PM.png)

- Review the scopes necessary for the integration and proceed by clicking “Authorize”

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-15-2026-11-09-46-1637-PM.png?width=670&height=449&name=undefined-Jun-15-2026-11-09-46-1637-PM.png)

- Once redirected to a successful connection page you can close it and go back to the config wizard.
- Click Next .

**(3) Order Creation**

Here you will need to map which Walmart Marketplace US orders will go to which CartonCloud warehouse.

-
  - Default Warehouse: Select a CartonCloud warehouse to use for Walmart orders that do not have a matching Fulfillment Center to Warehouse Mapping. If you choose to set a default warehouse, all orders will go to this warehouse unless you add Fulfillment Center to Warehouse Mapping.

-
  - Fulfillment Center to Warehouse Mapping: Configure mappings to control where orders should be routed. For each Walmart Fulfillment Center, select which CartonCloud warehouse Sale Orders should be created in, or leave blank to use the selected default.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-15-2026-11-09-47-8013-PM.png?width=670&height=389&name=undefined-Jun-15-2026-11-09-47-8013-PM.png)

- Click Next .

**(4) Fulfilment**

- Complete Fulfilment through CartonCloud: When enabled, Walmart Marketplace US orders will be marked as fulfilled when the Sale Order is dispatched in CartonCloud and tracking details are available.
- Tracking Information: Tracking information will be sent to Walmart when the order is dispatched, and will be updated if tracking details change.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Jun-15-2026-11-09-47-1925-PM.png?width=670&height=389&name=undefined-Jun-15-2026-11-09-47-1925-PM.png)

- Click Finish .

### Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed Walmart Marketplace US Integration

If you need to cancel and disconnect the integration you will need to:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click Walmart Marketplace US .
- Select the three-dot configuration icon and select Delete Integration.
- This will remove the integration and stop the billing of the integration to your account.

### Editing an existing Self-Managed Walmart Marketplace US Integration

To edit an existing Walmart Integration:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer .
- Click Walmart Marketplace US .
- Select Reconfigure .

### Managing Self-Managed Integrations

Because Self-Managed Integrations are a paid feature, it is important you are able to manage and keep track of the number of active integrations your customers have. This is useful if you wish to pass on the cost to your customer and reconcile your invoices.

If a Customer has a live integration they will have a green dot icon against their name. It will also display the number of active integrations for that customer below their name.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Mar-22-2026-10-08-44-3242-PM.png?width=670&height=145&name=undefined-Mar-22-2026-10-08-44-3242-PM.png)

<a id="self-managed-woocommerce-integration-"></a>
## Self-Managed WooCommerce Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-woocommerce-integration-_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Prerequisites
- Limitations
- Cost
- How to create a Self-Managed WooCommerce Integration
- Disconnecting a Self-Managed WooCommerce Integration
- Editing a Self-Managed WooCommerce Integration
- Managing a Self-Managed WooCommerce Integration

### Overview

Please note the Self-Managed WooCommerce Integration is currently in Beta. If you have any issues or questions, please reach out to the team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/contactsupport).

Self-Managed Integrations allow you to create and manage integrations directly within your CartonCloud account.

With the Self-Managed WooCommerce Integration, orders in WooCommerce will automatically create Outbound Orders in CartonCloud when the WooCommerce order reaches Processing status. Once the CartonCloud Outbound Order is Dispatched, the WooCommerce order will be updated to Completed.

If the WooCommerce store has a Shipment Tracking plugin installed and activated, CartonCloud will also send shipment tracking updates back to WooCommerce when the Outbound Order is moved to Packed or Dispatched, or when consignment tracking details are updated.

You can configure the integration yourself or you can have your customer set the integration up from their CartonCloud login. See [How to enable Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/How-to-enable-Customers-to-create-their-own-Self-Managed-Integrations).

### Prerequisites

- This is a paid integration, please ensure you read the included costs below.
- Your customer must have a WooCommerce account.
- The customer must create a new WooCommerce REST API key with Read/Write permissions to allow CartonCloud to create orders, update order statuses, and send shipment tracking information.
- The Product SKU in WooCommerce must match the product codes in CartonCloud .
- The Customer in CartonCloud must have access to the Warehouse the orders are being mapped to from WooCommerce. .
- If you are a Customer user, you must ensure your CartonCloud account owner has given you permission in your account to create your own Self-Managed Integrations. Please reach out to your account owner for this access.

### Limitations

- Changes to WooCommerce orders (e.g item quantity changes) will not be made in CartonCloud. Once CartonCloud has the order from WooCommerce, the order will not be updated if the order is changed within WooCommerce.
- Deleting a Sales Order in WooCommerce does not notify CartonCloud.
- Dates and datetimes are not converted between time zones.
- Mapping of requested batch numbers is not supported.
- Pickup orders are not currently supported. If this is important to your workflow, please reach out to the Service Desk team to discuss a possible workaround.

### Cost

We offer volume-based discounts—reach out to our support team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/contactsupport) to discuss pricing options.

### How to create a Self-Managed WooCommerce Integration

- Navigate to the Integrations page by typing in Integrations in the Search for Anything bar or More > Self-Managed Integrations .
- If an Admin user, select the customer you wish to create the integration for.
- Select WooCommerce from the Self-Managed Integrations menu selection.

- Click Configure .

- The configuration box will now appear, follow the below steps to configure the integration.

**(1) Initial Configuration**

- Fill in the Name field.
- Click Next .

**(2) Authentication**

- You will now need to connect CartonCloud to WooCommerce.
- In the Store URL field, enter the base URL of your WooCommerce store.
- Enter your Consumer Key and Consumer Secret . A new REST API key can be created in WooCommerce by going to WooCommerce → Settings → Advanced → REST API, clicking Add key, selecting Read/Write permissions, and generating the key.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Feb-11-2026-09-35-58-5006-PM.png?width=670&height=365&name=undefined-Feb-11-2026-09-35-58-5006-PM.png)

- Click Next.

**(3) Order Creation**

- Here you will need to assign a CartonCloud warehouse for where your WooCommerce orders will go to.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-4.png?width=670&height=363&name=undefined-4.png)

- Click Next.

**(3) Fulfillment**

- Complete Fulfilment through CartonCloud: when enabled WooCommerce Orders will be marked as complete when the Sale Order is dispatched in CartonCloud.

- Tracking Information: Tracking information will be sent to WooCommerce when the order is packed or dispatched, and will be updated when tracking details change. To enable this functionality, the WooCommerce Shipment Tracking plugin must be installed and activated in your WooCommerce store. Note: The Shipment Tracking plugin is not required for CartonCloud to complete orders in WooCommerce.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Feb-11-2026-09-35-58-8906-PM.png?width=670&height=366&name=undefined-Feb-11-2026-09-35-58-8906-PM.png)

- Click Finish.

### Disconnecting an existing Self-Managed WooCommerce Integration

If you need to cancel and disconnect the integration you will need to:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click WooCommerce .
- Select the three-dot configuration icon and select Delete Integration.
- This will remove the integration and stop the billing of the integration to your account.

### Editing an existing Self-Managed WooCommerce Integration

To edit an existing Self-Managed WooCommerce Integration:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer .
- Click WooCommerce .
- Select Reconfigure .

### Managing Self-Managed Integrations

Because Self-Managed Integrations are a paid feature, it is important you are able to manage and keep track of the number of active integrations your customers have. This is useful if you wish to pass on the cost to your customer and reconcile your invoices.

If a Customer has a live integration they will have a green dot icon against their name. It will also display the number of active integrations for that customer below their name.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/undefined-Feb-11-2026-09-35-59-2623-PM.png?width=670&height=145&name=undefined-Feb-11-2026-09-35-59-2623-PM.png)

<a id="self-managed-xero-integration"></a>
## Self-Managed Xero Integration

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/self-managed-xero-integration_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Prerequisites
- Cost
- Available workflow
- How to create a Self-Managed Xero Integration
- Examples
- Testing
- Disconnecting a Self-Managed Xero Integration
- Disabling a Self-Managed Xero Integration
- Editing a Self-Managed Xero Integration
- Managing Self-Managed Integrations
- Troubleshooting Steps

### Overview

Self-Managed Integrations allow you to create integrations from within your own CartonCloud account. Within the Self-Managed Integrations, you can choose the platform you wish to integrate with. One such platform is Xero.

With the Self-Managed Xero Integration, a Xero Invoice can create a Sale Order in CartonCloud and the Xero invoice will attach to the Sale Order in CartonCloud. This allows your customers to set up a seamless workflow between their Xero account and CartonCloud. You can choose what invoice status triggers the order to be created in CartonCloud and how the order is mapped to the CartonCloud warehouse.

You can configure the integration yourself or you can have your customer set the integration up from their CartonCloud login. This allows for greater security as your customer doesn’t have to share their Xero login details with you. Please note, that you must first enable the Customer to create their own Self-Managed Integrations from the Organisation and/or Customer Settings. Please see [How to enable Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/How-to-enable-Customers-to-create-their-own-Self-Managed-Integrations) for more information.

### Prerequisites

- This is a paid integration; please ensure you read the included costs below.
- Your customer must have an Xero account
- If you are a Customer user, ensure your CartonCloud account owner has given you permission in your account to create your own Self-Managed Integrations. Please reach out to your account owner for this access.
- You will need your customer’s Xero login credentials. If your customer does not wish to share these details with you, you can have the customer create the integration themselves (see How to enable Customers to create their own Self-Managed Integrations for more information).
- Product codes in Xero must match the product codes in CartonCloud
- The Customer in CartonCloud must have access to the Warehouse the orders are being mapped to from Xero

![self-managed-xero-integration-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-0.png?width=670&height=224&name=self-managed-xero-integration-0.png)

- The delivery address in Xero must be a valid address (e.g includes postcode, state, street name and number etc.)

### Cost

We offer volume-based discounts—reach out to our support team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/contactsupport) to discuss pricing options.

### Available Workflow

- Xero Invoice creates a Sale Order in CartonCloud
- The Xero Invoice PDF will be attached to the Sale Order in CartonCloud

### How to create a Self-Managed Xero Integration

- Navigate to the Integrations page by typing in Integrations in the Search for Anything bar or More > Self-Managed Integrations .
- If an Admin user, select the customer you wish to create the integration for.
- Click Xero from the Self-Managed Integrations menu selection.

![self-managed-xero-integration-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-1.png?width=670&height=259&name=self-managed-xero-integration-1.png)

- Click Configure .

![self-managed-xero-integration-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-2.png?width=670&height=318&name=self-managed-xero-integration-2.png)

- The configuration box will now appear, follow the below steps to configure the integration.
  - **(1) Initial Configuration**
    - Fill in the Name field. Ensure the name includes the name of the customer. If you are creating a Xero integration for multiple customers you will need to be able to easily identify the different integrations.
    - Click Next .

![self-managed-xero-integration-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-3.png?width=670&height=308&name=self-managed-xero-integration-3.png)

- **(2) Authentication**
  - You will now need to connect CartonCloud to the correct Xero account. You will require your customer's Xero login credentials for this step.
  - Click Connect against the Xero tile. Enter the Xero login credentials and click Login . Once the status dot icon has turned green the connection has been successful.

![self-managed-xero-integration-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-4.png?width=670&height=299&name=self-managed-xero-integration-4.png)

- **(3) Configuration**
  - Select the invoice payment status that will trigger a Sale Order being created in CartonCloud.
    - Awaiting Payment
    - Paid

![self-managed-xero-integration-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-5.png?width=670&height=314&name=self-managed-xero-integration-5.png)

- Select if you wish to include the Invoice Note field from Xero on the Sale Order in CartonCloud. You can choose where you would like to store this information against the Sale Order. Note, that you can only select one field to store the note field information against.
  - None
  - Delivery Instructions
  - Packing Instructions

![self-managed-xero-integration-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-6.png?width=670&height=312&name=self-managed-xero-integration-6.png)

![self-managed-xero-integration-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-7.png?width=670&height=313&name=self-managed-xero-integration-7.png)

- You will now need to map which Xero orders will go to which CartonCloud warehouse. The below describes the different options you have to map the Xero orders to CartonCloud.
- Default Warehouse: if you choose to set a default warehouse all orders will go to this warehouse unless you add reference mapping and the order matches this reference mapping. You can also choose to ignore the default warehouse and only apply the reference mapping. This means only orders with specific references specified in the mapping will come across to CartonCloud.

![self-managed-xero-integration-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-8.png?width=670&height=313&name=self-managed-xero-integration-8.png)

- Reference mapping: you can add particular reference mapping to determine what orders will come across to CartonCloud and what warehouse they will go to. You will need to specify the reference and then the warehouse it must go to. You can then order the reference mappings in order of priority using the arrows next to the mappings.
- Please note that the reference field is ‘Reference Contains’ which means if that reference is contained within another word it will be sent to that warehouse. For example, if you want orders with ‘Drink Bottle Distribution’ in the reference to go to the Sunshine Coast warehouse and orders with ‘Drink Bottle Distributions - GC’ to go to the Gold Coast warehouse then you will need to put the Gold Coast reference mapping first. This will prevent all orders with ‘Drink Bottle Distribution’ from going to the Sunshine Coast warehouse. This set-up is shown below:

![self-managed-xero-integration-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-9.png?width=670&height=376&name=self-managed-xero-integration-9.png)

- Click Finish .

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/0gBUhgE_c_E

### Examples

In the below examples, it is assumed that Drink Bottle Distribution is the CartonCloud account owner and Sunshine Drink Bottles is the customer. These configurations are set up for Sunshine Drink Bottles.

**Example 1**

**Use case:***I sometimes use a Drink Bottle Distribution warehouse for some of my orders, but I deliver most of them myself.*

![self-managed-xero-integration-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-10.png?width=670&height=345&name=self-managed-xero-integration-10.png)

**Example 2**

**Use case:***I mostly use a Drink Bottle Distribution Warehouse for all of my orders, but I use two different warehouses. If I don't put any special wording in the reference, I want the orders to be ignored.*

*![self-managed-xero-integration-11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-11.png?width=670&height=441&name=self-managed-xero-integration-11.png)*

**Example 3**

**Use case:***I always use a Drink Bottle Distribution Warehouse for all of my orders, but I use two different locations of these warehouses. If I don't put any special wording in the reference, I still want the order to be captured so it does not get missed (you will need to choose which warehouse it gets created in).*

*![self-managed-xero-integration-12](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-12.png?width=670&height=451&name=self-managed-xero-integration-12.png)*

**Example 4**

***Use case:** I do not use a special reference because all my orders go to one Drink Bottle Distribution Warehouse*

*![self-managed-xero-integration-13](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-13.png?width=670&height=409&name=self-managed-xero-integration-13.png)*

**Example 5**

**Use case:***I mostly only use a single Drink Bottle Distribution warehouse, but sometimes I have one or two orders I do not want them to fulfil*

*![self-managed-xero-integration-14](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-14.png?width=670&height=418&name=self-managed-xero-integration-14.png)*

### Testing

Once you have created the Self-Managed Xero Integration it is suggested that you test the integration with a test order. Place an order in Xero with the reference you have specified and the payment status. Once you have done this the Sale Order will be created in CartonCloud.

If you have any questions or issues please contact support via [CartonCoud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

### Disconnecting a Self-Managed Xero Integration

If you need to cancel and disconnect the integration you will need to:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click Xero Orders .
- Scroll down to Instances.
- Select the three-dot configuration icon and select Delete Integration.
- This will remove the integration and stop the billing of the integration to your account.

![self-managed-xero-integration-15](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-15.png?width=519&height=258&name=self-managed-xero-integration-15.png)

### Disabling a Self-Managed Xero Integration

The integration can be temporarily disabled without being deleted. This allows you to pause the integration with Xero orders while retaining all configuration settings. You can then later re-enable the integration without needing to reconfigre or reconnect the Xero account.

This is useful for troubleshooting, testing or business downtime without losing setup.

To disable the integration:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click Xero Orders .
- Click Reconfigure .
- Click Next.
- Toggle ' Enable Integration ' off.

![self-managed-xero-integration-16](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-16.png?width=670&height=248&name=self-managed-xero-integration-16.png)

### Editing an existing Self-Managed Xero Integration

To edit an existing Self-Managed Xero Integration:

- Navigate to the Integrations page.
- Select the relevant Customer .
- Click Xero Orders .
- Scroll down to Instances.
- Select Reconfigure .

![self-managed-xero-integration-17](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-17.png?width=384&height=376&name=self-managed-xero-integration-17.png)

### Managing Self-Managed Integrations

Because Self-Managed Integrations are a paid feature, it is important you are able to manage and keep track of the number of active integrations your customer's have. This is useful if you wish to pass on the cost to your customer and reconcile your invoices.

If a Customer has a live integration they will have a green dot icon against their name. It will also display the number of active integrations for that customer below their name.

![self-managed-xero-integration-18](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/self-managed-xero-integration-18.png?width=670&height=280&name=self-managed-xero-integration-18.png)

### Troubleshooting Steps

If you are experiencing issues with your Self-Managed Integration and orders are not coming through to CartonCloud please complete the following checks:

- Check the Paring Log for why the orders are failing. See Parsing Log for information on how to read the Parsing Log and diagnose the issue.
- Check that the reference text exactly matches what you have setup in Step 3 of the connection.
- If you are still not able to resolve the issue please reach out to the Service Desk team with screenshots here  - CartonCoud Help.

---
